# Transport Management

<a id="containers"></a>
## Containers

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/containers_

### Table of Contents

- What is a Container?
- Container Custom Fields
- How to create a Container?

### What is a Container?

A container in CartonCloud is a container that is being received into your warehouse.

### Container Custom Fields

Before creating a Container it is suggested you create the required Custom Fields. Custom Fields allow you to record custom information against the Container. Two custom fields that you should create are Container Arrival Date and Container Departure Date. For steps on how to create a Custom Field click here -

Introduction to Custom Field

.

### How to create a Container?

- Type Containers into the Search for anything bar.
- Click +Add .

![containers-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/containers-0.png?width=670&height=362&name=containers-0.png)

- Enter the Container Arrival Date, Container Departure Date and related Shipment reference (if the shipment has been created/if you have a related shipment).

![containers-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/containers-1.png?width=670&height=252&name=containers-1.png)

- Once the Container has been created you can view the container details from the View Container screen. From here, you can update the status.

![containers-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/containers-2.png?width=670&height=160&name=containers-2.png)

- The different statuses the container can move through include: Not yet Received, Received, Unloaded, Pickup Booked, Picked Up.

---

<a id="setting-up-vehicles-in-cartoncloud"></a>
## Setting up Vehicles in CartonCloud

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-vehicles-in-cartoncloud_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to enter Vehicles into CartonCloud

### Purpose

By entering your fleet's vehicles into CartonCloud, you can then track important information relating to those vehicles using Custom Fields (which you would have set up during the Custom Field's article).

CartonCloud also allows you to allocate Run Sheets to Vehicles and therefore track their performance by checking the revenue generated by an individual Vehicle. For example, by using Vehicles within CartonCloud they can then be displayed as a field on [Consignment Reports](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Consignment+Report).

Entering your fleet's vehicles into CartonCloud is entirely optional, however, we do recommend it for the benefits stated above.

### How to enter Vehicles into CartonCloud

To add a vehicle into CartonCloud begin by navigating to the  **Vehicles** page, the easiest way to do this is to type "Vehicles" into the  **Search for Anything** bar, then select when prompted.

![setting-up-vehicles-in-cartoncloud-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-vehicles-in-cartoncloud-0.png?width=670&height=293&name=setting-up-vehicles-in-cartoncloud-0.png)

Here you can see a list of Vehicles we have already set up (including Custom Fields to record their Rego number, minimum height clearance and rego expiry) in our demo tenancy, but your page will be empty for now until we begin entering Vehicles.

Next, click **+Add Vehicle** and you will be presented with a page of fields to fill out. At a minimum, these fields will be the Name of the Vehicle and which Warehouses it operates from. However, using Custom Fields it is also possible to create extra fields that you can then use to capture information against the vehicle. In the example provided you will notice we have created Custom Fields for the Registration Number and if the vehicle has a Tail Lift platform or not plus others. The fields you create is entirely up to your operational requirements and some users may not to utilise these at all.

![setting-up-vehicles-in-cartoncloud-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-vehicles-in-cartoncloud-1.png?width=670&height=503&name=setting-up-vehicles-in-cartoncloud-1.png)
Once you have completed the fields select **Save** and the Vehicle will be created. A **Success!** banner will display on the browser to indicate this.

And that's it! Now when you allocate Consignments you will be able to select the Vehicle the consignment is being allocated to. You will also be able to reference the information entered against the vehicle when delivery with specific requirements arises. For example, a delivery to a parking lot with a height restriction, or to a shop front without a forklift.

For reporting purposes, the "Bulk Export Consignments" report will show which Vehicle was used for a Consignment, making it easy analyse how your fleet is performing.

Next Step: [Setting up CartonCloud to automatically allocate Consignments](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-cartoncloud-to-automatically-allocate-consignments)

---

# Transport Management > Allocations

<a id="allocating-consignments-to-drivers"></a>
## Allocating Consignments to Drivers

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/allocating-consignments-to-drivers_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- What are Run Sheets in CartonCloud
- Important information about allocating

### Purpose

Learning to use CartonCloud to efficiently allocate consignments within your transport operation is an important part of the TMS setup. Becoming comfortable with this area of the system can save operators hours of the day to focus on other tasks.

The articles within this section aim to make you familiar with the options CartonCloud provides for consignment allocation.

### What are Run Sheets in CartonCloud?

When consignments are allocated to drivers CartonCloud will automatically produce a new Run Sheet (unless you allocate to an already existing Run Sheet).

This Run Sheet is a list of the consignments going with a single driver. This means that the deliveries for a day going to the Delivery Run "Gold Coast" might be split up across multiple Run Sheets (East, North, West), as each Run sheet is allocated to a different driver.

To put it briefly, a run sheet is a list of jobs that are going on one driver for that day, and typically they're broken into different areas.

This could also mean for example that a driver could end up with multiple run sheets for a single day. For example, imagine a driver who services hospital deliveries in the morning using the run sheet "Gold Coast Hospital Run" and then services supplier collections in the afternoon, using a different run sheet which might be called "Gold Coast Supplier Collections".

### Important information about allocating

- To allow a driver to see a consignment and get an electronic POD - all that's required is the consignment allocated to that drivers name.
- Drivers are created through the Creating New Users process and must be marked as a Driver to be allocated to and for Mobile App access.
- Physically allocating a consignment to a driver can be done from a number of places. The following videos and articles will cover these and suggest what will work best for you based on your operation.

Next Step: [Checklist before Allocating](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Checklist+before+Allocating)

---

<a id="allocating-from-the-bulk-allocation-screen"></a>
## Allocating from the Bulk Allocation screen

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/allocating-from-the-bulk-allocation-screen_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to allocate in bulk
- Customising the bulk allocation screen

### Purpose

If your operation uses a large number of Delivery Runs, you may find the traditional way of allocating (going into each Delivery Run) time consuming and restrictive. It doesn't provide any way of seeing consignments outside of the current run you're allocating which can mean you miss valuable run combinations (mixing jobs from different runs to maximize efficiency).

Bulk Allocation addresses this by allowing you to simultaneously allocate multiple Delivery Runs by letting you search across all consignments due to go out on a certain day.

### How to allocate in bulk

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/_uk1pdWnUy0

### Customising the Bulk Allocation Screen

**Optionally** the bulk allocation screen can be customised to your liking. Namely, you can:

- Enable/Disable the Map View for Bulk Allocation
- Change the Interface between Simple/Advanced Mode

For details on how to do this, see the article: [Customising the Bulk Allocation Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Customising+the+Bulk+Allocation+Screen)

Next Step: [Optimising the delivery order of Consignments](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Optimising+the+delivery+order+of+Consignments)

---

<a id="automatically-allocate-consignments-to-drivers-from-delivery-runs"></a>
## Automatically allocate Consignments to Drivers from Delivery Runs

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/automatically-allocate-consignments-to-drivers-from-delivery-runs_

### How to steps

In order to automatically allocate consignments to drivers

- Select Contacts > Users .
- Select the User you wish to edit.
- Select Edit Delivery Runs at the bottom of the page.
- Tick the Delivery Runs you wish to link to the Driver.

![automatically-allocate-consignments-to-drivers-from-delivery-runs-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/automatically-allocate-consignments-to-drivers-from-delivery-runs-0.png?width=670&height=352&name=automatically-allocate-consignments-to-drivers-from-delivery-runs-0.png)

- Scroll down and select Save .

---

<a id="bulk-allocation"></a>
## Bulk Allocation

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/bulk-allocation_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to allocate in bulk
- Customising the bulk allocation screen
- Exporting to route optimisation software
- Bulk allocation for 'undetermined' delivery run

### Purpose

If your operation uses a large number of Delivery Runs, you may find the traditional way of allocating (going into each Delivery Run) time consuming and restrictive. It doesn't provide any way of seeing consignments outside of the current run you're allocating which can mean you miss valuable run combinations (mixing jobs from different runs to maximize efficiency).

Bulk Allocation addresses this by allowing you to simultaneously allocate multiple Delivery Runs by letting you search across all consignments due to go out on a certain day.

### How to allocate in Bulk

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/_uk1pdWnUy0

### Customising the Bulk Allocation Screen

Optionally the bulk allocation screen can be customised to your liking. Namely, you are able to:

- Enable/Disable the Map View for Bulk Allocation
- Change the Interface between Simple/Advanced Mode

For details on how to do this, see the article: [Customising the Bulk Allocation Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Customising+the+Bulk+Allocation+Screen)

### Exporting to Route Optimisation Software

From the bulk allocation page, it is possible to export data to then be imported into another software (such as a route optimisation software), or import data from another software into CartonCloud.

This is ideal for operations that use CartonCloud as their Transport Management System but use another software for route optimisation.

For more information on how this functionality works please click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/XAI3I) and to set this functionality up in your own CartonCloud account please contact our [Integrations team](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket).

### Bulk Allocation for 'Undetermined' Delivery Run

For Consignments that are not yet allocated to a Delivery Run, you can use the 'Undetermined' Delivery Run on the Bulk Allocation screen to allocate them to the appropriate run. The 'Unallocated' Delivery Run helps to ensure no Consignments are missed and that all are allocated accordingly. If you are in the process of setting up your Transport Lanes, you can also use the 'Undetermined' Delivery Run to ensure all different zone combinations are covered.

To use the 'Undetermined' Delivery Run on the Bulk Allocation screen:

- From the Bulk Allocation screen, tick the select box next to the Delivery Run name **UNDETERMINED**.

![bulk-allocation-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bulk-allocation-0.png?width=670&height=304&name=bulk-allocation-0.png)

- You will then see all Consignments that do not have a Delivery Run.
- From here, you can then select the Consignments you wish to update the Delivery Run for by using the select box next to the Consignment then clicking the Update Delivery Run blue button at the bottom of the screen.
- Select the Delivery Run you wish to add the Consignments to and then click **Update**.

---

<a id="checklist-before-allocating"></a>
## Checklist before allocating

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/checklist-before-allocating_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Checklist

### Purpose

There are a few things which should be checked each day before allocations are started. This process is designed to prevent consignments from being missed in the allocation stages.

### Checklist

Check the Dashboard

Each of the below is shown in the notifications area of the Dashboard. You can also tailor the notifications to suit your personal preferences. For instance, if you don't need to see 'Draft Invoices', turn off that notification by clicking the gear icon and then making changes.

**Clean up the previous day's jobs**

Ideally, this can be monitored throughout the day to detect where issues may be occurring:

1. Check what Run sheets remain incomplete by selecting Transport in the main menu, followed by Run sheets in the drop-down menu. Then select the **Today's Incomplete** tab.
2. If the driver finished the run, find out why the jobs were not marked delivered and either mark them as delivered or if they're to be reattempted reallocate the consignments to another day. If you want to charge the customer for a second delivery, then you need to duplicate the consignment and mark the original one delivered.

**Pre-allocation steps**
Perform these in order to prevent double-handling

1. Allocate all **Unallocated Address Strings**
2. (If enabled in your settings) Approve all **Addresses Awaiting Approval**
3. Geocode all **Addresses Requiring Geocoding**
4. Allocate all **Unallocated Consignments** (if any remain after allocating Address Strings)
5. Update **Manifests** to **In Warehouse**
6. **Check 'Error / Unallocated' Runs** to make sure no consignments ended up on those. For instance, all suburbs and postcodes you don't service will likely be connected to an 'Unallocated' run - so this run needs to be checked daily, and all jobs on the run moved to the appropriate run (and also check why the Address allocated to that run in the first place - so next time it'll allocate correctly).

Once these steps are complete you will be ready to allocate.

Next Step: [Which way should I allocate my Consignments?](https://help.cartoncloud.com/pages/viewpage.action?pageId=530055420)

---

<a id="customising-the-bulk-allocation-screen"></a>
## Customising the Bulk Allocation Screen

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/customising-the-bulk-allocation-screen_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to enable/disable the map view
- Map view controls
- Changing bulk allocation interface between simple and advanced

### Purpose

You can configure specific controls and settings to customise the bulk allocation screen to best suit your operational needs.

When customising the bulk allocation screen, you can:

- Enable/disable the Map View.
- Utilise specific controls when using the Map View interface.
- Change the map view interface between Simple and Advanced Mode.

### How to enable/disable the map view

- Navigate to Organisation Settings, More > Organisation Settings .
- Select the Features & Options tab.

![customising-the-bulk-allocation-screen-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customising-the-bulk-allocation-screen-0.png?width=670&height=276&name=customising-the-bulk-allocation-screen-0.png)

- Scroll down to the Bulk Allocation Configuration window.
- Under Shows the map on the Bulk Allocation screen, tick the Bulk Allocation Map Enabled box.
- Scroll down and select Save .
- If you navigate to the Bulk Allocation screen, you will see the Map View at the bottom of the page.

### Map View Controls

You will need to have Consignments selected to use the Map View Controls. Click

here

for steps on selecting Consignments on the Bulk Allocation screen.

From the Bulk Allocations screen with the Map View enabled, the below controls are available:

**Move the map**

**Controls**: Click & Hold Left Mouse Button + Move Mouse

**Action:** Allows the user to move the map to select and view different Consignments.

**Select a single Consignment**

**Controls:** Click left on the red dot.

**Action:** Shows an information popup and selects the corresponding consignment in the action tables above the map.

**Selecting multiple Consignments**

**Controls:**CTRL + Left Click on Red Dot

**Action:**Once you have selected one Consignment, you can select other Consignments all at once by holding CTRL. Both Consignments will turn green to indicate they have been selected.

**Drag to select multiple Consignments**

**Controls:** CTRL + SHIFT + Click & Hold Left Mouse Button + Move Mouse

**Action:** Drawing a box across an area will result in any Consignments within that boxes' boundaries being selected.

Suppose a Selection Box has been drawn on the map, but you wish to adjust the map view to see a new location to extend the existing Selection Box to the location or make additional manual selections. In that case, You will need to hold down the CTRL key while moving the mouse.

NOTE: If you Click & Hold Left Mouse Button without pressing the CTRL Key, any previous selections will be lost.

### Changing Bulk Allocation Interface Between Simple and Advanced

**Simple interface**

Has one table responsible for selection and action.

**Advanced interface**

It has two tables, one for selection and the other for action.

**To change the interface:**

- Navigate to Organisation Settings, **More**>**Organisation Settings**.
- Select **Features & Options**.
- Scroll down to Bulk Allocation Configuration.
- Tick the Bulk Allocation Simple Interface option if you wish to use the simple interface. If you want to use the advanced interface, leave the option unticked.

---

<a id="fix-the-delivery-run-allocation-for-a-consignment"></a>
## Fix the Delivery Run Allocation for a Consignment

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/fix-the-delivery-run-allocation-for-a-consignment_

If you find that Consignments are being allocated to the wrong Delivery Runs, it is a simple process to determine how and why the Consignment is being allocated the way it is, follow this guide to work through the steps to correct CartonCloud so in future the consignments will allocate correctly, automatically.

![fix-the-delivery-run-allocation-for-a-consignment-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/fix-the-delivery-run-allocation-for-a-consignment-0.png?width=273&height=476&name=fix-the-delivery-run-allocation-for-a-consignment-0.png)

<a id="job-allocation"></a>
## Job Allocation

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/job-allocation_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to allocate a job
  - Job allocation view
  - Allocation modes
  - Allocate a job by manual entry
  - Allocate a job by barcode scanning
- Job allocation status
  - Uploading
  - Successful
  - Failed
  - Failed with multiple matches
- Troubleshooting
  - iOS app
  - Android app

### Purpose

The Job Allocation View allows users to allocate jobs from their mobile devices, either by entering a barcode using a connected Bluetooth barcode scanner or through the manual entry option.

The video below demonstrates how this works.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/HA4ctUZTSqw

Please note that the Job Allocation functionality is only available to mobile app users that have been assigned a "Driver" role through the CartonCloud web app. Users who are solely "Pickers" will not see the Job Allocation menu option in the main menu, as described below.

For more information on User Modes please check out this article: [User Modes](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/User+Modes)

### How to allocate a job

#### **Job Allocation View**

The Job Allocation View can be reached by opening the slide-in menu through selecting the menu button in the top left of the main view and then choosing "Allocate Jobs".

![job-allocation-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/job-allocation-0.png?width=307&height=546&name=job-allocation-0.png)

#### **Allocation Modes**

There are three allocation modes available in the Job Allocation view: "**Allocate**", "**Unallocate**" and "**Mark as in Warehouse**". The current mode is displayed on top of the view and can be changed by tapping on the mode label and choosing a mode from the mode picker.

![job-allocation-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/job-allocation-1.png?width=485&height=434&name=job-allocation-1.png)

#### **Allocate a job by manual entry**

To allocate a job by manual entry, choose the plus ( **+** ) sign next to the allocation mode label. An alert window will be displayed, allowing you to enter a barcode manually. Once you have selected "Add Barcode", the job allocation will be displayed in the job allocation list.

![job-allocation-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/job-allocation-2.png?width=503&height=432&name=job-allocation-2.png)
**Allocate a job by barcode scanning**

To be able to allocate jobs by scanning a barcode, ensure a Bluetooth scanner is connected to your mobile device. Once this is all set up, simply navigate to the Job Allocation View & start scanning. Job allocations will immediately be displayed in the job allocation list after scanning.
For more information on how to connect a Bluetooth barcode scanner to your mobile device please check out this article: [Connect a Bluetooth Barcode Scanner](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Connect+a+Bluetooth+Barcode+Scanner)

![job-allocation-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/job-allocation-3.png?width=283&height=506&name=job-allocation-3.png)

### Job Allocation Status

After adding a job allocation, there are several statuses the allocation can be in.

#### **Uploading**

This is the initial state for any allocation, as the information is being transferred to the CartonCloud server. Allocations in this state will not be deleted from the list until you leave the Job Allocation View. The only bit of information being displayed while uploading is the entered barcode.

#### **Successful**

#### After a successful allocation, the corresponding entry in the job allocation list will be adjusted accordingly, showing more information about the allocated consignment and the server response.

![job-allocation-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/job-allocation-4.png?width=308&height=549&name=job-allocation-4.png)

 A successful status will also be displayed if no changes were made on the server due to the consignment already being in the desired state. In this case, a warning will be displayed in orange in place of  the "success" server response, informing the user about the fact that no changes were made on the server.

![job-allocation-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/job-allocation-5.png?width=311&height=556&name=job-allocation-5.png)
**Failed**

After a failed allocation, the corresponding entry in the job allocation list will be adjusted accordingly, showing details about the issue that was encountered when trying to allocate the job on the server.

#### **Failed with Multiple Matches**

A possible failure can be encountered if multiple matches are found for an entered barcode, e.g. if the entered barcode is "123" and there exists one consignment with Id "0123" and another one with Id "1123". If this is the case, the list entry will be updated to be shown as a failure, giving the user the option to choose which one of the consignments they want to continue the allocation with. On selecting the desired consignment, the app will automatically remove the failed allocation and replace it with a new allocation linked to the selected consignment.

![job-allocation-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/job-allocation-6.png?width=670&height=406&name=job-allocation-6.png)
![job-allocation-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/job-allocation-7.png?width=277&height=492&name=job-allocation-7.png)
**Notes**

- On the **iOS** app, the job allocation list will reset to an empty list every time you leave the Job Allocation View. On the **Android** app, the list will be cleared when you enter the Job Allocation View.
- Only 5 items are being kept in the allocation list at any time, meaning "old" items will be dropped as new allocations are added. Notable exceptions are allocations that are still in "uploading" status, and those that find multiple matches. These will be kept in the list until the upload is resolved or the consignment is chosen.
- A short delay of 0.2 sec is enabled between barcode reads when using a barcode scanner. Please be aware that scanning barcodes any faster than this may cause barcodes to be read incorrectly.
- ​​​​​​​Internet connection is required for any allocation to take place successfully.

### ​​​​​​​Troubleshooting

#### **iOS app**

- **No keyboard displaying when in manual entry alert**:
  - On your bluetooth barcode scanner: Ensure HID features for Apple iOS are enabled. Double-pressing the trigger button on your scanner may be required to bring up the iPhone keyboard for manual entry if you do not want to disconnect/reconnect your bluetooth scanner every time manual entry is required. HID features can normally be enabled/disabled by scanning the corresponding barcode in your bluetooth barcode scanner's manual.
- **Scanned barcode does not appear**: Ensure your bluetooth barcode scanner is connected to your iOS device. Alternatively, try manual entry.

#### **Android app**

- **No keyboard displaying when in manual entry alert**: This normally happens when your device favours a hardware input method, e.g. barcode scanner, over soft keyboard.
  - Normally a click on the input field will bring up the keyboard. If not, try to double click or long click on the input field. The keyboard may come up or a notification will pop up on the top of the screen, prompting you to “Select keyboard input” or “Choose input method”. Click on that: disable the hardware input method or choose the soft keyboard one.
  - After clicking on the input field, check whether a keyboard symbol shows up in the bottom menu area. Click on that and choose the right keyboard.
  - An alternative is to temporarily disable the barcode scanner and then click on the input field. Some barcode scanners allow to be temporarily disabled with simple steps.
  - If nothing works, unpair the scanner to remove this hardware input method.
- **Scanned barcode does not appear**: Ensure your bluetooth barcode scanner is connected to your mobile device. Alternatively, try manual entry.

---

<a id="product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings"></a>
## Product Update: Bulk Allocation Configuration settings

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings_

### Table of Contents

- Overview
- Navigating to the setting
- Current behaviour
- New behaviour

### Overview

If you are using Bulk Allocation, there are a number of Bulk Allocation Configuration Settings you can utilise to customise your Bulk Allocation workflow. One setting includes **Override Consignment Delivery Run** defaulted to yes. With this setting selected, the 'Override Consignment Delivery Run' option will be ticked by default on certain allocation screens within CartonCloud, however, you can still unselect the 'Override Consignments Delivery Run' option on an individual screen level

### Navigating to the setting

- Navigate to **Organisation Settings**, **More**>**Organisation Settings**.
- Select the **Features & Options** tab and scroll down to **Bulk Allocation Configuration**.

![product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings-0.png?width=670&height=128&name=product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings-0.png)

### Current Behaviour

With the**'Default 'Override Consignments Delivery Run' checkbox to checked on Bulk Allocation and Move Consignments Screens'** selected:

- 'Override Consignments Delivery Run' will be checked by default on the Bulk Allocation and Move Consignments Screen
- You can choose to unselect the 'Override Consignments Delivery Run' option on the individual screen when performing the allocation

**Bulk Allocation Screen**

![product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings-1.png?width=670&height=361&name=product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings-1.png)

 **Move Consignment Screen**

![product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings-2.png?width=670&height=214&name=product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings-2.png)

### New Behaviour

As a part of an upcoming release, we will be updating this setting so that you can ensure the **'Override Consignments Delivery Run'**checkboxis ticked by default on the Bulk Allocation screen, the Move Consignments screen, ***and*the Edit Run Sheet screen.**

With the**'Default "Override Consignments' Delivery Run" to checked** selected:

- 'Override Consignments Delivery Run' will be checked by default on the Bulk Allocation, Move Consignments and Edit Run Sheet screen
- You can choose to unselect the 'Override Consignments Delivery Run' option on the individual screen when performing the allocation

**Bulk Allocation Screen**

![product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings-3.png?width=670&height=361&name=product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings-3.png)

**Move Consignment Screen**
 ![product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings-4.png?width=670&height=214&name=product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings-4.png)

**Edit Run Sheet Screen**
 ![product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings-5.png?width=670&height=269&name=product-update-bulk-allocation-configuration-settings-5.png)

Note that if you have this setting ticked in your Organisation Settings, it will stay ticked with the new release, and will now cause the Edit Run Sheet screen to default to checked too.

<a id="setting-up-cartoncloud-to-automatically-allocate-consignments"></a>
## Setting up CartonCloud to automatically allocate Consignments

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-cartoncloud-to-automatically-allocate-consignments_

Please note that if your CartonCloud account was created prior to 1 July 2019 the below functionality may not be available at this stage. If you would like to discuss migrating to the newer version of the CartonCloud TMS, please use [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com) and lodge a case with our Service Desk.

CartonCloud has the ability to automatically assign a new consignment to the appropriate Delivery Run. For this functionality to work, you must set up your [Delivery Runs](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/nQGYHw), [Transport Zone Sets](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/wILcI), and [Transport Lanes](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/ZoPcI).

Follow the below steps to enable CartonCloud to automatically assign your consignments.

1. Create Delivery Runs
2. Set up Transport Zone Set
3. Create Transport Lanes

The below diagram helps to explain how CartonCloud uses Delivery Runs, Transport Zone Sets, and Transport Lanes to automatically assign a consignment to a Delivery Run.

Note, Sale Orders will also follow the same Zone Sets and Transport Lanes logic when determining the expected Delivery Run (unless a default Delivery Run has been set up in the [Warehouse Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/add-edit-warehouse)). The Warehouse address of the Sale Order will be utilised as the collect address and the conditions in the Transport Lane that are related to Consignments will not be included in the logic when determining the Sale Order Delivery Run.

![setting-up-cartoncloud-to-automatically-allocate-consignments-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-cartoncloud-to-automatically-allocate-consignments-0.png?width=389&height=441&name=setting-up-cartoncloud-to-automatically-allocate-consignments-0.png)

**Delivery Runs:**How you divide your consignments into manageable quantities for delivery.

**Transport Zone Sets:** These are the zones your operation uses for assigning consignments.

Please note, that the Transport Zone matched to the Consignment will depend upon the criteria below.

For example, for an address in New Zealand, both the Suburb AND Postcode on the Consignment's address must match to find the correct Transport Zone.

| **Location Entries Type** | **Country** | **Matching Criteria** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Australia Locations | Australia | State AND Suburb AND Postcode |
| Global Locations | New Zealand | Suburb AND Postcode |
| Global Locations | All other countries | Suburb OR Postcode |

Please see [Zone Set Matching Criteria](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Zone-set-matching-criteria) for more information.

**Transport Lanes:** Provides the logic for CartonCloud to know what Delivery Run a consignment needs to be assigned to.

First step: [Setting up Delivery Runs](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/delivery-runs)

---

<a id="which-way-should-i-allocate-my-consignments"></a>
## Which way should I allocate my Consignments?

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/which-way-should-i-allocate-my-consignments_

Within CartonCloud there are multiple ways in which you can allocate Consignments. Which way you allocate will likely depend on the quantity of deliveries your operation performs each day, as well as other factors.

In the video below our Onboarder discusses the different ways you can choose to allocate within CartonCloud.

No matter which way you allocate, the result of the consignment being allocated to a driver's mobile will still be the same, however, the workflow you choose can heavily affect your operation's productivity.

If you are unsure on which is best for you, feel free to try out the different allocation methods shown in the video. If you are still unsure, please reach out to your onboarder or support and we can suggest a workflow for your operation.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/e7EKs8d8x0s

Optional Next Step: [Allocating from the Bulk Allocations Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Allocating+from+the+Bulk+Allocations+screen)

If your operation has a large volume of deliveries each day see this step for further instructions on how to allocate in bulk.

Next Step:[Optimising the order of deliveries](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Optimising+the+delivery+order+of+Consignments)

# Transport Management > Carriers

<a id="carriers"></a>
## Carriers

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/carriers_

### Table of Contents

- What is a carrier
- How to create a carrier
- How to enable multiple carriers

### What is a carrier

A Carrier in CartonCloud is used for operational purposes. A Carrier is a Transport Carrier (delivery, trucking or freight company) who delivers your transport jobs (Consignments).

When multi-carrier functionality is enabled, you will need to assign a Carrier to each Delivery Run. See [Enabling Multiple Carriers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-service-types) for more information.

### How to create a carrier

- Navigate to the Carriers page, by typing in Carriers into the Search for anything bar.
- Select the green + Add Carrier

![carriers-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/carriers-0.png?width=670&height=108&name=carriers-0.png)

- Enter the name of the Carrier in the Name field.
- Select Save .

### How to enable multiple carriers

- Navigate to Organisation Settings, by typing Organisation Settings into the Search for anything bar.
- Select the Features & Options tab.

![carriers-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/carriers-1.png?width=670&height=153&name=carriers-1.png)

- Scroll down to the Carrier Configuration heading.
- Tick Multi Carrier Enabled .
- Click Save .

<a id="linking-drivers-carriers"></a>
## Linking Drivers, Carriers and Warehouses to Suppliers

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/linking-drivers-carriers_

### How to Link Drivers, Carriers and Warehouses to Suppliers

Please note that if your CartonCloud account was created post 1 July 2019, you will only be able to link a Warehouse to a Supplier. You will NOT be able to link Drivers and/or Carriers. If you have any questions please use [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com) and lodge a case with our Service Desk.

To link a Driver or Carrier or Warehouse to a Supplier begin by searching for Suppliers in Search for anything.

From the Suppliers page, select the Supplier you wish to link. In the example below, we've chosen a Driver who is set up as a supplier.

Now within the Supplier select **Edit**.

![linking-drivers-carriers-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/linking-drivers-carriers-0.png?width=539&height=362&name=linking-drivers-carriers-0.png)

This will go to the Edit screen for that Supplier. Navigate to **Linked To** tab.

This tab will allow the adding of Drivers, Carriers or Warehouses.
![linking-drivers-carriers-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/linking-drivers-carriers-1.png?width=562&height=409&name=linking-drivers-carriers-1.png)

 **To link a new Driver/Carrier/Warehouse to the Supplier:**

1. Select which Supplier Type to add (Driver or Carrier or Warehouse)
2. Choose the Driver/Carrier/Warehouse to link to the Supplier from the second dropdown
3. Click Link

In the example provided we are linking our Supplier John Smith to the Driver John Smith.

![linking-drivers-carriers-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/linking-drivers-carriers-2.png?width=670&height=191&name=linking-drivers-carriers-2.png)

Linked Drivers/Carriers/Warehouses can be unlinked by deleting them from the table of Linked Drivers/Carriers/Warehouses.

1. To delete Linked Drivers/Carriers/Warehouses:
2. Check the box of the Driver/Carrier/Warehouse to delete. This will highlight the selected row.
3. Click the Delete button. Then click OK in the confirmation message that appears after clicking delete

![linking-drivers-carriers-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/linking-drivers-carriers-3.png?width=670&height=143&name=linking-drivers-carriers-3.png)

<a id="making"></a>
## Making Carriers visible to Customers and giving them aliases

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/making_

- To adjust the Carriers visible to Customers begin by navigating to a Customer's record by selecting Contacts , then selecting Customers from the drop-down menu.
- On the View Customer page select Edit . Then select the Transport Management tab, followed by the Carriers tab.
- From this page, a complete list of the Carriers within your tenancy is displayed.
- Selecting these Carriers as Visible to Customer will then do exactly that.
- The Visible Name field allows you to provide an alias name for the Carrier which the Customer will see in their view of CartonCloud. If the visible name field is left empty the true carrier name will be displayed to the customer.
- Ensure to scroll to the bottom of the page select Save after making any changes within this tab.

![making-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/making-0.png?width=670&height=255&name=making-0.png)

# Transport Management > Consignments

<a id="add-consignment"></a>
## Add Consignment

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/add-consignment_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to add a Consignment manually

### Purpose

To manually add a Consignment to CartonCloud.

### How to add a Consignment manually

- Navigate to the Consignments page, Transport > Consignments .
- Click the green +Add button.

![add-consignment-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-consignment-0.png?width=670&height=132&name=add-consignment-0.png)

- Select the Customer from the drop-down menu.

If you wish to charge a different Customer, tick the Charge to a different customer box and select the Customer you want to charge the job to.

- Enter the Customer Reference. This is how you will identify the Consignment.
- The Custom Fields you have set up for Consignments will appear here. Fill in the appropriate fields. Click here for more information on setting up Custom Fields.

![add-consignment-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-consignment-1.png?width=670&height=212&name=add-consignment-1.png)

- Select if the Consignment requires to be picked up or not. Next, search for the pickup address and select the correct address. If the address is not listed, select +Add New Pickup Address .
- Search for and select the Delivery Address. If the address is not listed, select +Add New Delivery Address .

![add-consignment-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-consignment-2.png?width=670&height=199&name=add-consignment-2.png)

- Enter the Invoice Value if required.
- Select if you wish to add the Consignment to an existing Manifest, create a new Manifest or have no Manifest.

![add-consignment-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-consignment-3.png?width=670&height=233&name=add-consignment-3.png)

- Select the Advanced Options drop-down arrow.
- Select the Consignment Type from the drop-down menu. See Consignment Types for more information.

- If an Onforwarder is being used, search and select the Onforwarder Address . If the address is not listed, click Add New Onforwarder Address .
- The Delivery Run will automatically be determined ; however, you can select a Delivery Run from the drop-down menu if you wish to override this.
- Select a Delivery Date .
- Select a Product Type . Click here for more information on Product Types.

- The Income From and To Rate Zone will be automatically determined; however, you can select a Rate Zone from the drop-down menus if you wish to override this.
- Enter Special Instructions if required.
- Click +Add Consignment Items .
- Enter the Consignment Items by selecting the item from the code drop-down menu.
- Enter the quantity.
- Select Save .
- Select the blue plus icon if you wish to add another Consignment Item.

- Select the Details tab, and you will see all relevant information for the Consignment.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/BD201mXwuhw

---

<a id="add-consignments-to-a-bill"></a>
## Add Consignments to a Bill

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/add-consignments-to-a-bill_

### How to steps

- To add consignments to a bill, first navigate to the Bill you wish to add to by selecting More , then selecting Bills in the drop-down menu.
- Next, click on the Consignments tab at the top of the page. Then click Add Consignments button.
- The next page will display all the consignments related to the Supplier of the bill that are not billed. Options are provided to filter the consignments based on:
- Reference (Consignment Reference): Filter based on consignment reference. Enter each reference in separate lines.
- Delivery Runs Date: Select the From and To date to filter consignments based on delivery run dates.
- From the list of displayed consignments select Consignments that are to be added to the Bill and click on Add Selected Consignments button.

![add-consignments-to-a-bill-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/add-consignments-to-a-bill-0.png?width=581&height=321&name=add-consignments-to-a-bill-0.png)

- The consignments will now be added to the bill.

<a id="adding-a-comment-to-a-consignment"></a>
## Adding a comment to a Consignment

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/adding-a-comment-to-a-consignment_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits
- How to add a comment to a consignment on the web app
- How to add a comment to a consignment on the mobile app

### Purpose

To add a comment to a Consignment either from the web or mobile app for other users (not including customers) to see.

### Benefits

- Easily communicate between the driver and admin users. Comments that are made by either the driver or admin user will show on the mobile app and web app for both users.
- Record important information against the Consignment.

### How to add a comment to a Consignment on the web app

- Navigate to the Consignments page, Transport > Consignments .
- Select the relevant Consignment.
- Select the Comments tab.

![adding-a-comment-to-a-consignment-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-a-comment-to-a-consignment-0.png?width=670&height=341&name=adding-a-comment-to-a-consignment-0.png)

- Click Add comment .
- Type in the comment.
- Click Submit .
- The comment will now appear against the Consignment on the mobile and web app for other users to view (excluding customers).

### How to add a comment to a Consignment on the mobile app

- Select the relevant Consignment
- Click the comment icon against the Consignment.
- Enter the comment.

![adding-a-comment-to-a-consignment-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-a-comment-to-a-consignment-1.png?width=216&height=467&name=adding-a-comment-to-a-consignment-1.png)

- Click Post .
- This comment will now appear against the Consignment on the web and mobile app for all users (excluding customers).

## Approving Consignment Deliveries

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/approving-consignment-deliveries_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to approve the POD

### Purpose

To manually check that the Proof of Delivery scanned or photographed meets requirements. For example, when completing a delivery, Drivers may take a photo that is poor quality or unreadable.

### How to approve the POD

- Navigate to the Documents page, More > Documents .
- Select the Unapproved Consignment Deliveries tab.
- You will see all the Consignments with a POD uploaded against them.
- To approve the image, select the blue Approve button. By clicking Approve , the Consignment delivery status will be updated to Approved.

![approving-consignment-deliveries-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/approving-consignment-deliveries-0.png?width=670&height=169&name=approving-consignment-deliveries-0.png)

<a id="assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods"></a>
## Assigning Documents (Consignment Invoices, Sale Order Invoices & PODs)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to assign documents to the consignment/sale order
  - From the dashboard
  - From the documents page

### Purpose

To assign Consignment Invoices, POD's and Sale Orders to the relevant Consignment/Sale Order in CartonCloud.

Documents can be added to CartonCloud through a variety of sources, such as email, scanned documents or uploaded manually. In some cases, the documents may not be attached directly to the Consignment or Sale Order and in that case, you will need to assign the documents to the correct Sale Order/Consignment.

### How to assign documents to the consignment/sale order

You can view the documents that need assigning from the**Dashboard** or the **Documents**page.

**From the Dashboard**

- Navigate to the Dashboard.
- Scroll down to the Notifications widget.
- Select the blue number against**Unassigned Consignment Customer Invoices**or **Unassigned Sale Order Customer Invoices**.
- This will take you through to the unassigned documents.
- Click the **Begin Assigning** button.

![assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods-0.png?width=670&height=156&name=assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods-0.png)

- Select **Leave File Invoices as it is***(if you want to keep the existing file)*or **Override Invoice with New File** *(if you wish to replace the file)*. If you override the file you will need to upload a new file by clicking **Choose file**.

![assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods-1.png?width=670&height=195&name=assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods-1.png)

- **Search for a Consignment** to assign it to or click **Add New Consignment** to create a new Consignment.

![assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods-2.png?width=670&height=114&name=assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods-2.png)

- Click **Save** or **Save and Process Next Unassigned**.

#### **From the Documents page**

- Navigate to the Documents page, **More**>**Documents**.
- Select the **Unassigned** tab.
- Select **Begin Assigning**.

![assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods-3.png?width=670&height=160&name=assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods-3.png)

- Select **Leave File Invoices as it is***(if you want to keep the existing file)*or **Override Invoice with New File** *(if you wish to replace the file)*. If you override the file you will need to upload a new file by clicking **Choose file**.

![assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods-4.png?width=670&height=195&name=assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods-4.png)

- **Search for a Consignment** to assign it to or click **Add New Consignment** to create a new Consignment.

![assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods-5.png?width=670&height=114&name=assigning-documents-consignment-invoices-sale-order-invoices-pods-5.png)

- Click **Save** or **Save and Process Next Unassigned**.

<a id="authority-to-leave"></a>
## Authority To Leave

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/authority-to-leave_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to set-up
- How to use

### Purpose

There are times when it is not possible to collect a signature at delivery, this provides flexibility to the driver to be able to deliver without a signature.

When enabled this will allow for special instructions to be added to the consignments details to let the driver know they have the Authority to leave the delivery without receiving a signature. They will still be required to record where they left the delivery and take a photo of the delivery for the POD.

Authority to Leave is a Customer level setting, so you will need to enable this for any Customer you wish to use it with.

### How to set-up

- Navigate to your Customers page > Click Edit
- Select the Transport Management Tab > POD tab
- Check to enable  " Allow option for authority to leave on Add Consignment Page " This will add the option on the add consignment page to select "Yes" and will then allow for the driver instructions to be added. Further information on the settings can be found in our Knowledge article here .
- Check to enable " Allow Electronic Deliveries to take place without Signature ". This is required for the driver to be able to mark the order as delivered with no signature. Further information on the settings can be found in our Knowledge article here .

![authority-to-leave-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/authority-to-leave-0.png?width=670&height=405&name=authority-to-leave-0.png)

### How to use

- Once enabled you will see an option for "Authority to Leave" on the "Add Consignment" page and when set to " Yes " you will be able to enter in further instructions for the driver.

![authority-to-leave-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/authority-to-leave-1.png?width=413&height=127&name=authority-to-leave-1.png)

- Once you have selected "Yes" and added the instructions for the driver, these will be visible on their Mobile Delivery App.

![authority-to-leave-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/authority-to-leave-2.png?width=263&height=543&name=authority-to-leave-2.png)

- The Driver can then go ahead and record their POD, further instructions on how to record a signatureless POD can be found here .

<a id="mapping-product-unit-of-measures-to-consignment-fields-transport-products"></a>
## Auto-Generated Consignment Items (Mapping Product Unit of Measures to Consignment Items)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/mapping-product-unit-of-measures-to-consignment-fields-transport-products_

### Table of Contents

- [Purpose](https://help.cartoncloud.com#purpose)
- [#purpose](https://help.cartoncloud.com#purpose)[Prerequisites](https://help.cartoncloud.com#prerequisites)
- [Example](https://help.cartoncloud.com#example)
- How to set up Auto-Generated Consignment Items
- Auto-Generated Consignment Items and the Pack Screen

### Purpose

Please note that if your CartonCloud account was created prior to 1 July 2019, you will be using Consignment Fields. If your account was created post 1 July 2019, you will be using Transport Products. If you would like to discuss migrating to the newer version of the CartonCloud TMS, please use [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com) and lodge a case with our Service Desk.

Auto-generated Consignment Items are created when a Product Unit of Measure (PUOM) is mapped to a Transport Product. This allows CartonCloud to automatically determine how products should be packed and shipped, without requiring manual entry from users.

Auto-generated items reduce data entry and streamline workflows for customers who ship standard product types in consistent formats, such as full cartons, pallets, or directly shippable units.

These items are particularly useful for non-eCommerce warehouses, where precise packing is not always required. However, for e-commerce operations using the Pack Screen, please see '[Auto-Generated Consignment Items and the Pack Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Mapping-Product-Unit-of-Measures-to-Consignment-Fields-Transport-Products#auto-generated-consignment-items-and-the-pack-screen)'.

### Prerequisites

- Automatic Consignment generation from Sales Order must be enabled. Please see Generating a Consignment from a Sale Order .

### Example

| **Unit of Measure** | **Product Type** | **Transport Product** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Carton | Chilled | Chilled Carton |
| Carton | Frozen | Frozen Carton |
| Pallet | Chilled | Chilled Pallet |
| Pallet | Frozen | Frozen Pallet |

### How to set up Auto-Generated Consignment Items

- Navigate to the **Units of Measure** page by typing **Units of Measure** into the Search for anything bar.
- Select the relevant Product Unit of Measure.
- Scroll down to the **Link to Transport Product**section.
- Select a **Product Type** or keep it as None if you do not wish to link the Product Type.
- Select the **Transport Product**to link to the Unit of Measure from the Transport Product drop-down menu.
- Select the **Item Measure**to link to the Unit of Measure from the Item Measure drop-down menu.
- To add an additional link, select the plus icon.
- Click **Save**.

![mapping-product-unit-of-measures-to-consignment-fields-transport-products-0-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/mapping-product-unit-of-measures-to-consignment-fields-transport-products-0-1.png?width=670&height=316&name=mapping-product-unit-of-measures-to-consignment-fields-transport-products-0-1.png)

**From the products page**

You can map the Products Unit of Measure to a Product Type and Transport Product upon adding a new Product Unit of Measure when creating a new Product.

- Navigate to the Products page, **Warehouse**>**Products**.
- Select **+ Add Product**.
- Fill in the applicable fields.
- Within Measurement Category, select **+Add New Measurement**.

![mapping-product-unit-of-measures-to-consignment-fields-transport-products-1-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/mapping-product-unit-of-measures-to-consignment-fields-transport-products-1-1.png?width=670&height=189&name=mapping-product-unit-of-measures-to-consignment-fields-transport-products-1-1.png)

- Fill in the fields for the new Product Unit of Measure and link the Transport Product and Product Type.

![mapping-product-unit-of-measures-to-consignment-fields-transport-products-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/mapping-product-unit-of-measures-to-consignment-fields-transport-products-2.png?width=670&height=424&name=mapping-product-unit-of-measures-to-consignment-fields-transport-products-2.png)

### Auto-Generated Consignment Items and the Pack Screen

You can choose to hide or show Auto-Generated Consignment Items on the Pack Screen. By hiding Auto-Generated Consignment Items, you can utilise the Pack Screen to create Consignment Items, which at times can be a more accurate workflow. With the below settings, you have the flexibility to choose how you create your Consignment Items.

#### **To enable at the organisation level:**

- Navigate to **More > Organisation Settings**.
- Select **Warehouse > Sale Order Settings**.
- Find the setting **“Hide Auto-Generated Consignment Items”**.
- Choose **Yes** to hide or **No** to show auto-generated items on the Pack Screen by default.
- Click **Save**.

#### **To override for a specific customer:**

- Navigate to **Contacts > Customers**.
- Select a customer and click **Edit**.
- Go to the **Warehouse Management > Sale Order** tab.
- Under **Auto-Generated Consignment Items**, select:
  - **Use Organisation Setting**
  - **Yes** (always hide)
  - **No** (always show)
- Click **Save**.

**Factors to consider:**

**Visibility**

- If hidden by settings, unverified auto-generated items will not appear on the Pack Screen.
- If not hidden by settings, a badge labelled “Auto-Generated” appears next to the consignment.

![mapping-product-unit-of-measures-to-consignment-fields-transport-products-3-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/mapping-product-unit-of-measures-to-consignment-fields-transport-products-3-1.png?width=455&height=455&name=mapping-product-unit-of-measures-to-consignment-fields-transport-products-3-1.png)

- You can toggle visibility at any time using the “Show Auto-Generated Items” control on the Pack Screen.
  - If toggling from hidden → visible while editing, you will be prompted to confirm (existing changes may be overwritten).

**Verification**

- Auto-generated items are created with a status of unverified.
- When you pack the order:
  - All packed items become verified.
  - Any hidden, unverified items are deleted and replaced by the packed ones.
- If you edit consignment items manually or update them via the Parser, they are also marked as verified.

**Totals**

- When auto-generated items are hidden, all calculations (weight, volume, quantity) will exclude them.

---

Cash on Delivery's

(COD) together for banking purposes.

here

for more information.

 Export Banking Sheet

- Open the downloaded file.

<a id="cash-on-deliveries"></a>
## Cash on Deliveries

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/cash-on-deliveries_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Cash on delivery overview
- Cash on delivery process
- How to handle EFT payments
- Tight vs flexible control
- Drivers collecting COD on the app
- Additional resources

### Purpose

CartonCloud supports Cash On Delivery (COD) processes both within the Web Application, and on the [Mobile App](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Mobile+App).

The COD processes in CartonCloud have been designed to provide as much visibility and trace-ability as possible, ensuring CODs never go missing.

### Cash on delivery overview

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/4mxvd7jH3u4

### Cash on delivery process

![cash-on-deliveries-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/cash-on-deliveries-0.png?width=670&height=516&name=cash-on-deliveries-0.png)

### How to handle EFT Payments

If the driver does not pickup either Cash or Cheque due to the store advising they have paid via EFT, the best process for the Driver is to lodge that they collected $0.00.
The system will then ask them why they are not collecting the correct amount of money and they can then write down: "Customer paid EFT".

The process from here becomes very easy to handle, as the Cash On Delivery is recorded as $0.00 was collected, the office can then see the reason why the cash was not collected and provide this information back to the client via the Banking Sheet.

### Tight vs Flexible Control

Cash on Delivery (COD) can be configured to be optional (Flexible Control), or forced (Tight Control).

Tight Control means that if a particular Consignment does not have Cash On Delivery Loaded, the Driver will have NO option to add COD to the consignment. This is the typical way COD is used, to prevent drivers being given Cash / Cheques when the client has not specified the particular job is COD.

Flexible Control, however, means the driver will ALWAYS have the option to record COD for the job, even if the job does not have COD listed.

This feature can be configured on a per-customer basis from the Customer Edit page.
**Contacts -> Customers -> (find customer) -> Edit**

Then modify the option to 'Yes - Flexible Control (Driver will always have the option to record COD)'.

Now, on the app the driver will have the option to record COD if they like.

Note: If the Consignment is recorded as 'Requiring COD', then the driver must record COD, otherwise they'll be prompted to enter a reason why.

### Drivers collecting COD on the App

See: [Cash On Delivery](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Cash+On+Delivery)

### Additional Resources

[Export Cash On Delivery Summary Sheet](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Export+Cash+On+Delivery+Summary+Sheet)

---

<a id="cash-on-delivery-cod"></a>
## Cash on Delivery (COD)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/cash-on-delivery-cod_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to enable Cash on Delivery (COD)
- How to mark a Consignment as requiring COD
- Drivers collecting COD on the mobile app
- How to handle EFT payments
- Summary of COD Consignments

### Purpose

A Cash on Delivery is a Consignment where the Driver is required to collect payment at the delivery point. This payment could be for just the freight component or the value of the goods.

CartonCloud supports Cash On Delivery (COD) processes within the Web Application and the Mobile App.

The COD process in CartonCloud is designed to provide as much visibility and traceability as possible.
![cash-on-delivery-cod-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/cash-on-delivery-cod-0.png?width=670&height=516&name=cash-on-delivery-cod-0.png)

### How to enable Cash on Delivery (COD)

To use Cash On Delivery (COD), you need to enable it in the Customer Settings.

- Navigate to the Customers page, Contacts > Customers .
- Select the Customer you wish to apply COD to.
- Select Edit .
- Select the Transport Management tab.
- Select the Defaults tab.
- Scroll down to the Cash On Delivery box.
- From the Accept Cash on Delivery (COD) for the customers consignments setting, select an option from the drop-down menu.

| **Setting** | **Explanation** |
| --- | --- |
| No | The Customer's Consignments will NOT be able to record COD against the Consignment. |
| Yes - Tight Control (Driver will only have the option to record COD if the Consignment is marked as requiring COD) | The Driver will only be able to record COD on the Consignment if the Consignment is marked as requiring COD. This prevents the Driver from being given cash/cheques when the Customer has not specified that particular Consignment is COD. |
| Yes - Flexible Control (Driver will always have the option to record COD) | The Driver will ALWAYS have the option to record COD on the Consignment even if the Consignment does not have COD listed. |

- Scroll to the bottom of the page and select Save .

### How to mark a Consignment as requiring COD

If you selected the Tight Control option in the above steps, you would need to ensure that the Consignments that require COD are flagged as requiring COD; otherwise, the Driver will not have the option to record the COD.

- When adding a Consignment, select the Advanced Options at the bottom of the screen.

![cash-on-delivery-cod-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/cash-on-delivery-cod-1.png?width=670&height=203&name=cash-on-delivery-cod-1.png)

- Select Yes from the drop-down menu against Cash On Delivery .
- Against Cash On Delivery Requirement, select if you wish it to be required, optional or for the Driver to call the supplier.
- Enter the value against the Cash On Delivery Value .
- Scroll down and click +Add Consignment Items .

### Drivers collecting COD on the mobile app

For more information on recording Cash On Delivery Consignments on the mobile app, click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/VgmYHw).

### How to handle EFT Payments

If the Driver does not pick up either Cash or Cheque due to the store advising they have paid via EFT, the best process for the Driver is to lodge that they collected $0.00.
The system will then ask them why they are not collecting the correct amount of money, and they can then write down: "Customer paid EFT".

The process from here becomes straightforward to handle, as the Cash On Delivery is recorded as $0.00 was collected; the office can then see why the cash was not collected and provide this information back to the client via the [Banking Sheet](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/banking-sheets).

### Summary of COD Consignments

Drivers can be given a summary of their COD Consignments for the day. Click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/qAG_Hw) for more information.

---

<a id="changing-the-delivered-date-on-a-consignment"></a>
## Changing the delivered date on a Consignment

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/changing-the-delivered-date-on-a-consignment_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to change the delivered date on a consignment

### Purpose

To change the delivered date on a Consignment. This is useful if the original delivered date on the Consignment is incorrect or there were errors when recording the POD.

### How to change the delivered date on a consignment

- Navigate to the relevant Consignment, Transport > Consignments > Select the relevant Consignment .
- Scroll down to the Specifics heading and click the plus icon to open up more options.
- Scroll down to the Date Delivered within the Specifics window and click Change .

![changing-the-delivered-date-on-a-consignment-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/changing-the-delivered-date-on-a-consignment-0.png?width=408&height=421&name=changing-the-delivered-date-on-a-consignment-0.png)

- Enter the new Date Delivered .
- Click Update .

![changing-the-delivered-date-on-a-consignment-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/changing-the-delivered-date-on-a-consignment-1.png?width=448&height=167&name=changing-the-delivered-date-on-a-consignment-1.png)

<a id="check-delivery-schedule-customer"></a>
## Check Delivery Schedule (Customer)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/check-delivery-schedule-customer_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to view Service Days on a Delivery Run

### Purpose

From the View Service Days  page, it is possible to check the delivery schedule your Transport or Warehousing provider has set up going to a particular delivery zone (suburb & postcode). This is particularly useful for Transport providers who go to rural areas and therefore only service an area on certain days of the week.

Please note that by default delivery schedules will show every day as an active delivery day, so this page is only relevant if your provider has elected to use this feature.

### How to view Service Days on a Delivery Run

- To check the schedule to a specific suburb, search for it in the search bar.

![check-delivery-schedule-customer-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/check-delivery-schedule-customer-0.png?width=670&height=85&name=check-delivery-schedule-customer-0.png)

- Once found, select it and the service days will appear.

![check-delivery-schedule-customer-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/check-delivery-schedule-customer-1.png?width=670&height=429&name=check-delivery-schedule-customer-1.png)

- In the example provided, the suburb has not been configured, therefore all days are showing as active during workdays.
- Active Service days are represented by a tick next to the date.

<a id="configure-the-pickup-addresses-for-ex-warehouse-consignments-on-a-per-customer-basis"></a>
## Configure the Pickup Addresses for Ex-Warehouse Consignments

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/configure-the-pickup-addresses-for-ex-warehouse-consignments-on-a-per-customer-basis_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Step by step guide

### Purpose

By default, every Consignment which is created from a Sale Order will have the Pickup Address set to the Warehouses address. This address is configured underneath the Warehouse setting when you navigate to the "Warehouses" page through Search for anything, then select a Warehouse to edit (shown below).

![configure-the-pickup-addresses-for-ex-warehouse-consignments-on-a-per-customer-basis-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/configure-the-pickup-addresses-for-ex-warehouse-consignments-on-a-per-customer-basis-0.png?width=670&height=393&name=configure-the-pickup-addresses-for-ex-warehouse-consignments-on-a-per-customer-basis-0.png)
However, if you want to have specific Pickup Addresses for each of your customers, you can set this up within the Customer Configuration.

### Step by step guide

To begin, select **Contacts** on the main menu, followed by **Customers** in the drop-down menu.

On the Customers page, select the Customer you wish to set up a specific Ex-Warehouse address for.

Then on the View Customer page, select **Edit**.

On the Edit Customer Page, select the 'Warehouse Management tab followed by the Sale Order sub-tab. Then Scroll Down until reaching the Consignment section.

![configure-the-pickup-addresses-for-ex-warehouse-consignments-on-a-per-customer-basis-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/configure-the-pickup-addresses-for-ex-warehouse-consignments-on-a-per-customer-basis-1.png?width=670&height=181&name=configure-the-pickup-addresses-for-ex-warehouse-consignments-on-a-per-customer-basis-1.png)

From here you can change the **Default Sender Address for Consignments Generated from Sale Orders**.

Once completed, scroll to the bottom and select **Save**.
