<a id="consignment-errors"></a>
## Consignment Errors

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-errors_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Types of consignment errors
- Viewing consignment errors
- Emailing consignment errors to customers for review
- Updating the status of a consignment error
- Closing a consignment error
- Consignment error settings (DMA configuration)

### Purpose

Consignment Errors are reported by Users of CartonCloud and can be reported from within the Consignments themselves. They are typically issued by drivers out doing deliveries. These Errors range from the Consignment being Undeliverable to having their Cartons/Pallets count changed. Consignment Errors by default are visible only to Admins and Onforwarders.

When Consignment Errors are reported, they will need to be actioned a CartonCloud user within your organisation with Administration level permission to be resolved.

### Types of consignment errors

- Undeliverable - Incorrect Address
- Undeliverable - Address Closed
- Damaged Goods
- Delivered Short
- Goods Rejected by Receiver
- Custom
- Undeliverable - Entire Consignment Lost
- Temporary Consignment Error
- POD Generation Failed
- POD FTP Upload Failed
- # of Carton/Pallets Changed
- # of Cartons/Pallet Changed by Driver
- Consignment Altered After Invoicing
- Temperature Issue

You can find more information on how a driver can lodge an error [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/BwqYHw)

### Viewing consignment errors

Click in the "Search For Anything" bar at the top of the screen and type "Consignment Errors"

### Emailing Consignment Errors to Customers for Review

CartonCloud can send a notification to your customer whenever a Consignment Error is lodged.

From the Consignment Error page, select the consignment error and select 'Email to Customer'
![consignment-errors-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-errors-0.png?width=552&height=284&name=consignment-errors-0.png)
From the next screen, select 'Email' and this will bring up a draft email to your customer. You can select/deselect photos to send by clicking individual photos or using the 'select/unselect all' buttons.

![consignment-errors-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-errors-1.png?width=324&height=513&name=consignment-errors-1.png)

Once you hit send this will send a direct notification to your customer asking them for direction on how to deal with the consignment.

In addition to emailing each Consignment Error individually, you can also send these in bulk via a [Discrepancy Report](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/discrepancy-report).

### Updating the status of a Consignment Error

To keep the system up to date, you will need to click the 'Edit' button

![consignment-errors-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-errors-2.png?width=670&height=287&name=consignment-errors-2.png)
From here you can update the status of the Consignment Error, log Customer Decisions and add comments;

| **Heading** | **Meaning** |
| --- | --- |
| Reported By | User who reported the Consignment Error |
| Error Caused By | Who caused the Consignment Error |
| Consignment Error Type | What caused the Consignment Error |
| Consignment Error Charge Action | How do you want to handle the charging of the consignment the error is allocated to (Note this has no impact on the rating of the consignment) |
| Consignment Error Status | The current status of the Consignment Error |
| Customer Decision | Does the customer want you to destroy, return or re-deliver the consignment |
| Comments | Free text field to place any relevant notes |

### Closing a Consignment Error

Once you have actioned all steps to close out the Consignment Error, the status will need to be updated;

Under the Edit Consignment Error page change, the 'Consignment Error Status' to 'Case Closed'

Once completed, click Update and this will return you to the main page of the Consignment Error. Make sure to mark the error as Resolved.

### Consignment error settings (DMA configuration)

From the DMA Configurations page (Consignment Error Settings) you can edit and create Error charge actions, Consignment error statuses and Customer decisions. You can then use these configurations when creating and updating Consignment Errors.

- Navigate to the DMA Configurations page by typing Consignment Error Settings into the Search for anything bar.
- Select either the Error charge actions , Consignment error statuses or Customer decisions tab (depending on what configuration you want to create) and click the Add new button .
- Enter the name and click Add .

| **Configuration** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Error charge actions | How do you want to handle the charging of the consignment the error is allocated to (Note this has no impact on the rating of the consignment) |
| Consignment error status | The status of the Consignment Error |
| Customer decisions | The action the customer wants you to take. For example does the customer want you to destroy, return or re-deliver the consignment? |

---

<a id="consignment-errors-introduction"></a>
## Consignment Errors Introduction

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-errors-introduction_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Type of Consignment Errors

### Purpose

Consignment Errors are reported by Users of CartonCloud and can be reported from within the Consignments themselves. They can be created by drivers out doing deliveries, or by staff in the office or warehouse. Errors could occur due to a Consignment being Undeliverable or due to it having a change of item quantity. By default, Consignment Errors are only visible to Admins and Onforwarders.

When Consignment Errors are reported, they need to be actioned by a CartonCloud user within your organisation with Administration level permission to be resolved.

While no action needs to be taken on consignment errors just now during the setup stage, it's important to understand what they are and how they work, as you'll no doubt have them appear on or before Go Live.

### Types of Consignment Errors

Consignment errors can be created for the following reasons.

- Undeliverable - Incorrect Address
- Undeliverable - Address Closed
- Damaged Goods
- Delivered Short
- Goods Rejected by Receiver
- Custom
- Undeliverable - Entire Consignment Lost
- Temporary Consignment Error
- POD Generation Failed
- POD FTP Upload Failed
- # of Carton/Pallets Changed
- # of Cartons/Pallet Changed by Driver
- Consignment Altered After Invoicing
- Temperature Issue

---

<a id="consignment-grouping"></a>
## Consignment Grouping

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-grouping_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Which consignments can be grouped together
- Where consignment grouping settings can be configured in CartonCloud
- How to manually group consignments
  - Consignment list view
- Mobile app grouping
- Viewing and modifying consignment groups
- Turning on consignment group charging
- Recording adhoc or manual charges on grouped consignments
- Grouping consignments with different product types
- Automatically group consignments when added to an invoice
- Automatically group consignments on a manifest
- Prevent consignment grouping by address

### Purpose

There are some small differences to Consignment Grouping behaviour between accounts created before or after 1 July 2019. If your account was created prior to 1 July 2019 please see [this article](https://help.cartoncloud.com/pages/viewpage.action?pageId=540477952)instead.

Consignment Grouping is when CartonCloud groups multiple consignments together. When consignments are grouped they become known as "child" consignments and a new "parent" consignment is created which links these "child" consignments together.

This allows you to allocate multiple consignments in a group and charge for them as a single consignment with all consignment items aggregate.

This differs from [Consignment Grouping on the mobile app](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Grouping+Consignments+%28Mobile%29+to+record+a+single+POD) which is about how consignments appear on the driver's list of consignments and the ability to record multiple POD's for the same location once grouped.

To summarise, Consignment Grouping on the Web app allows you to group consignments to be allocated and charged as a single consignment, while grouping on the mobile app is about grouping the consignments to record a single POD.

### Which Consignments can be grouped together

There are some requirements for consignments to be grouped together:

- Consignments must not be on an "Approved" invoiced yet - If a consignment is added to an "Approved" invoice they will not group together until it is rolled back to a draft.
- Consignments being grouped must be of the same Service type. For example, the system will not allow you to group together an Express consignment with a General consignment. This is to avoid charging related issues.
- Consignments with different Consignment Types can be merged together for invoicing purposes, however, they must have matching Service Types and the resulting parent Consignment will inherit its Consignment Type from the first consignment that is selected.

### Where Consignment Grouping Settings can be configured in CartonCloud

Consignment Grouping in CartonCloud can be adjusted across multiple areas of the system for customised configuration based on your requirements.

A complete list of Consignment Grouping settings and their linked information is provided below.

| **Setting Location** | **Description** | **Setting Default** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Address Settings | [Allow automatic Consignment grouping](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Consignment+Grouping#ConsignmentGrouping-automatic) | Enabled |
| Customer Settings | [Automatically Group Consignments on a Manifest](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Consignment+Grouping#ConsignmentGrouping-group) | Disabled |
| Customer Settings | [Automatically Group Consignments when added to an Invoice](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Consignment+Grouping#ConsignmentGrouping-invoice) | Disabled |
| Organisation Settings | [Group Consignments with different Product Types](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Consignment+Grouping#ConsignmentGrouping-product) | Disabled |

### How to manually group Consignments

Consignment List View

From within the Web App, you can group consignments manually by selecting the consignments you wish to group and select 'Group Together';

![consignment-grouping-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-grouping-0.png?width=670&height=204&name=consignment-grouping-0.png)

A new page will open providing you with further functionality for the grouping of the consignments you have selected.

These are the details which will carry through to the "parent" consignment. The parent consignment is a new consignment which will be created in the system to contain all of the consignments you are grouping together. This consignment will be marked as a Group consignment with a red G next to it.

You may also choose to add extra consignments to the group from this page by selecting **Add Consignment**.

![consignment-grouping-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-grouping-1.png?width=435&height=371&name=consignment-grouping-1.png)

Once you are ready, select **Group** and the consignments you have selected will all be grouped underneath the parent consignment you have just created.

The parent consignment will now appear on the Consignment List Screen. Groups can be distinguished by the red G next to the ID column.

![consignment-grouping-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-grouping-2.png?width=670&height=109&name=consignment-grouping-2.png)

### Mobile App Grouping

Grouping consignments in the Mobile app behaves different from the web app and is explained in the article "[Grouping Consignments to record a single POD](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Grouping+Consignments+%28Mobile%29+to+record+a+single+POD)"

### Viewing and Modifying Consignment Groups

To view and modify an existing Consignment Group, you will need to select on the 'Parent Consignment' from the Consignment List view. This will be flagged by the red 'G' as indicated above. You can then access the group details by selecting the **Group** tab.

![consignment-grouping-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-grouping-3.png?width=670&height=253&name=consignment-grouping-3.png)
From here you can select each line to navigate to each respective consignment. You can also select **Edit Group** which will allow you to either remove the consignments or add additional consignments to the group.

![consignment-grouping-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-grouping-4.png?width=501&height=196&name=consignment-grouping-4.png)

Automatic Consignment Grouping when added to an Invoice

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/C3G6w0cGrBA

This automatic grouping setting now also requires consignments to be of the same service type.

### Turning on Consignment Group Charging

If you want grouped consignments to be charged **as a single consignment** on an invoice, rather than the individual consignments contained within that group, you must first enable a setting on the Rate Card being used by the Customer.

- To do this, select More in the main menu, followed by Customer Charges in the drop-down menu.
- Select the Customer charge you wish to charge consignment Groups for.
- Once viewing the Customer Charge, select Edit .
- Scroll down until you get to the setting: Consignment Group Charging and change it to Yes.
- Finally, scroll down and select Save for the changes to be applied to the Rate Card.
- Now all Consignments using this Rate Card that you group together will be charged as a group, rather than individual consignments.
- Updating and Recording Charges on a Group Consignment
- To adjust the number of items on grouped consignments the children consignments must be updated individually. The number of items on the parent consignment is aggregated from the children and is read-only.
- Once changes to a child consignment are made (such as adding a pallet) the group parent consignment will inherit those changes and its charges will update accordingly.

### Recording Adhoc or Manual Charges on grouped Consignments

Adhoc & Manual charges can be recorded against the parent or any child consignment (provided the consignment is not on a finalised invoice).

If an Adhoc or manual charge is added to a child consignment it will automatically also appear against the parent consignment in the charges table.

A link to the child consignment will display on the charges line in the table so that it is easy to find which consignment it belongs to.

Manual and Adhoc charges recorded against a child consignment will also display next to the child consignment on the Invoice summary once the grouped consignment is invoiced. This makes it easier to see where charges on the group originated from while providing a complete breakdown.

Aggregation of Group Consignment Items

If consignments are grouped together with identical consignment line items then they will be merged into the same line and the quantities will be added together.

However, if just one detail, such as the Code, Description or a dimension does not match, then they will be added as separate line items.

### Grouping Consignments with Different Product Types

By default Consignments of different Product types (for example General & Frozen) are not allowed to be grouped in the system. However, if required this can be changed so that for example you can group an ambient consignment with a chilled consignment (perhaps it does not matter if the ambient products get cold).

- To enable this, in the main menu select More , followed by Organisation Settings .
- Select the Transport Tab.
- Scroll down to Other Transport Settings
- Tick the box for the setting Allow Consignment Grouping when consignments have different Product Types .
- Finally, scroll to the bottom of the page and select Save .
- CartonCloud will now allow you to group consignments with different Product Types.
- Enabling or Disabling Automatic Consignment Grouping
- If you wish to modify the settings around Consignment Grouping, you can do so by following the below steps.

### Automatically Group consignments when added to an Invoice

It is possible to choose for each customer whether you want their consignments to be grouped when added to an invoice, provided the **Delivery Run**, **Delivery Address** and **Delivery Date** are the same.

By default, this will not occur so a setting change is required.

- Navigate to the customer you wish to turn the setting on for by selecting Contacts in the main menu, followed by Customers in the drop-down menu.
- Then select the Customer.
- Now on the View Customer page, select Edit .
- From within the Invoice tab scroll down until you see the section Other Invoice Configuration Options and enable the setting Automatically group consignments when added to Invoice if Delivery Run, Collect Address, Delivery Address, Delivery Date and Service Type are same .
- Finally, scroll to the bottom of the page and select Save to apply the change.

### Automatically Group consignments on a Manifest

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/AYI5z7cpSS0

- By default, consignments which are going to the same location on the same Manifest will not be automatically grouped together.
- If you do want consignments to group together and be charged together for a specific customer then you will need to turn the below setting on.
- Navigate to the customer you wish to turn the setting on for by selecting Contacts in the main menu, followed by Customers in the drop-down menu.
- Then select the Customer.
- Now on the View Customer page, select Edit .
- From within the Transport Management tab and within the Defaults sub-tab you can enable Automatic Consignment Grouping on Manifest Import by enabling the setting shown below.
- Finally, scroll to the bottom of the page and select Save to apply the change.

### Prevent Consignment Grouping by Address

- If you don't want Consignments to automatically group for a specific address you can turn this setting off for each specific address record.
- Navigate to the Address record by selecting More in the main menu, followed by Addresses in the drop-down menu.
- Find and select the address you wish to turn grouping off for.
- Once viewing the Address record, select Edit .
- At the bottom of the Edit Address page, you will be able to disable the setting shown below.
- Finally, scroll to the bottom of the page and select Save to apply the change.

---

<a id="consignment-item-level-scanning"></a>
## Consignment Item-Level Scanning

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-item-level-scanning_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Prerequisites
  - Configure Transport Products
  - Consignment Item Label
- Benefits
- Use Cases
- How To Steps
  - Web App
  - Mobile App

### Purpose

Item-Level Scanning allows drivers to scan individual item labels at the point of delivery using the CartonCloud mobile app. This ensures that every item in a Consignment is accounted for, reduces delivery errors, and provides complete scan visibility.

This feature also supports label generation rules based on transport product quantity or pallets, making it easier to match the physical items loaded to what’s scanned on delivery.

### Prerequisites

Before using this feature:

- Enable the feature in your CartonCloud account, **Organisation Settings** > **Transport**> **Enable Item-Level Scanning**.
- It is not required, but highly recommended that your Transport Products are configured with a **Split By Field** value.
- You must have set up the correct Item-Level label template (ZPL or PDF).
- Drivers must be using a 6.34.0 or higher version of the CartonCloud mobile app.

#### Configure Transport Products

- Navigate to Transport Product by typing Transport Products into the Search for anything.
- Select the relevant Transport Product.
- Update the **Split by Field** to either **Quantity** or **Pallet**. This field will be used to determine how many item labels are required for the Transport Product.

![consignment-item-level-scanning-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-item-level-scanning-0.png?width=670&height=270&name=consignment-item-level-scanning-0.png)

Note: If you have a large number of Transport Products to update, you can update the Transport Products in bulk following the instructions [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Setting-up-Transport-Products#export-import-transport-products).

#### Consignment Item Label

Consignment Item Level Scanning uses the Consignment Item ZPL template. This is used for ZPL and PDF labels.

### Benefits

- Reduces the risk of missed items during delivery.
- Prevents re-delivery costs due to loading mistakes.
- Provides full visibility over each scanned item.
- Captures individual item proof-of-delivery.

### Use Cases

Use Item-Level Scanning when:

- Customers require full item-level proof of delivery.
- Drivers need to confirm delivery of multiple cartons or pallets.
- You want to monitor delivery performance at an item level.

### How To Steps

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/-fWpvr5bUUU

#### Web App

From the web app, you can view and edit consignment items, print consignment item labels and view scan history.

- Navigate to Consignments, **Transport** > **Consignments**.
- Select the relevant Consignment.
- Select the **Consignment Items** tab.
- The **ruler** icon will be highlighted if the field is used for a cubic multiplier.
- The **printer** icon will be highlighted if the field is used for label generation. This is set from the Split by Field at the Transport Product level and can also be updated directly against the Consignment Item by selecting the printer icon.

![consignment-item-level-scanning-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-item-level-scanning-1.png?width=670&height=245&name=consignment-item-level-scanning-1.png)

**Generating Consignment Item Labels:**

- As you enter a Product Code and a Quantity/Pallet count, the required number of labels will be generated automatically on save.

![consignment-item-level-scanning-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-item-level-scanning-2.png?width=670&height=299&name=consignment-item-level-scanning-2.png)

![consignment-item-level-scanning-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-item-level-scanning-3.png?width=670&height=314&name=consignment-item-level-scanning-3.png)

- Click Save .

![consignment-item-level-scanning-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-item-level-scanning-4.png?width=670&height=270&name=consignment-item-level-scanning-4.png)

- If you choose not to use the auto-generated labels, you can edit the label reference before saving.

**Printing Consignment Item Labels:**

- You can print all Consignment Item labels using the **Print Labels** button in the top right corner, or print individual Consignment Item labels using the print icon against each label. This is useful if a particular label has been damaged.

![consignment-item-level-scanning-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-item-level-scanning-5.png?width=670&height=261&name=consignment-item-level-scanning-5.png)

**Viewing Scan History:**

- As the Consignment Item labels are scanned using the mobile app, the scan history will appear in the Scan History tab.

![consignment-item-level-scanning-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-item-level-scanning-6.png?width=670&height=226&name=consignment-item-level-scanning-6.png)

- You will be able to view:
  - Each Consignment Item label reference
  - Scan date and time
  - Verification method (manual or scanned)

### Mobile App

From the mobile app, you can scan and confirm the Consignment Items when recording the POD.

- On the CartonCloud mobile app, select the **Delivering** mode.

![consignment-item-level-scanning-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-item-level-scanning-7.png?width=281&height=560&name=consignment-item-level-scanning-7.png)

- Select the relevant Consignment.
- Select the **Record POD** tab.
- Under the Delivered heading, select the **Scan Items**button.

![consignment-item-level-scanning-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-item-level-scanning-8.png?width=289&height=580&name=consignment-item-level-scanning-8.png)

- Use the Scan Items camera scanning functionality to scan the Consignment Item label barcodes. You can also use the tick box against the label to manually update the item as confirmed. Whether the label was confirmed via scan or manually will be available in the Scan History.

![consignment-item-level-scanning-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-item-level-scanning-9.png?width=307&height=618&name=consignment-item-level-scanning-9.png)

- As the labels are scanned, the Consignment Items on the Record POD are updated to delivered.

![consignment-item-level-scanning-10](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-item-level-scanning-10.png?width=290&height=585&name=consignment-item-level-scanning-10.png)

- Continue with the POD process of recording a signature, photos and name and click **Save POD**.

![consignment-item-level-scanning-11](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-item-level-scanning-11.png?width=293&height=585&name=consignment-item-level-scanning-11.png)

![consignment-item-level-scanning-12](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-item-level-scanning-12.png?width=281&height=566&name=consignment-item-level-scanning-12.png)

<a id="consignment-list-view"></a>
## Consignment List View

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-list-view_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Consignment information
- Individual consignment
- Grouped consignments
  - Closed
  - Open
- Consignment types and labels
- List actions
- Record POD shortcut
  - Individual consignments
  - Grouped consignments
- Ordering consignments
- Locking consignments positions

### Purpose

Within the CartonCloud mobile apps, consignments are presented in a list view to allow an overview of outstanding jobs and the option of selecting consignments for further actions (e.g. to see more details or collect a POD).

![consignment-list-view-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-list-view-0.png?width=225&height=401&name=consignment-list-view-0.png)

### Consignment Information

Each incomplete consignment is represented in the list view as either an individual row of data or as part of a group of consignments. Groups of consignments are created automatically based on a consignment's address.

The information displayed includes:

### Individual Consignment

![consignment-list-view-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-list-view-1.png?width=319&height=257&name=consignment-list-view-1.png)

- **Type of Consignment:** Please see "*Consignment Types and Labels*" below for more information. This label also acts as a lock/unlock button should you wish to lock a consignment into its current position before optimizing a route (see "*Locking Consignment Positions*" below).
- **Consignment Address:**This is either the delivery, pickup or onforwarder address, depending on the type of consignment (or the stage of the consignment if it is a Point to Point consignment). Both the company name and the suburb details will be given (if available). For Point to Point consignment that had their pickup completed and are awaiting delivery, this will be reflected here as well, e.g. "*Big W, MOOREBANK (1/2)*"
- **Customer Name**
- **Consignment Date**
- **Consignment Id and****Reference**
- **Custom Fields:**Based on the tenant settings, information about for example the number of Cartons or Pallets included in the consignment will be displayed here, using the custom field's short name - e.g. CTN for Cartons. For more information see: [Custom Fields on Mobile](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Custom+Fields+on+Mobile)

### Grouped Consignments

#### Closed

![consignment-list-view-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-list-view-2.png?width=341&height=219&name=consignment-list-view-2.png)

The information displayed includes:

- **Consignment Address:**This is either the delivery, pickup or onforwarder address, depending on the type of consignment (or the stage of the consignment if it is a Point to Point consignment). Both the company name and the suburb details will be given (if available).
- **Consignment Date**
- **Custom Fields:**Based on the tenant settings, information about for example the number of Cartons or Pallets included in the grouped consignment will be displayed here, using the custom field's short name - e.g. CTN for Cartons. The values shown here represent the total number per custom field for all the consignments in the group.
- **Consignment Counter:**This button displays the number of consignments grouped together and will open a more detailed summary of all the individual consignments when tapped.

#### Open

After tapping the Consignment Counter Button on a Grouped Consignment row, additional rows will open up, showing the consignments contained within the group. The details included in these rows are the same as for individual consignments (see above, "*Individual Consignment*").
![consignment-list-view-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-list-view-3.png?width=264&height=470&name=consignment-list-view-3.png)

### Consignment Types and Labels

Based on the type of the consignment, each row in the list view displays a Consignment Type label illustrating the type of consignment you're dealing with (and which stage if it is a Point to Point consignment).

### List Actions

**Row Selection / Consignment Detail View**

On selecting a row in the list view, you will be forwarded to the Consignment Detail View which presents you with more information about the consignment. In the case of grouped consignments, tapping on the group's main row (the one containing the counter button) will again forward you to the Consignment Detail View. This time though the details of all the consignments contained within the group will be displayed, one after another, the same way they would be presented if you grouped consignments manually through the "*Group Consignments*" menu option.

### Record POD Shortcut

In addition to being able to select the consignment rows to proceed to the consignment detail view, the consignment list view also allows you to proceed directly to recording a POD.

This can be achieved by swiping right on the consignment row.

#### **Individual Consignments**
![consignment-list-view-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-list-view-4.png?width=273&height=487&name=consignment-list-view-4.png)

#### Grouped Consignments

The shortcut to the Record POD view is available for grouped consignments as well. As with individual consignments simply swipe right on the group's row. Doing this will combine all consignments in the group and allow you to collect a single POD for all of them.

Please note, that under certain circumstances a grouped POD will not be possible, e.g. when combining consignments of varying types or when combining Point to Point consignments. An appropriate warning will be given if this applies.
 ![consignment-list-view-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-list-view-5.png?width=280&height=500&name=consignment-list-view-5.png)

On an open group of consignments, individual consignments also have the POD shortcut available, should you want to record a POD for only one of them or if grouped PODs are not available.

![consignment-list-view-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-list-view-6.png?width=275&height=492&name=consignment-list-view-6.png)

### Ordering Consignments

Ordering Consignments allows users to sort their jobs according to their preference without the sort order getting lost on refreshing their jobs from the server.

Each consignment row can be dragged and dropped. Just select the consignment you want to move around and drag it into your preferred position before dropping it there. Now, even on refreshing consignments from the server, the sort order of the job list will be preserved.

Please note that on starting a drag & drop action, all open grouped consignments will be automatically closed. Moreover, individual consignments within a group cannot be moved from their position.

![consignment-list-view-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-list-view-7.png?width=303&height=539&name=consignment-list-view-7.png)

### Locking Consignment Positions

Should you want to lock a consignment into a certain position before optimizing a route, tap the Consignment Type label on the left of the consignment info in the relevant row of the list view to activate a lock for the consignment.

Locks can also be applied to grouped consignment, by tapping the empty space to the left of the consignment info (where a Consignment Type label is positioned for individual consignments). In this case, all the individual consignments within the group will be locked into their current position.

To remove a lock, simply tap the label again.

![consignment-list-view-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-list-view-8.png?width=289&height=518&name=consignment-list-view-8.png)

---

<a id="consignment-sorting-and-filtering"></a>
## Consignment Sorting and Filtering

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-sorting-and-filtering_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- To access the settings
- Sort consignments
- Default sort order
- Sort by proximity
- Filter consignments
  - Error consignments ​​​​​​​
- Address groups
  - Always expand address groups
- Completed consignments - show completed jobs
- Split by
  - Delivery run
  - Run sheet

### Purpose

The CartonCloud app allows you to choose from a number of settings to personalise the way consignments are displayed in the job list.

### To access the settings

To access these settings, select the filter button in the navigation bar.

![consignment-sorting-and-filtering-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-sorting-and-filtering-0.png?width=219&height=390&name=consignment-sorting-and-filtering-0.png)

There are several buttons located within the filter view:

- Reset: reset any changes that have occurred since opening the filter view.
- Cancel: cancels the filter view display.
- Apply: applies the current settings and updates the consignment list accordingly.

### Sort Consignments

There are two options for sorting consignments within the list view:

![consignment-sorting-and-filtering-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-sorting-and-filtering-1.png?width=284&height=507&name=consignment-sorting-and-filtering-1.png)

### Default Sort Order

This selection defaults to the standard sort order, i.e. the one set in the web app or the one achieved by dragging and dropping consignments or optimizing a route.

### Sort By Proximity

On selecting this option, the app will use your current location to sort the consignments by proximity to your current position. For this information to be accurate, you need to be clocked on and have location services enabled.

If the app cannot access a current location, a warning will be displayed informing the user that the last known location is being used. This is due to the last known location potentially being out of date.

Consignment distances to the current (or last known) location are being shown in the list view for each consignment. Current location values are shown in blue, last known (and potentially inaccurate) location values are shown in red.

### Filter Consignments

#### **Error Consignments**

Using the filter view, you can choose whether or not to display error consignments in the list view.
 ![consignment-sorting-and-filtering-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-sorting-and-filtering-2.png?width=270&height=481&name=consignment-sorting-and-filtering-2.png)
See the example below for a list view showing error consignments vs. the same list view without error consignments being displayed.

### Address Groups

Using the filter view, you can choose whether or not to group consignments by address. ( Stop Consignment Grouping )
![consignment-sorting-and-filtering-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-sorting-and-filtering-3.png?width=259&height=461&name=consignment-sorting-and-filtering-3.png)

#### **Always Expand Address Groups**

Once address grouping has been activated, you are presented with another option - choosing whether or not to always expand address groups. If this is enabled, you will always be able to see the sub-consignments of an address group. If this setting is disabled, the address groups will be initially closed and can be manually opened by selecting the counter button on the right-hand side of the main consignment of the group.

![consignment-sorting-and-filtering-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-sorting-and-filtering-4.png?width=432&height=366&name=consignment-sorting-and-filtering-4.png)

### Completed Consignments - Show Completed Jobs

Display Delivered Consignments (won't disappear when has a POD automatically). Using the filter view, you can choose whether or not to display completed consignments in the list view.
![consignment-sorting-and-filtering-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-sorting-and-filtering-5.png?width=278&height=495&name=consignment-sorting-and-filtering-5.png)

Completed consignments are highlighted in green in the list view and while they can still be selected to see the consignment details, actions that can be performed on them are limited, i.e. no POD can be recorded and no errors lodged. Adhoc Charges can be submitted for completed consignments.

![consignment-sorting-and-filtering-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-sorting-and-filtering-6.png?width=389&height=348&name=consignment-sorting-and-filtering-6.png)

### Split By

#### **Delivery Run**

Using the filter view you can choose whether to separate the list view by delivery runs.

![consignment-sorting-and-filtering-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-sorting-and-filtering-7.png?width=248&height=441&name=consignment-sorting-and-filtering-7.png)

See the examples below for a list showing the consignment list separated and not separated by a delivery run. Please note that within each separate section consignments will still be grouped by address if applicable.

Also, dragging and dropping of consignments is only allowed within the delivery run section they belong to.

#### **Run Sheet**

Within the mobile apps, there is an additional option of splitting the consignments into sections by run sheets.

See the examples below for a list showing the consignment list separated by run sheet and not separated by run sheet. Please note that within each separate section consignments will still be grouped by address if applicable.

Also, dragging and dropping of consignments is only allowed within the delivery run section they belong to.

---

<a id="consignment-status-colours"></a>
## Consignment Status Colours

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-status-colours_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Consignment status colours
- Map view pin colours

### Purpose

As a consignment changes status within the CartonCloud mobile apps the user interface will display different prompts to this is highlighted by changing its background colour in both of the list views, as well as modifying its pin colour on the map view.

### Consignment status colours

| Colour | Status | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **White** | Normal | Waiting for Action. |
| **Purple** | Error Lodged | An error has been lodged for this consignment. |
| **Orange** | Point To Point Stage 1 (Pickup) Completed | The consignment is a Point to Point consignment and the first stage (Pickup) has been completed |

### Map view pin colours

Consignments pins on the map view change colour depending on the consignment status in the same way as illustrated above for list views. The below image and table highlight what each different coloured pin represents. To distinguish a Pickup consignment in normal status from a Point To Point consignment, Point to Point consignments are displayed as "split" pins, showing them as containing both a Pickup and a Delivery stage with the pin numbers illustrating which stage of the Point to Point consignment the pin relates to -  **(1)** or  **(2)**.
​​​​​​​
![consignment-status-colours-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-status-colours-0.png?width=210&height=374&name=consignment-status-colours-0.png)

| **Colour** | **Status** |
| --- | --- |
| Dark Orange | Normal |
| Light Orange | Pickup Job |
| Red | Error Lodged |
| Green (with "split" split pins showing both a Pickup and a Delivery stage) | Point to Point Job |

---

<a id="consignment-statuses"></a>
## Consignment Statuses

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-statuses_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- To add/edit a consignment cancelled status
- Update or reset consignment status

### Purpose

The below statuses are used to communicate the point in the process a Consignment is currently at.

| **Awaiting Sale Order Packing** | The Sale Order associated with the Consignment has not yet been packed. |
| --- | --- |
| **Awaiting Pickup** | The Consignment is yet to be collected by the driver. This status is only for Consignments that require a pickup. |
| **In Warehouse** | The Consignment is in the warehouse and is ready to go out for delivery. |
| **Awaiting Pickup (Point to Point)** | The Consignment is yet to be picked up by the driver. This status is only for Consignment types of Point to Point. |
| **In Transit (Pickup->Warehouse)** | The Consignment has been collected by the driver and is en route to the warehouse. This status is only for Consignments that require a pickup and are coming back to the warehouse. |
| **In Transit (Warehouse->Delivery)** | The Consignment has left the Warehouse and is with the driver en route to its delivery location. This status is for Consignments that are already at the warehouse. |
| **In Transit (Pickup→Delivery)** | The Consignment has been picked up and is with the driver and en route to its delivery location. This status is for Consignments that require a pickup. |
| **With On Forwarder** | If the Consignment is travelling with an On Forwarder and the Consignment has been handed over for delivery (left the Warehouse). |
| **Delivered to Warehouse** | The Consignment has now arrived at the Warehouse. This status is for pickup Consignments that do not require delivery and are coming back to the Warehouse. |
| **Delivered** | The Consignment has been delivered to its final destination. |
| **Delivered (Point to Point)** | The point to point Consignment has been delivered to its final destination and is now complete. |
| **Collected** | Collected status is based off the Delivery Run that the Consignment is allocated to. If you go to Transport > Delivery Runs > (select a Run) > Details > Edit > Update Final Consignment Delivery Status field |
| **Awaiting Drop Off** | this is set when creating a Consignment, for the pickup address, this is an option to select "Goods will be dropped off at depot". |

When cancelling a Consignment there are a number of statuses you can use depending on why the Consignment has to be cancelled.

- Cancelled
- Returned
- No Stock/Never Arrived
- Reissued
- Lost

Consignment Cancelled statuses are customisable, meaning you can add and edit a Consignment Cancelled status.

### To add/edit a Consignment Cancelled status

- Navigate to the Consignment Delivery Cancelled Statuses page by typing 'Consignment Delivery Cancelled Statuses' into the Search for anything bar.
- Select the Add Consignment Delivery Cancelled Status button in the top left corner.
- From here you can create your own Consignment Delivery Cancelled Status.
- To edit a current status, select the Edit button next to the status you would like to edit.

![consignment-statuses-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-statuses-0.png?width=670&height=161&name=consignment-statuses-0.png)

### Update or reset consignment status

To update a Consignment status you will need to do so manually, either individually or in bulk.

The only time the status will update automatically and no manual intervention is required, is when a POD is recorded against the Consignment. When the POD is recorded the Consignment will automatically update to 'Delivered' or if it is a Pick Up Consignment the status will update to 'In Warehouse'.

There is also the option to enable [Auto In Transit](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/make-consignments-auto-update-to-in-transit-warehouse-to-delivery) which will allow CartonCloud to automatically update the status from In Warehouse to In transit. However, this is only for Consignments that meet certain criteria and is only updated once a day.

**To update the status of a Consignment in bulk (for example, when the truck leaves the warehouse you would update all Consignments to 'In Transit' using the bulk function).**

- Navigate to the Consignments page by typing 'Consignments' into the Search for anything bar.
- Use the filter and sort function to find the relevant Consignments.
- Select the Consignments you wish to allocate by selecting the tick box.
- Once all relevant Consignments are selected, click Update Status .
- From the drop-down menu select the status you wish to apply.

**To update or reset the status of a Consignment individually:**

- Click on the individual Consignment you wish to update.
- From here, you can either reset or update the status.

---

<a id="consignment-types"></a>
## Consignment Types

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-types_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Consignment types
- Workflow of consignment types
  - Delivery, split, duplicate, return
  - Pickup
  - Point to point
  - Warehouse Fulfilment
- Configuring the default consignment type
- Consignment type field positions
  - Standard field position
  - Advanced field position

### Purpose

Consignment Types change the behaviour of how a Consignment is handled within CartonCloud.

The largest operational difference between Consignments Type is whether a driver is required to record a signature at the pickup, delivery point, or both.

They also come into play if you are using Onforwarders for the delivery of Consignments.

### Consignment types

**CartonCloud contains the following consignment types:**

- Consignment Types - Delivery Consignment
- Consignment Types - Pickup
- Consignment Types - Pickup + Delivery
- Consignment Types - Point to Point Consignment
- Consignment Types - Return
- Consignment Types - Warehouse Fulfilments

### Workflow of consignment types

#### **Delivery, Split, Duplicate, Return**

![consignment-types-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-types-0.png?width=670&height=241&name=consignment-types-0.png)

Delivery style consignments are considered "Cross-Dock", in that they're leaving from the Warehouse and only tracking on the delivery component is recorded.

With these consignments, they're not typically given a "Delivery Run Date" (and therefore don't show up for allocation), until they have been marked "In Warehouse".

**Pickup**

![consignment-types-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-types-1.png?width=670&height=145&name=consignment-types-1.png)
Pickup Consignments are often used in conjunction with Cross-Dock (Delivery) consignments in order to bring the bulk pallets back into the depot from the client's site.

**Point to Point**

![consignment-types-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-types-2.png?width=670&height=153&name=consignment-types-2.png)
Point to Point (commonly referred to as Taxi-Truck), are deliveries which require the driver to capture both Pickup and Delivery details on the phone. These are jobs in which a single driver will be both collecting the stock, and also delivering to the end destination.

#### **Warehouse Fulfilment**

Warehouse Fulfilment Consignments are available for WMS-only CartonCloud accounts. The Warehouse Fulfilment works in conjunction with the [Pack Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Pack-Screen) to create an optimised packing process. The Warehouse Fulfilment moves between the following statuses:

- Awaiting Sale Order Packing
- In Warehouse
- Shipped
- Delivered (Warehouse Fulfilment)

### Configuring the Default Consignment Type

The default consignment type can be configured from the Organisation Settings (under the Transport tab):

| **Field** | **Description** | **Default** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Default Consignment Type for Admins | When an administrator or other staff member (anything other than being logged in as a Customer) is entering a consignment, what should the Default consignment Type be?      **Note**: None will force the user to select an option, so they cannot proceed with manually selecting something. | Delivery |
| Consignment Type Field Position for Admins | Where the Consignment Type option appears if the user is another other than a Customer, either under the "Standard" or the "Advanced" sections, see below for more information | Standard Fields |
| Default Consignment Type for Customers | When a customer is entering a consignment, what should the Default Consignment Type be? | Delivery |
| Consignment Type Field Position for Customers | Where the Consignment Type option appears if the user is a Customer, either under the "Standard" or the "Advanced" sections, see below for more information. | Advanced Fields |

Be careful not to set the Default to None, and then put the field into the "Advanced Fields". The reason is, Advanced Fields are hidden by default when the page is shown, so the user will fill out everything they can see, click Save, and then they'll need to open up the Advanced Options to fill out the form. If you're going to force users to select a Consignment Type, put it into the Standard Fields.

### Consignment Type Field Positions

When adding a new consignment the placement of the "Consignment Type" field can be in either the "Standard fields" or the "Advanced Fields". Putting things into the "Advanced" fields is good if you do 95% of your work with a single Consignment Type and are not expecting it to be changed often.

#### **Standard Field Position**

In the Standard Field Position, the Consignment Type selection appears at the top right underneath the Customer Selection (note, if a Customer is adding a Consignment then they don't have the Customer selection box).

![consignment-types-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-types-3.png?width=600&height=239&name=consignment-types-3.png)

#### **Advanced Field Position**

In the Advanced Field Position, the Consignment Type selection appears lower down, underneath the "Advanced Options". Note that when the page loads the Advanced Options are hidden and have to be expanded.

![consignment-types-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-types-4.png?width=670&height=319&name=consignment-types-4.png)

---

<a id="consignment-types-delivery-consignment"></a>
## Consignment Types - Delivery Consignment

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-types-delivery-consignment_

This is the most common consignment within a Cross Dock scenario.

Delivery Consignments contain only a Delivery component. This means the driver will not be given a collection address, nor will they be able to collect a signature at the time of collection.

This Consignment type is usually best for freight leaving a designated warehouse.

---

<a id="consignment-types-pickup"></a>
## Consignment Types - Pickup

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-types-pickup_

Pickup Consignments are only used for collecting freight and returning it to a set Warehouse. These Consignments will only contain only a Pickup component in which the Driver can optionally gather a signature/photograph when collecting.

---

<a id="consignment-types-pickup-delivery"></a>
## Consignment Types - Pickup + Delivery

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-types-pickup-delivery_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Behaviour

### Purpose

This Pickup + Delivery Consignment type creates two separate consignments, one for Pickup and one for Delivery. These two consignments are linked to each other by a parent-child relationship.

After creating a Pickup + Delivery Consignment, the user will be redirected to the corresponding new Delivery consignment.

**By default, the Pickup consignment will be the Parent Consignment, while the Delivery consignment will be the Child Consignment. This can be seen within the Tree Structure Tab when viewing either of the Consignments.**

### Behaviour

1) All the information on the newly created Pickup and Delivery consignments will be same, except for addresses (see 2) & 3) below).

2) For the Pickup consignment created:

1. Pickup Address: Pickup address set by the user while creating Pickup + Delivery.
2. Delivery Address: Address of current warehouse. If the address for the warehouse is not set, the tenant's default address is used.

3) For the Delivery consignment created:

1. Pickup Address: Address of current warehouse. If the address for the warehouse is not set, the tenant's default address is used.
2. Delivery Address: Delivery address set by the user when creating a Pickup + Delivery Consignment.

4) The newly created **Pickup** and **Delivery** consignments are linked to each other by a parent-child link, which can be accessed via the **Tree Structure** tab in either of the two consignments.

---

<a id="consignment-types-point-to-point-consignment"></a>
## Consignment Types - Point to Point Consignment

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-types-point-to-point-consignment_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Charging Behaviour
- Mobile App Behaviour
- Lodging errors
- Retrying failed uploads

### Purpose

Point-to-Point consignments contain both a Pickup and Delivery component. This allows a driver to collect a signature at both the collection and delivery points within a single Consignment.

Within the Web Application, Point-to-Point Consignments display with the Delivery Address of the consignment.

### Charging Behaviour

Point to Point Consignments are charged like Delivery Consignments, with the Rate Zone being selected based on the Delivery Address. If you wish to charge hourly or a flat rate for these jobs you will need to use an alternative charge scheme.

### Mobile App Behaviour

Within the App, Point to Point consignments display with both the Pickup and Delivery component.

1. The map view shows both the Pickup (1), and the Delivery (2), navigating to the job using Google Maps will load in the Pickup Address as the Pickup needs to be performed first. Similarly, when using the route optimization feature, the Pickup address will be used.
2. When recording a POD the driver must Record the Pickup POD First.
3. Recording information such as the signature and name is optional when performing the Pickup. The consignment is then updated to the status "In Transit (Pickup → Delivery)"
4. With the Pickup recorded, the job now turns orange to notify the driver he has the stock on board, it also shows he has completed the Pickup and not the Delivery (1/2)
5. Within the Consignment, the pickup job has now been marked completed with the green tick.
6. Only the Delivery address now shows on the map, and the Delivery address will be loaded into Navigation. Also, route optimization now uses the Delivery address for the consignment.
7. Like a Delivery Consignment, the Proof Of Delivery for the Delivery is required.
8. Once the Proof of Delivery for the Delivery is completed, the Point-to-Point consignment is removed from the job list on the driver's device (exactly like any other consignment). The consignment is then updated to the status "Delivered".

### Lodging errors

On lodging an error for a Point-to-Point consignment, the driver has to choose whether to lodge the error for the Pickup or Delivery part of the consignment. This information will then also be displayed on the error screen of the Web Application.

### Retrying failed uploads

If both the Proof of Pickup and Proof of Delivery have failed, the driver can either Retry All in the Outbox view or retry an individual upload by swiping right-to-left (iOS) or long-pressing (Android) the failed upload in the list. For Point-to-Point consignments, an individual retry on a Proof of Delivery is only allowed if the Proof of Pickup has already been sent through. This is to ensure the job is completed in the correct order.

---

<a id="consignment-types-return"></a>
## Consignment Types - Return

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-types-return_

A Return Consignment refers to a situation where goods were initially delivered but need to be collected and returned to the warehouse.

Unlike a standard Pickup, a Return Consignment typically occurs when there has been an error in the order, such as receiving incorrect stock, or when a product needs to be recalled. In such cases, a return is scheduled for the item to be collected and sent back.

---

<a id="consignment-types-warehouse-fulfilments"></a>
## Consignment Types - Warehouse Fulfilments

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-types-warehouse-fulfilments_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits
- Warehouse Fulfilments Workflows
- How to enable Warehouse Fulfilments

### Purpose

Warehouse Fulfilments are a Consignment Type available to CartonCloud accounts that have the WMS module enabled. While they require the WMS, they can also be used by customers who have both WMS and TMS enabled.  This type of Consignment enables the [Pack Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Pack-Screen) workflow.

### Benefits

- Enhanced packing workflow: Using the Pack Screen creates a Warehouse Fulfilment and the associated packages. To use the Pack Screen, Sale Orders must be set up to generate Warehouse fulfilments .
- Package-level data: Each package (Consignment Item) within a Warehouse Fulfilment contains dimensions and weight.
- Item-to-package tracking: CartonCloud records which item(s) were packed into which box, improving accuracy and traceability.
- Delivery tracking: Warehouse Fulfilments move through Shipped and Deliveed statuses, providing visibility after the order has left the warehouse.

### Warehouse Fulfilments Workflows

Enabling Warehouse Fulfilments allows for the [Pack Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Pack-Screen) workflow.

The statuses a Warehouse Fulfilment progresses through:

- Awaiting Sale Order Packing
- In Warehouse
- Shipped
- Delivered (Warehouse Fulfilment)

### How to enable Warehouse Fulfilments

Warehouse Fulfilments are enabled from the Organisation Settings and can be further controlled at the Customer level (if you wish to only enable it for certain customers).

**Organisation Settings**

*This will turn on Warehouse Fulfilments for all Customers.*

- Navigate to Organisation Settings, More > Organisation Settings .
- Click the Warehouse > General tab.
- Scroll down to the setting Automatically Generate a Consignment from a Sale Order.
- Select either:
  - **Yes, when Sale Order is Picked Only** - a Consignment (Warehouse Fulfilment) will generate when a Sale Order is picked. **Yes, on Sale Order Import or Pick Completion** - a Consignment (Warehouse Fulfilment) will generate when a Sale Order is imported or upon pick completion.
- Scroll down and click Save .

If you wish to turn this off for certain Customers, you will need to do so from the [Customer Settings - Warehouse Management (Sale Order Tab)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Customer-Settings-Warehouse-Management)

---

<a id="consignments"></a>
## Consignments

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignments_

### Table of Contents

- What is a Consignment
- Consignment List View (Consignments page)
- Configuring the Consignments list view
  - Filter
  - Adding and removing columns
  - Sorting columns
- Allocate Consignments
- Exporting Consignments
- Deleting a Consignment
- Approving Consignment

### What is a Consignment

Consignments in CartonCloud are Transport Jobs. There are a number of different [types of Consignments](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/fwG_Hw) you can create in CartonCloud. The type of Consignments you create and how you choose to manage your Consignments will depend upon your operational requirements and setup.

### Consignments List View (Consignments page)

On the Consignments page, you are able to view, [add](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/add-consignment), [filter](https://3883312.hs-sites.com/consignments), [sort](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Consignments#Consignments-sorting), [allocate](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Consignments#Consignments-allocate), [export](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Consignments#Consignments-export), [delete](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Consignments#Consignments-delete), [group](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-grouping), [approve](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Consignments#Consignments-approve), and [update the status](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Consignments#Consignments-status)of Consignments.

**To navigate to the Consignments page:**

- Type **Consignments** into the Search for anything bar OR from the **Transport** drop-down menu select **Consignments.**
- Once on the Consignments page, you will see the Consignments list view. This table view provides you with access to all Consignments that have been created in CartonCloud.

![consignments-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignments-0.png?width=670&height=186&name=consignments-0.png)

### Configuring the Consignments list view

You have the flexibility to configure the Consignment list view using the filter and sort functions to best meet your operational needs.

**Filter**

The Consignment list view contains a set of pre-defined filters. By selecting the appropriate filter tab you will find Consignments filtered to that specification.

You can select the **More** tab to find additional filter options.

![consignments-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignments-1.png?width=670&height=174&name=consignments-1.png)

You can also use the Filter tab and configure your own filters. Use the below definitions to choose what filters to apply to your Consignment list.

| **Filter** | **Definition** |
| --- | --- |
| Repeating Consignments | No : not show repeating Consignments Yes: show repeating Consignments  See [Repeating Consignments](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Repeating-Consignments) for more information. |
| Customer | The Customer of the Consignment. Select if you wish to show only Consignments for a particular Customer. |
| Delivery Status | The delivery status of the Consignments. Show Consignments for a particular delivery status. See [Consignment Statuses](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Consignment-Statuses) for definitions on each delivery status. |
| Approval | Approval status of the Consignment's POD. Show Consignments for a particular approval status. See [Approving Consignment Deliveries](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Approving-Consignment-Deliveries) for more information. |
| Date Added | The date the Consignment was added. Filter Consignments by the date they were added to CartonCloud. |
| Delivery Run Date | Filter Consignments by the Delivery Run date. |
| Delivery Run | Filter Consignments by the name of the Delivery Run the Consignment are allocated to. |
| Type | Filter Consignments by the Consignment type. See [Consignment Types](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Consignment-Types) for more information. |
| Driver | Filter Consignments by the driver they are allocated to. |
| Completed | Refers to if the Consignment's paper POD has been uploaded or not.  Not Delivered (Open): Not yet delivered, irrespective of Paper POD status. Delivered (Open): All Delivered/Collected, irrespective of Paper POD status. Delivered but incomplete (Open): Delivered/Collected, but awaiting Paper POD.  Incomplete (Open): Not yet delivered, and awaiting Paper POD. Complete (Closed): A completed Cancelled status with Paper POD Uploaded.  Successfully complete (Closed): Delivered / Collected with Paper POD uploaded. |
| Sale Order Ship Date | Filter Consignments by the associated Sale Order's ship date. |

From the **Filter**tab, you can set your own filters based on a range of different Consignment variables. Select the parameters you wish to filter your Consignments and then click **GO**. Your filter will continue to apply even when you go to other screens in the application.

**Adding and removing columns**

To customise the columns on the Consignment list:

- Select the cog icon in the top right corner of the page.

- A new pop-out window will appear where you can select and/or deselect the columns you wish to view.

Please note that there are 3 different addresses. Pick up, Delivery, and Dynamic. The Dynamic address fields dynamically change on certain consignment types to reflect the status of the consignment and consignment type. For a Pick up Consignment, it will show the pickup address. For a Point to Point consignment, it will show the pickup address until it has been picked up then it will show the delivery address.

**Sorting Columns**

To sort columns select the arrow icon next to the applicable column heading. By clicking it once the data will sort A-Z, twice it will sort Z-A and three times will reset the data to the default sort for that page.

### Allocate Consignments

For more information on allocating Consignments please see [Which way should I allocate my Consignments?](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/-ACYHw)

- Use the filter function to find the relevant Consignments.
- Select the Consignments you wish to allocate by selecting the tick box.
- Once all relevant Consignments are selected, click Move .
- From here you will be able to allocate Consignments to the appropriate Delivery Run.

For more information on allocating Consignment see [Which way should I allocate my Consignments?](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/which-way-should-i-allocate-my-consignments)

### Exporting Consignments

- Use the [filter](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Consignments#Consignments-filter) function to find the relevant Consignments.
- Select the Consignments you wish to allocate by selecting the tick box.
- Once all relevant Consignments are selected, click **Export Excel**.

![consignments-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignments-2.png?width=670&height=289&name=consignments-2.png)

### Deleting a Consignment

- Click on the individual Consignment you wish to delete.
- From the View Consignment page select **Delete**.

**When you can't delete a Consignment:**

- Once it has left the warehouse . To delete a Consignment with a status post 'In Warehouse' you will need to revert the status back to 'In Warehouse' by using the Reset Status button.
- If the Consignment contains manual charges. To remove the manual charges to be able to delete the Consignment, select **Automatically Calculate Income Charges**and under existing charges select the ones you wish to remove. Press **Save**.

### Approving Consignments

If your customer has created a Consignment through their login you will need to approve the Consignment to proceed with the job.

- Select the **More** tab.
- Select **All Not Approved** from the drop-down menu.
- Use the tick boxes to select the Consignments you wish to approve.
- Select the green **Approve** button at the top of the screen.

---

<a id="consignments-customer"></a>
## Consignments (Customer)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignments-customer_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to create a Consignment in CartonCloud

### Purpose

Consignments in CartonCloud are Transport jobs. You have the ability to add Consignments through your CartonCloud login or via a [Parser](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Parsers).

### How to create a Consignment in CartonCloud

When you create a Consignment in CartonCloud you have the option to add the Consignment to a [Manifest](https://help.cartoncloud.com/pages/viewpage.action?pageId=530055678). A Manifest is a list of all Consignments your CartonCloud account owner/transport company will be delivering on your behalf. Once you have created all of your Consignments you will then need to finalize the Manifest which makes the Manifest and the related Consignments available to your transport company for work. You also have the option to create individual Consignments that are not a Manifest and approve them individually. Each workflow is stepped out below

![consignments-customer-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignments-customer-0.png?width=455&height=240&name=consignments-customer-0.png)

**Creating a Consignment on a Manifest**

- Navigate to Transport > Consignments .
- Click +Add Consignment .
- Select the Consignment Type.
- Type in the customer references (this is how you will reference and identify the order)
- The Custom Fields that are set up for Consignments will appear here. Fill in the appropriate fields.
- Select if the Consignment needs to be picked up or not, next search for the pickup address and select the correct address. If the address is not listed, select +Add New Pickup Address .
- Search for and select the Delivery Address. If the address is not listed, select +Add New Address.
- Enter the Invoice Value if required.
- Click the drop down arrow against Advanced Options .
- Click Add to Existing Manifest or Create a new Manifest .

![consignments-customer-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignments-customer-2.png?width=670&height=131&name=consignments-customer-2.png)

- Fill in any other applicable fields if required.
- Click +Add Consignment Items .
- Enter the Consignment Items by selecting the item from the code drop-down menu.
- Enter the quantity.
- Select Save .
- Select the blue plus icon if you wish to add another Consignment Item.
- Select the Details tab, and you will see all relevant information for the Consignment.
- You will then need to Finalize the Manifest once all Consignments have been added to the Manifest and all changes and edits have been made to the associated Consignments.
- To Finalize the Manifest, navigate to the Manifests page by clicking Transport > Manifests .
- Select the Draft tab and you will see all Manifests that are not yet approved.
- Click View against the Manifest and click Finalize Manifest .

![consignments-customer-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignments-customer-4.png?width=670&height=95&name=consignments-customer-4.png)

![consignments-customer-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignments-customer-5.png?width=670&height=270&name=consignments-customer-5.png)

**Creating a Consignment not on a Manifest**

- Navigate to Transport > Consignments .
- Click +Add Consignment .
- Select the Consignment Type.
- Type in the customer references (this is how you will reference and identify the order)
- The Custom Fields that are set up for Consignments will appear here. Fill in the appropriate fields.
- Select if the Consignment needs to be picked up or not, next search for the pickup address and select the correct address. If the address is not listed, select +Add New Pickup Address .
- Search for and select the Delivery Address. If the address is not listed, select +Add New Address.

![consignments-customer-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignments-customer-6.png?width=670&height=221&name=consignments-customer-6.png)

- Enter the Invoice Value if required.
- Click the drop down arrow against Advanced Options .
- Click No Manifest.
- Fill in any other applicable fields that are required.
- Click +Add Consignment Items .
- Enter the Consignment Items by selecting the item from the code drop-down menu.
- Enter the quantity.
- Select Save .
- Select the blue plus icon if you wish to add another Consignment Item.
- Select the Details tab, and you will see all relevant information for the Consignment.

![consignments-customer-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignments-customer-7.png?width=670&height=125&name=consignments-customer-7.png)

- You will now need to approve the Consignment for it to be available to your CartonCloud account owner/transport company.
- To approve the Consignment, navigate back to the Consignments page. Click on the relevant Consignment.
- You will notice a red banner alerting you that the Consignment is still in a draft status and not yet approved. Click Approve Now .

![consignments-customer-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignments-customer-8.png?width=670&height=264&name=consignments-customer-8.png)

- The Consignment will now be available to your CartonCloud account owner/transport company.

---

<a id="creating-a-consignment"></a>
## Creating a Consignment

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/creating-a-consignment_

You are now able to create Consignments which will then be automatically allocated to a Delivery Run (if configured) and automatically priced using the Rate Card configured for the Customer.

When you go live you may have your Customers enter Consignments themselves, or Consignments may enter the system via an integration. But for now, let's manually enter a test Consignment into the system as a way to validate that allocation and pricing are behaving as expected.

We recommend making the details of the test Consignment similar to a delivery you complete on a regular basis (so it's pricing and delivery run is already familiar to you).

To create a Consignment navigate to the Add Consignment page. This is most easily done by selecting **+****Quick Add** then selecting **New Consignment**.

Now follow the video guide below for further instructions.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/BD201mXwuhw

Next Step: [Consignment Errors Introduction](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Consignment+Errors+Introduction)
