<a id="creating-automatic-pickup-consignments-for-manifests"></a>
## Creating Automatic Pickup Consignments for Manifests

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/creating-automatic-pickup-consignments-for-manifests_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Manifest workflow options
  - Option 1
  - Option 2
- How to enable CartonCloud to create automatic pickup consignments for manifests
- Charging for Manifest Pickup Consignments

### Purpose

To enable CartonCloud to automatically create a Pickup Consignment when a new Manifest is generated.

This is useful because you can:

- Schedule the pickup without the need for extra data entry (which can then be allocated to the Driver facilitating the collection).
- Charge accurately for pickups using the rate card assigned to the Customer.

### Manifest Workflow Options

**Option 1 - Pickup Consignment will NOT automatically be created for Manifests**

**Setting**: Automatically create Pickup Consignment is **No**

In this workflow, the Manifest is collected from the Customer's Warehouse and then delivered to the different Consignments final destinations. The Manifest is not created into a Pickup Consignment.

![creating-automatic-pickup-consignments-for-manifests-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-automatic-pickup-consignments-for-manifests-0.png?width=670&height=180&name=creating-automatic-pickup-consignments-for-manifests-0.png)

 **Option 2 - Pickup Consignment will automatically be created for Manifests**

**Setting**: Automatically create Pickup Consignment is **Yes**

In this workflow, once the Manifest is imported into CartonCloud it will automatically be created into a Pickup Consignment. The Consignment is picked up from the Customer's Warehouse and is brought back to your Warehouse/Depot to be sorted. It will then later be delivered to its final destination.

Note, if you do not wish to charge for a pickup you will need to create a Service Type (such as 'Manifest PU') that has no charge against it. For more information see the [charging](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Creating+Automatic+Pickup+Consignments+for+Manifests#CreatingAutomaticPickupConsignmentsforManifests-rates)section of this article.

![creating-automatic-pickup-consignments-for-manifests-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-automatic-pickup-consignments-for-manifests-1.png?width=670&height=179&name=creating-automatic-pickup-consignments-for-manifests-1.png)

### How to enable CartonCloud to create automatic Pickup consignments for Manifests

This setting is configured from the Customer Settings, meaning it will only apply to the Customer you set it up for.

**Prerequisites:**

- Ensure you have created and/or have a **Service Type** for the Pickup Consignment. See [Setting up Service Types](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-service-types)for more information.
- Ensure you have created and/or have a**Delivery Run** you wish the Pickup Consignments to be allocated to. See [Setting up Delivery Runs](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-delivery-runs) for more information.

**To enable the setting:**

- Navigate to Customer Settings (Contacts > Customers > Select applicable Customer > Edit).
- Select the **Transport Management** tab followed by the **Defaults** sub-tab.

![creating-automatic-pickup-consignments-for-manifests-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-automatic-pickup-consignments-for-manifests-2.png?width=670&height=435&name=creating-automatic-pickup-consignments-for-manifests-2.png)

- Set **Manifest Pickup up by Default** to Yes.
- Select the **Default Pickup Address**(this is a required field and only one Pickup Address per customer).
- Change **Automatically create pickup consignment**to **Yes**.
- If you do not want the Manifest Pickup Consignment to update to "Delivered to Warehouse" when Manifest is marked "In Warehouse", untick the box.
- Select the **Default Service Type** you wish to use for the Pickup Consignments.
- Select the **Delivery Run**you wish the Pickup Consignments to be allocated to (this is a required field).
- Select if you wish to Sum the Consignment fields (this will aggregate Consignment Item lines when they match). For example, it will total the number of pallets or cartons being collected.
- Select **Save**.

![creating-automatic-pickup-consignments-for-manifests-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-automatic-pickup-consignments-for-manifests-3.png?width=670&height=461&name=creating-automatic-pickup-consignments-for-manifests-3.png)

### Charging for Manifest Pickup Consignments

To charge a specific rate for a Manifest Pickup Consignment:

**Option 1: Within the Customer's Rate Card under the Details tab**

- Navigate to the relevant Rate Card (by typing in **Rate Card** in the Search for anything bar).
- Select **Edit**.
- Within the **Manifest Charge Scheme** box, type in the **Manifest Pickup Charge** and **Manifest Minimum Charge**(if applicable).

Please note, this charge is for the Manifest, not the Pickup Consignment. This means that the fee will be applied on top of the Pickup Consignment charge (if there is a Pickup Consignment associated with the Manifest and a fee configured for a Pickup Consignment).

**Option 2: Within the Customer's Rate Card under the Transport Rates tab**

- Navigate to the relevant Rate Card (by typing in **Rate Card** in the Search for anything bar).
- Select the **Transport Rates** tab.
- Create a Transport Rate with the applicable Transport Zones and Service Type. See [Setting up Transport Rates](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/creating-transport-rates) for more information on how to configure a Transport Rate.

**NOT charging for Manifest Pickup Consignments**

If you do not wish to charge for a Manifest Pickup Consignment:

- Create a Service Type for a no charge Pickup Consignment (for example, Manifest PU). See [Setting up Service Types](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-service-types) for information on how to create a new Service Type.
- Create a Transport Rate with the applicable Transport Zones (you can choose All if you wish the no charge to apply to all Pickup Consignments with that Service Type) and the Manifest Pickup Consignment Service Type.
- Select **Yes** from the drop-down menu of **No Charge**.
- Select **No Charge** as the **Fee Category** from the drop-down menu.

![creating-automatic-pickup-consignments-for-manifests-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-automatic-pickup-consignments-for-manifests-4.png?width=643&height=435&name=creating-automatic-pickup-consignments-for-manifests-4.png)

**Pickup Consignment's Product Type**

The automatically generated pickup consignment will have its product type determined by reviewing the product type of each Consignment on the manifest and picking the product type with the lowest priority number i.e. 1 is the lowest.

In the instance where there are multiple product types on the manifest that are all set to the same priority, the product type with the lowest ID will be used.

---

<a id="documents"></a>
## Documents

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/documents_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits
- Using the documents page
- Adding documents

### Purpose

Documents stores all documents associated with Consignments and Sale Orders. The type of documents includes:

- Consignments Customer Invoices
- Sale Order Customer Invoices
- ​​​​​​​Consignment Proof of Deliveries

### ​​​​​​​ Benefits

- Producing a [Superimposed Proof Of Delivery](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Superimposed+Proof+Of+Delivery) on the Consignment Invoice
- Automated Document Management. Consignment Invoices can be automatically imported and allocated, then printed at the time of allocation and delivered with the goods.
- ​​​​​​​Printed with QR Code Overlay for Invoices for use with Driver Scan Allocation

### ​​​​​​​
Using the documents page

![documents-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/documents-0.png?width=670&height=133&name=documents-0.png)

- **Filter:** You can filter the documents by Customer, Date Added, Associated To, Retyring, Status and Type.
- **All**: lists all Documents.
- **Unassigned:**lists Documents that are not assigned to a Consignment. For more information, click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/2wG_Hw).
- **Retrying**: Consignment Invoices that have been uploaded before the Consignment. To prevent the Invoices from immediately just going to "Unassigned", they're put into a "Retrying" status while they wait for the associated Consignment to arrive. For more information, click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/-QG_Hw).
- Unapproved Consignment Deliveries: POD's that have not yet been approved. For more information, click here .

### Adding documents

​​**Documents can either be added:**

- Directly through the Documents page.
- Added from the Consignment or Sale Order.
- Uploaded via Parser.

**Adding Documents directly through the Documents page:**

- Click the **+Add button** in the top left corner.

![documents-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/documents-1.png?width=670&height=115&name=documents-1.png)

- Choose the file to upload.
- Select the **File Type** from the drop-down menu (if assigning the file to a Consignment).
- Select if you are linking the file to a Consignment or Sale Order.
- Search for the Consignment or Sale Order reference.
- Click **Upload**.

![documents-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/documents-2.png?width=670&height=262&name=documents-2.png)

**Adding directly through the Sale Order or Consignment**

- Navigate to the Sale Order or Consignment.
- Select the Customer Invoices tab.
- Click the **+Add Invoice** button.

![documents-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/documents-3.png?width=670&height=125&name=documents-3.png)

**Drag and drop for Consignments**

This option only works when uploading documents to a Consignment

- Navigate to the relevant Consignment.
- Drag the file from your desktop (or where it is saved) and drop it onto the screen (you don't need to be on the Customer Invoices tab for this drag and drop to work).
- Click **Done**.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/3SmtxexQQXk

Automated Duplicate Deletion

CartonCloud compares the file to the existing documents associated with that Consignment or Sale Order when a new document is assigned to a Consignment. If a duplicate is found (the newly added file is exactly the same as a file already associated with the Consignment/Sale Order), the new file is deleted rather than assigned.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/9e67JwjKG0g

---

<a id="downloading-consignment-invoices-and-consignment-notes-in-bulk"></a>
## Downloading Consignment Invoices and Consignment Notes in Bulk

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/downloading-consignment-invoices-and-consignment-notes-in-bulk_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Downloading for multiple run sheets
- Downloading from an individual run sheet

### Purpose

This feature allows CartonCloud users to download multiple Consignment Invoices and printable paper consignment notes for a CartonCloud Consignment. This is perfect if your printing 'just-in-time' for the driver to leave.

When downloading both Invoices and Connotes in one-click, only Connotes for jobs which **don't** have an Invoice will be included in the downloaded file.

You can also specify how many copies of Invoices and Connotes you want to be printed, this is perfect if you need multiple copies to give to the drivers for some clients, and not others.

### Downloading for multiple Run Sheets

On the Run Sheets page, select the Run Sheets whose Consignment Invoices are to be downloaded and click the **Export** button at the bottom left corner of the screen. A list of options will appear, from which you can select:

- **Download Consignment Invoices -**This will download the invoices attached to consignments within the selected Run Sheets. In the case there are no Invoices attached to the consignments, a message will be displayed on the same page saying "*None of the consignments contain Invoices*".
- Download Consignment Connotes - This will download the Connotes for all the consignments in the selected Run Sheets.
- ​​​​​​​ Download Consignment Invoices and Connotes - This will download invoices attached to consignments in the selected run sheets. For the ones that don't have any invoices, Connotes (Consignment Notes) will be download.

### Downloading from an individual run sheet​​​​

- From the Run Sheets page, click on the Run Sheet whose Consignment Invoices are to be downloaded.
- A page will open listing the details of that Run Sheet.
- At the bottom of the page click the Download button.
- A menu will appear listing the options for download.
- Click on Consignment Invoices .
- This will download the Consignment Invoices attached to the Consignments in that Run Sheet. In the case that there are no Invoices attached to the Consignments, a message will be displayed on the same page saying " None of the consignments contain Invoices ".
- A page will open, listing all the consignments for the tenant. Select the Consignments whose Invoices are to be downloaded.
- Scroll to the bottom of the page and click Download Invoices .
- This will download the invoices attached to the consignments.  In the case that there are no Invoices attached to the Consignments, a message will be displayed on the same page saying " None of the consignments contain Invoices ".

Drivers can be given a summary of their COD Consignments for the day. This is useful if the Driver has a large number of Consignments that require COD.

<a id="finding-and-downloading-a-pod"></a>
## Finding and Downloading a POD

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/finding-and-downloading-a-pod_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to download a POD

### Purpose

With CartonCloud, you can download a POD any time you like online.

### How to download a POD

- To begin, click on Transport in the main menu followed by Consignments in the drop-down menu, then use the Search for a Consignment bar to start typing in your reference number.
- You can scroll up and down through the list and once you have found the consignment you want, simply click on it.
- Now on the View Consignment page, select Download POD
- Then, on the page that loads, click the Download POD button.
- The POD will then download to your PC

**Want to receive PODs via Email when they’re delivered?**

You can receive an email notification for a POD (Proof of Delivery) as soon as a consignment is marked "Delivered." To set this up, you need to enable POD email notifications in your customer’s settings. Here’s how:

- Go to Contacts > Customers and select the relevant customer.
- Edit the customer, then navigate to the Email Notifications settings.
- Enable the option to send POD emails upon consignment delivery.
- Enter the email address(es) where you want the POD notifications sent.

This will ensure an automated email with the POD is sent when the consignment is delivered.

<a id="handling-unassigned-a2ic-consignments"></a>
## Handling Unassigned A2IC Consignments

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/handling-unassigned-a2ic-consignments_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Assigning unassigned A2IC consignments

### Purpose

Sometimes when importing a Manifest, for example, CartonCloud is unable to work out which **Customer** needs to be charged for the Consignment. When this occurs the Consignment is marked as "**Unassigned A2IC**". Specifically, a Consignment is marked as unassigned when CartonCloud fails to find a matching **Address To Invoice Customer Mapping (A2IC Mapping)** for the delivery address provided with the Consignment. When a Consignment is marked as Unassigned, it needs to be manually resolved to a Charge Customer. CartonCloud handles this using **Receiver Pays Freight and Address To Invoice Customer (A2IC) Mapping**. This functionality allows you to associate the Delivery Address of a given Consignment (**Address**) to a Customer to Charge (**Invoice Customer**).

For example, assume you have stock which is going from one of your customers, *Joe's Fruit*, to a store in regional New South Wales, *IGA Kurrajong* and the store (the receiver) is paying for the freight. One way you can do this is by specifying the "**Customer**" as *IGA Kurrajong*, but this can become confusing if you're looking at a job because you refer to it as "the stock from Joe's Fruit". To avoid this confusion, **Receiver Pays Freight and A2IC mapping** is used, which allows you to leave the **Customer** as *Joe's Fruit*, but specify that you want the job charged to *IGA Kurrajong*.

### Assigning Unassigned A2IC Consignments

When the Organisation Settings **Enable Receiver Pays Freight And A2IC****Mappings** is enabled, a new tab will appear in Consignments called **Unassigned A2IC Consignments**. This tab contains Consignments that have been marked as unassigned when parsed from a Manifest import. To assign Consignments that appear in this tab with A2IC Mapping, click on the green **Begin Assigning** button that appears at the bottom of the tab:

![handling-unassigned-a2ic-consignments-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/handling-unassigned-a2ic-consignments-0.png?width=670&height=282&name=handling-unassigned-a2ic-consignments-0.png)
Clicking on the **Begin Assigning** button will take you to the assign screen:

![handling-unassigned-a2ic-consignments-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/handling-unassigned-a2ic-consignments-1.png?width=670&height=188&name=handling-unassigned-a2ic-consignments-1.png)
Clicking on the **Assign** button in this screen will assign the selected **Charge Customer** as the **Invoice Customer** for the given **Address** and redirect back to the Consignments listing table. Clicking on the **Assign & Process Next Unassigned** will assign the selected **Charge Customer** as the **Invoice Customer** for the given **Address** and will redirect to the next **Unassigned Consignment**. Clicking on the **Skip** button will skip the current **Unassigned Consignment** and go to the next **Unassigned Consignment**.

---

<a id="how-to-download-proof-of-deliveries-pod-in-bulk-download-including-ftp"></a>
## How to download Proof Of Deliveries in Bulk

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-download-proof-of-deliveries-pod-in-bulk-download-including-ftp_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- FTP POD Download

### Purpose

You can export bulk Proof Of Deliveries from either an Invoice or Manifest. Due to the processing time required to generate a bulk proof of delivery (POD), the system will notify you when your bulk export is ready for download through the notifications bell.

Depending on the number of POD's you’re trying to download, the file could take anywhere from 5 minutes to several hours to export, however you’ll be notified instantly when the files are available.

Once generated, files are only available for download for 24 hours. After this time they’re deleted and will need to be re-downloaded again.

### FTP POD Download

Another option for customers to access POD's is via the FTP Download option. This will send a copy of POD's as they are completed to the nominated FTP Server where Customers can access them from that point. To configure this select**Contacts** in the main menu followed by **Customers** in the drop-down menu then find the correct customer and use Edit to bring up the edit screen where you will find the FTP tab option.

Now tick the box for the PODs or Sale Order Receipts as appropriate for what you want to send. Then select **Save** and navigate to this screen again, now select **Add FTP Server**. Complete with the details as noted in this screen based upon the FTP settings that the customer wants the files to be sent to.

**Providing a directory is not necessarily required and is up to the receiving party to advise where they would like POD's to go.**

The **Name** field is for you to simply name this FTP Server for ease of use, this is not to do with the FTP Server itself.

Then select **Save** when ready and it will now be active and send new PODs to this FTP Server.

---

<a id="how-to-rearrange-and-set-a-default-service-type"></a>
## How to rearrange and set a default Service Type

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-rearrange-and-set-a-default-service-type_

When manually entering consignments it is possible to make the task slightly easier by rearranging your service types from most used to least used.

Alternatively, if you regularly use the same service type it can be set as the default, removing the need to select it each time.

- To navigate to the Custom Fields page, type Custom Fields into the Search for anything bar.
- Select the Consignment Data tab
- Select the pencil icon button next to the "Service" custom field to be able to edit it
- You can now rearrange the drop-down fields as required

- To set a default service type, use the Default field drop-down to select which service should be populated by default when a consignment is created.
- Once the fields have been re-arranged select Save .

The order or default value you have selected will now be reflected in the [Add Consignment](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Add+Consignment)page.

---

<a id="importing-consignments"></a>
## Importing Consignments

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/importing-consignments_

### Table of Contents

- How to import Consignments
- Unsuccessful import errors
- Successful import
- What if 'allow multiple consignments to have the same reference' is turned on?
- Triggering notifications with the Parser

### How to import Consignments

From the consignments page, it's possible to import Consignments if you have a [Consignment with Items Parser](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/List+of+Parsers)set up.

To import consignments:

- Navigate to the Consignments page by typing Consignments into the Search for anything bar.
- Select the More Button, followed by Import Consignments .

![importing-consignments-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/importing-consignments-0.png?width=670&height=150&name=importing-consignments-0.png)

- A box will appear on the page, allowing you to select the Parser you wish to use to read the file in and choose the file to be read.
- If you have multiple types of Consignment Item Parsers set up, for example, you have multiple formats provided by your Customers which need to be parsed, then select the appropriate Parser for the file you will be parsing.
- Select Choose File and find the file you wish to Parse.
- Once you have selected the file, click Import .

### Unsuccessful Import Errors

![importing-consignments-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/importing-consignments-1.png?width=670&height=125&name=importing-consignments-1.png)

I

f

the upload is unsuccessful a list of error messages will display on the page providing you with information on what must be amended for the import to run successfully.

In the case shown above the system is telling us that it could not match a Customer record with the Customer name provided in the CSV file. This could be resolved by checking the Customer's actual name in CartonCloud by navigating to **Contacts** then **Customers** and then amending the typo in the CSV file before reuploading.

If you encounter an error you can easily resolve it by:

- Checking the error message provided
- Amending any typos in the CSV file so fields match exactly what is entered in CartonCloud (for example a Driver's name)
- Reuploading the amended CSV file by selecting Upload another file .

### Successful Import

If the file is successfully imported the following page will provide a breakdown of the consignments that were created. These results are broken down into separate customers. In the example below two consignments were created using 4 lines in the CSV file (which can be identified by the fact that each consignment has 2 Consignment Item lines each, and as they were for the same customer going to the same place these were aggregated into a single consignment).

![importing-consignments-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/importing-consignments-2.png?width=670&height=324&name=importing-consignments-2.png)

### What if "Allow multiple consignments to have the same reference" is turned on?

If this Customer level setting is turned on then the Parser will still attempt to aggregate lines into a single consignment with the same Customer reference and customer. However, if it fails because for example, if the two CSV lines have different manifest references, then multiple separate consignments will be created accordingly.

### Triggering Notifications with the Parser

The Consignment Item Import Parser will not trigger notifications for newly created Consignments. This is due to its capability to create consignments for multiple customers at a time which would make it possible for customers to see each other's information in the notification.

---

<a id="make-consignments-auto-update-to-in-transit-warehouse-to-delivery"></a>
## Make Consignments Auto Update to In Transit (Warehouse to Delivery)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/make-consignments-auto-update-to-in-transit-warehouse-to-delivery_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to enable auto in transit

### Purpose

If you do not wish to manually update the Consignment status of 'In Transit' you can enable the Auto in Transit feature. Once enabled, CartonCloud will automatically update all Consignments with the status of 'In Warehouse' that are scheduled for delivery that same day to 'In Transit (Warehouse - > Delivery) at the pre-defined time each day you set when enabling the setting.

For the Consignment status to be automatically updated it must meet the below criteria:

- Currently have the status of 'In Warehouse".
- Be allocated to a Delivery Run.
- Be scheduled for delivery either for that day or earlier.
- Not be a Pickup or Multi-leg Consignment Type.

### How to enable auto in transit

- Navigate to Organisation Settings by typing in Organisation Settings in the Search for anything bar.
- Select the Transport tab and scroll down to the heading Other Transport Settings .
- Tick the first check box which reads Enable Auto In Transit .
- Once ticket a box will appear for you to fill in with the time you wish the update to be triggered.

![make-consignments-auto-update-to-in-transit-warehouse-to-delivery-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/make-consignments-auto-update-to-in-transit-warehouse-to-delivery-0.png?width=670&height=239&name=make-consignments-auto-update-to-in-transit-warehouse-to-delivery-0.png)

<a id="making-the-dimensions-of-a-consignment-required"></a>
## Making the dimensions of a Consignment required

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/making-the-dimensions-of-a-consignment-required_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Modifying the custom fields
- How the changes will affect booking a consignment

### Purpose

By default when a consignment is entered into CartonCloud the Length, Width and Height of the Consignment's items are optional fields to be recorded.

However, some operations which rely on the dimensions for charging or allocating consignments may wish to make it required for all consignments to be entered with Length, Width and Height provided for all items.

This article will show you how to enforce dimensions to be required when a Consignment item is added to a Consignment.

### Modifying the custom fields

- To begin, type and select "Custom Fields" in Search for Anything! to navigate to the page.
- Once on the Custom Fields page, select the Consignment Item tab.

![making-the-dimensions-of-a-consignment-required-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/making-the-dimensions-of-a-consignment-required-0.png?width=670&height=199&name=making-the-dimensions-of-a-consignment-required-0.png)

Then for each of the dimension fields named Length, Width, and Height that you wish to set as required complete the following:

- Select the pencil button to edit the Custom Field.
- Enable the required setting within that custom field.

![making-the-dimensions-of-a-consignment-required-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/making-the-dimensions-of-a-consignment-required-1.png?width=408&height=380&name=making-the-dimensions-of-a-consignment-required-1.png)

- Select Save

### How the changes will affect booking a Consignment

- Now that the dimension fields are set as required if a user attempts to enter a Consignment item into a Consignment they will not be able to save the item line until the Length, Width and Height fields are populated.
- An example of the warning that will be displayed is shown below.

![making-the-dimensions-of-a-consignment-required-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/making-the-dimensions-of-a-consignment-required-2.png?width=670&height=215&name=making-the-dimensions-of-a-consignment-required-2.png)

---

<a id="making-the-invoice-value-of-a-consignment-required-upon-creation"></a>
## Making the Invoice value of a Consignment required upon creation

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/making-the-invoice-value-of-a-consignment-required-upon-creation_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- To enable this setting for a particular customer

### Purpose

An invoice value can be recorded on a Consignment to reflect the value of the freight moving on it. Optionally this can then be used for calculating the charges for that delivery (by charging a percentage of the Invoice). It can also be used within the Consignment Report as a field.

This field by default is not required, so it is at the discretion of the Customer creating the consignment as to whether this field is populated or not, this includes consignments being keyed in manually and those created by Parsers.

If you want this field to be required for a Consignment on creation, then there is a that can be enabled to enforce this. Please note as it is a Customer setting it will only be applied to the Customers you select.

### To enable this setting for a particular customer

- Select Contacts in the main menu, then select Customers from the drop-down menu.
- Select the Customer you wish to force to enter an Invoice value.
- Once on the View Customer page, select Edit .
- Select the Invoice tab.
- Scroll to the bottom of the Invoice tab until to you find the option Invoice Value Required (When creating Consignments)
- Check the box to enable this setting.
- Finally, select Save .
- Now that the setting is enabled whenever a Consignment is created for this Customer an Invoice Value greater than 0 must be entered before the Consignment can be saved.

The dot on the map is the Consignment. You can click this for more information. This dot will be larger depending on the number of deliveries going to that location.

<a id="moving-a-consignment-s-date-or-run"></a>
## Moving a Consignment's Date or Run

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/moving-a-consignment-s-date-or-run_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Selecting consignments to move
  - View consignment page
  - View delivery run page
  - View run sheet page
  - Move page

### Purpose

If you want to move a consignment to a different run, change the date that the consignment is scheduled to be delivered, or change which driver is doing a delivery, you can do it from multiple places:

1. From the View Consignment Page.
2. From the View Delivery Run Page.
3. From the View Run Sheet Page.

### Selecting consignments to move

#### **View Consignment Page**

- On the top Menu click:
- Transport --> Consignments --> (then find the Consignment you want to move) --> scroll down the page a little and you'll see the Move button.

![moving-a-consignment-s-date-or-run-0-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/moving-a-consignment-s-date-or-run-0-1.png?width=670&height=264&name=moving-a-consignment-s-date-or-run-0-1.png)

- The Move button is a little way down the View Consignment Page.

#### **View Delivery Run Page**

- On the top Menu click:
- Transport --> Delivery Runs --> (then find the Delivery Run you want to move):

![moving-a-consignment-s-date-or-run-1-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/moving-a-consignment-s-date-or-run-1-1.png?width=493&height=327&name=moving-a-consignment-s-date-or-run-1-1.png)

- Select the Consignment(s) you want to move and then click the Move button.

#### **View Run Sheet Page**

- On the top Menu click:
- Transport --> Run Sheets --> (then find the Run Sheet you want)--> Click on the 'Consignments' sub menu.

![moving-a-consignment-s-date-or-run-2-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/moving-a-consignment-s-date-or-run-2-1.png?width=492&height=249&name=moving-a-consignment-s-date-or-run-2-1.png)

- Select the Consignment(s) you want to move and then click the Move button.

#### **Move Page**

- Note that at the top of the page there are a number of tabs which allow you to switch between allocating, changing dates and switching runs.

![moving-a-consignment-s-date-or-run-3-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/moving-a-consignment-s-date-or-run-3-1.png?width=553&height=308&name=moving-a-consignment-s-date-or-run-3-1.png)

<a id="optimising-the-delivery-order-of-consignments"></a>
## Optimising the delivery order of Consignments

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/optimising-the-delivery-order-of-consignments_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Automatically ordering all Consignments on a Driver
- Reordering Consignments Manually for a Driver
- Reordering Consignments Manually on a Run Sheet

### Purpose

CartonCloud includes optimisation features to assist you in ordering your drivers deliveries. This article will introduce you to these features.

The following features will only be effective if the driver leaves consignment sort on the mobile app as "Default". If a driver elects to sort by proximity the below settings will not affect the driver's view of consignment order.

### Automatically ordering all Consignments on a Driver

Using this method you can automatically optimise the delivery order of consignments on a driver. However, it should be noted that this will reorder ALL consignments allocated to the driver, even if they are spread over multiple run sheets (for example a morning run and afternoon run). For this reason, you should carefully consider if this optimisation best suits your operation.

- To begin, select Contacts in the main menu, followed by Drivers in the drop-down menu. Then, on the Driver's page, select the driver that you wish to optimise deliveries for.
- Now, on the View Driver page, select the Map tab.
- On this page, you are able to see all consignments allocated to the driver for the current day and the current delivery order. You can also change the date to see future deliveries using the Delivery Date filter at the top right.
- From here, you should select a Starting Point and Ending Point if desired. These points can either be deliveries allocated to the driver (Select Consignment) or they can be any address that you set (by changing the type to Address, then Searching for or adding a new Address). A good example of when you might want to use an address as the start and end points would be setting the collection depot as the Start Point, and the driver's home address as the endpoint, therefore allowing them to finish there run closest to home and preserve fuel & time (in the case he drives his vehicle home).
- In the example above we have a delivery run to supermarkets around the Gold Coast starting from the CartonCloud office in Burleigh Heads, you will notice that initially the delivery order takes the driver on an inefficient route, and requires them to double back.
- After optimising the consignments, remembering to Save Consignment Order , the run is now in the most efficient delivery order possible based on geographical location Note: There is no direct road between points 3 & 5 due to waterways.

### Reordering Consignments Manually for a Driver

If you want to manually change the order of deliveries on a driver yourself (perhaps due to Express service levels) this can be done by dragging the addresses into the desired order, then selecting

Save Consignment Order

, as shown in the animation below.

![optimising-the-delivery-order-of-consignments-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/optimising-the-delivery-order-of-consignments-0.png?width=287&height=533&name=optimising-the-delivery-order-of-consignments-0.png)

### Reordering Consignments Manually on a Run Sheet

- The same process of manually reordering consignments as shown in the animation above can be used on a Run Sheet (in the case that a driver is allocated multiple Run Sheets).
- To reorder consignments per Run Sheet, select Transport in the main menu, followed by Run Sheets in the drop-down menu.
- Then, select the Run Sheet you wish to change the delivery order on.
- Now on the View Run sheet page select the Map tab.
- You can now reorder the consignments by dragging them into the preferred order. Once completed, select Save Consignment Order for the changes to take effect.

Next Step: [Using the Mobile App within the TMS](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Using+the+Mobile+app+within+the+TMS)

---

<a id="photograph-invoices-to-create-pods"></a>
## Photograph Invoices to Create PODs

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/photograph-invoices-to-create-pods_

If you're just getting set up with CartonCloud and don't have everything manifested by your Customers, it is still possible for the drivers to get electronic PODs in the field.

Drivers can photograph signed invoices using their mobile and these are lodged in the CartonCloud system as PODs which you then allocate to a consignment.

On the App, the driver simply presses the Camera button, takes a photo and then presses 'Confirm' to have it sent to CartonCloud.

![photograph-invoices-to-create-pods-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photograph-invoices-to-create-pods-0.png?width=567&height=324&name=photograph-invoices-to-create-pods-0.png)
Within CartonCloud you can see when these Invoice Photos have been sent in from the dashboard by looking at
"Unassigned Consignment Invoices / PODs".

![photograph-invoices-to-create-pods-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photograph-invoices-to-create-pods-1.png?width=489&height=260&name=photograph-invoices-to-create-pods-1.png)
Simply click the number (ie: 18), and this will take you straight to the list of Unassigned Consignment Invoices.
From there, simply click Assign next to one of the Proof of Deliveries you want.

![photograph-invoices-to-create-pods-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photograph-invoices-to-create-pods-2.png?width=615&height=56&name=photograph-invoices-to-create-pods-2.png)

On the screen, simply click the Download button to download the photo taken by the driver.

From there, you can search for an existing Consignment, or if it doesn't already exist, click 'Add New Consignment'.

![photograph-invoices-to-create-pods-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/photograph-invoices-to-create-pods-3.png?width=670&height=400&name=photograph-invoices-to-create-pods-3.png)

Once the consignment has been added you'll be able to choose it from the box, and then click either "Save" or "Save and Process Next Unassigned" (if you have more to process).

The photograph will be saved as the POD

---

<a id="proof-of-delivery-pod-email-notifications-for-the-delivery-addresss-email"></a>
## Proof of Delivery (POD) Email Notifications (for the delivery address's email)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/proof-of-delivery-pod-email-notifications-for-the-delivery-addresss-email_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Use Cases
- Configuration Overview
- How to enable POD Email Notifications for the delivery address's email
  - At the Customer Level
  - At the Organisation Level

### Purpose

Proof of Delivery (POD) email notifications automatically send confirmation of a completed delivery to the delivery address email on a consignment. This ensures recipients receive delivery confirmation without manual intervention.

### Use Cases

- Provide delivery confirmation directly to the recipient
- Reduce manual communication after delivery
- Improve customer transparency and service experience

### Configuration Overview

POD email notifications are controlled at both the **Customer** and **Organisation** level.

- The Customer setting overrides the Organisation setting
- The delivery address against the Consignment must have an email address for the POD email notification to be sent.

### How to enable POD Email Notifications for the delivery address's email

#### At the Customer Level

- Navigate to the Customer Settings by selecting Contacts > Customers.
- Select the relevant Customer.
- Click Edit.
- Select the Email > Notifications tab.
- Scroll down to Proof of Delivery Notification Configuration and enable Send Proof of Delivery Notification Email .
- Click Save .

#### At the Organisation Level

- Navigate to Organisation Settings by selecting More > Organisation Settings .
- Select the Email tab and scroll down to Disable Proof Of Delivery Notification For Delivery Address's Email and set it to No .

---

<a id="qr-code-overlay-for-consignment-invoices"></a>
## QR Code Overlay for Consignment Invoices

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/qr-code-overlay-for-consignment-invoices_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Use cases
- How QR code overlay works
- Configuring QR code overlay for invoices
- QR code positioning tool

### Purpose

The QR Code overlay feature makes it possible to superimpose a QR code on top of Consignment Customer Invoices.

### Use cases

This feature can be used in conjunction with [Driver Scan Allocation](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Scan-Allocation) to allow transport operators to allocate work to a driver by simply scanning the QR code on the invoice.

- Alternatively,  the QR code can also be used to match signed consignment notes automatically, so the paperwork can be signed, bought back, and then automatically allocated to the correct Consignment. This is particularly useful when giving out deliveries to onforwarders who are not able to use the CartonCloud mobile app, but you still need to capture a POD for the delivery. See Using QR Codes to automatically attach a POD to a Consignment for more information.

If you need assistance with setting up the QR Code Overlay, please reach out to our Service Desk by lodging a case at [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket) .

### How QR Code Overlay Works

The QR Code overlay is performed when the Consignment Invoice file is assigned to the Consignment. This step **modifies the original file** to include the QR code. This means that the original file (without the QR Code) no longer exists within CartonCloud.

Because the QR Code Overlay is set up from the Customer level, you can modify where the QR Code will be placed for each Customer. However, you can only select one document on which to model the QR Code for each Customer.

When the QR Code Overlay feature is enabled, it only affects new Consignment Customer Invoices. Previously existing Consignment Customer Invoices will not be affected.

Points to consider

The QR code is overlaid as the Consignment Customer Invoice is allocated to a Consignment within CartonCloud. The original (non-overlaid) file is then deleted.
This results in the following potential issues:

1. If the position of the QR overlay gets changed, the previous overlay will still show on the invoice.
2. If the user disables this feature, the Invoices already uploaded will have the QR code, so they will have to be re-uploaded.

### Configuring QR Code Overlay for Invoices

The QR Code Overlay is set up at the Customer level. This means each Customer can have their own Consignment Customer Invoice template and the QR code position can be different for each Customer and their invoice.

**To set up the QR Code Overlay:**

- Navigate to the Customer Settings, Contacts > Customers >click E dit against the relevant Customer.
- Select Transport Management > Defaults tab.

![qr-code-overlay-for-consignment-invoices-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/qr-code-overlay-for-consignment-invoices-0.png?width=670&height=134&name=qr-code-overlay-for-consignment-invoices-0.png)

- Scroll down to Advanced and tick Enable Overlaying of QR on Customer Invoices. This will occur on Invoice generation .

![qr-code-overlay-for-consignment-invoices-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/qr-code-overlay-for-consignment-invoices-1.png?width=670&height=224&name=qr-code-overlay-for-consignment-invoices-1.png)

- You will now need to select an Invoice to be the template for choosing the position of the overlay. You can either select an existing recent invoice, or a new PDF file can be uploaded.
- Once you have selected the file, it will appear on the page inside the QR Code positioning tool.
- Use the QR Code positioning tool (move the red box) to place the QR Code in the desired location on the document and in the desired size.

![qr-code-overlay-for-consignment-invoices-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/qr-code-overlay-for-consignment-invoices-2.png?width=670&height=330&name=qr-code-overlay-for-consignment-invoices-2.png)

- Scroll to the bottom of the page and click Save .

### QR Code Positioning Tool

The QR Code positioning tool supports the following.

| Function | Description |
| --- | --- |
| QR Code Placement | Dragging and dropping the red QR code square will place it in that location for all future documents using the overlay feature. |
| QR Code Resizing | Dragging from the bottom right corner of the red QR code square allows it to be resized as required. |
| Page Rotation | If the sample page has been uploaded in the wrong orientation, it can be rotated as required. |
| On Pages | In the scenario where a Customer Consignment invoice is multiple pages, this allows the user to select which page/s the QR code will be overlaid on. |
| Rotation | Not required as QR codes are omnidirectional. |

![qr-code-overlay-for-consignment-invoices-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/qr-code-overlay-for-consignment-invoices-3.png?width=399&height=515&name=qr-code-overlay-for-consignment-invoices-3.png)

---

<a id="repeating-consignments"></a>
## Repeating Consignments

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/repeating-consignments_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Creating a repeating consignment
- Extra options available for repeating consignments
  - Placeholders
  - Manifest creation
  - Consignment items on repeating consignments
  - Editing or testing a repeating consignment
  - Scheduling repeating consignments based on the day of week

### Purpose

The Repeating Consignments feature allows you to configure Consignments which recur on a daily, weekly or monthly basis.

This is useful for recurring orders or jobs that you don't want to have to key in every time.

Repeating Consignments are created shortly after the time they are set to be created. This process is triggered every 5 minutes.

### Creating a repeating consignment

Note, when creating a repeating consignment you must either add the Consignment to an existing Manifest or create a new Manifest. You can not create a Repeating Consignment unless it is on a Manifest.

To begin, navigate to the Consignments page by selecting **Transport** in the main menu, followed by **Consignments** in the drop-down menu.

Now on the Consignments page, select the drop-down arrow on the **+Add** button, followed by **Repeating Consignment**.

At the top of the page, specify how often the Consignment will repeat, as well as it's Beginning and End Dates.

If you do not wish for it to End until further notice, leave the End Date field blank.

You will now need to follow the usual process of booking a consignment.

### Extra options available for repeating consignments

**Placeholders**

In the Customer Reference and Manifest fields, you're able to insert placeholders. These placeholders will automatically update to the correct value when the consignment is generated by the system.

For example, if you want the reference to read "Daily Pickup - 2020-06-20", where "2020-06-20" is the date of the consignment's creation, you would enter the example reference shown below.

![repeating-consignments-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/repeating-consignments-0.png?width=525&height=123&name=repeating-consignments-0.png)

**M****anifest Creation**

The other option which differs from adding a regular consignment is whether or not you want to **Always** create a new Manifest for this Consignment, or whether you want the job to be added to an existing manifest for that day (if it exists). If it doesn't exist, then create a new Manifest.

Regardless of your choice, you need to insert a New Manifest Name to be used for the new Manifest.

Once the repeating consignment is saved, a new consignment will be created automatically on the specified intervals with the settings in respective repeating consignment.

**Consignment Items on Repeating Consignments**

Once you save the repeating Consignment you will be able to add Consignment Items.

If you know what will be moving on the recurring consignment then you can add these details now.

For consignments with changing freight quantities, the Consignment Items can be left blank for now and filled out on the day the Consignment is generated.

**Editing or Testing a Repeating Consignment**

You can see your existing Repeating Consignments at any time from the Consignments page by clicking on the **Repeating Consignments** tab.

From here, you have the option to **Run**, **Edit** or **Delete** the repeating consignment.

Running the Repeating Consignment allows you to force the system to create a Consignment based on the settings you have just entered in the Repeating Consignment template. The generated consignment will be visible in your Consignment List allowing you to check over it.

If any further changes need to be made, you can then navigate back to the Repeating Consignment and edit the settings as required.

**Scheduling Repeating Consignments based on the day of week**

It is also possible to schedule repeating consignments on specific days of the week.

To manage this schedule, once the Repeating Consignment is created, navigate the list of repeating consignments and click on **Edit**for the repeating consignment.

Once on the Edit Repeating Consignment Page, click on **Manage Schedules**.
On the **Add Schedule for Repeating Entity** page select the days on which you want the Consignment to be created.

![repeating-consignments-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/repeating-consignments-1.png?width=670&height=377&name=repeating-consignments-1.png)

This can be done multiple times, allowing you to make certain weeks skip normal delivery days (for example public holidays).

Sunday is treated as the starting of the week in CartonCloud, therefore if the "Start date" selected is not Sunday, the system will automatically set the Start date to be the last Sunday from the date selected.

Once the Day specific schedule has been set, a calendar view will be presented, allowing you better visibility of when the system will be generating the repeating Consignment.

![repeating-consignments-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/repeating-consignments-2.png?width=556&height=431&name=repeating-consignments-2.png)
In the example provided above, the repeating Consignment is set to be created on Wednesday and Friday each week.

---

<a id="setting-up-service-types"></a>
## Setting up Service Types

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-service-types_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Prerequisites
- Benefits
- Use Cases
- How to create Service Types

### Purpose

Service Types allow you to classify and differentiate the types of transport services your operation provides. This is commonly used to distinguish between service levels such as **General** and **Express**, or to indicate specific service requirements like **Frozen**, **Chilled**, **Tail Lift**, **HIAB**, or **Air Ride**.

By setting up Service Types, you can manage pricing and delivery urgency more effectively across your consignments.

### Prerequisites

- You must have **Administrator** access to manage Custom Fields.
- Ensure your [**Rate Cards**](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Creating-Transport-Rates) are set up if you plan to apply pricing by Service Type.

### Benefits

Using Service Types allows you to:

- **Apply different pricing** to consignments based on the selected Service Type
- **Link delivery urgency** to each consignment by associating it with the relevant service level
- Confirm and update the Service Type when using the [Pack Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Pack-Screen)

### Use Cases

- Charge a higher rate for Express deliveries
- Apply specific rates for HIAB-required deliveries

### How to create Service Types

- In the top navigation bar, type **Custom Fields** into the **Search for Anything!** bar.
- Select the **Custom Fields** page from the search results.
- Click the **Consignment Data** tab to view all custom fields related to consignments.

![setting-up-service-types-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-service-types-0.png?width=670&height=170&name=setting-up-service-types-0.png)

- Locate the existing **Service Type** field.
- Click the **pencil icon** under the **Action** column to configure it.
- CartonCloud includes **General** and **Express** Service Types by default.
- Use the **green toggle sliders** to enable or disable each one as needed

![setting-up-service-types-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-service-types-1.png?width=349&height=486&name=setting-up-service-types-1.png)

**Adding a Service Type**

- Click the **plus icon** at the bottom of the Service Types list.
- Enter the **name** of your new Service Type (e.g. Frozen, Tail Lift).
- Click **Save** to apply the changes.

**Setting a Default Service Type**

- Select a default Service Type to auto-populate this field when new consignments are created.
- This is especially useful for consignments generated from **Sale Orders**, ensuring consistency and reducing manual entry.

---

<a id="setting-up-transport-products"></a>
## Setting up Transport Products

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-transport-products_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits
- T ransport Products Video Overview
- How to create a Transport Product
- Transport Product Status
- How to charge for a Transport Product
- Transport Products List View
- Export/Import Transport Products
- Setting up Transport Products with barcodes for the Pack Screen
- How Transport Product weights interact with the system

### Purpose

Transport Products allow you to set preconfigured descriptions and codes for a Consignment Item. You can also optionally add the predefined length, width and height.

### Benefits

Once a Transport Product is created, you are then able to do two things:

- Book Consignments much faster by using Transport Products within Consignment items to reduce repetitive data entry
- Define Rates in your Rate Cards based on specific Transport Products. For example, sending a tyre from Brisbane to Sydney or sending a Solar Panel from Melbourne to Adelaide.
- Use the Pack Screen and automatically assign Transport Products to Consignment Items for packing.

### Transport Products Video Overview

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/ocMEqIFIK4M

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/tvCDxgRRHbg

### How to create a Transport Product

- Navigate to the Transport Products page, Transport > Transport Products .
- Select the green +Add Product in the top left corner.
- Complete the required fields.
- Select the green Save button.

![setting-up-transport-products-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-transport-products-0.png?width=670&height=242&name=setting-up-transport-products-0.png)

The unit of measure the dimensions are displayed in can be configured in the Organisation Settings. For more information, please see [Changing the unit of measure in your tenancy](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/changing-the-unit-of-measure-in-your-tenancy).

### Transport Product Status (Active and Inactive)

When creating a Transport Product, you can choose the status of either Active or Inactive.

If a Transport Product is Inactive, it will not be listed as an option in the Consignment item code dropdown on the Consignment.

If a Parser is imported with an inactive Transport Product, the order will be rejected, and the error message will advise that the item code is not valid. If a Sale Order Unit of Measure is mapped to a Transport product, then the Transport Product will not be able to be set to Inactive.

To change the status of a Transport Product from the list page view:

- Use the check box on the side of the product.
- Select the blue Update Status button.
- Select Deactivate .

![setting-up-transport-products-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-transport-products-1.png?width=670&height=272&name=setting-up-transport-products-1.png)

**To change the status of a Transport Product from the edit Transport Product view:**

- Select the Transport Product you wish to edit.
- Slide the Active/Inactive toggle.
- Select Save .

![setting-up-transport-products-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-transport-products-2.png?width=670&height=295&name=setting-up-transport-products-2.png)

### How to charge for a Transport Product (Consignment Item)

Transport Products can create set rates within your Customers Rate Cards for moving a specific Transport Product from one Rate Zone to another.

How to set up charges for Transport Products is covered in the [Setting up Transport Rates](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/kIDcI) article of the setup guide, with further per page support available on the [View Rate Card](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/View+Rate+Card) article.

### Transport Products List View

You can sort and filter the list from the Transport Products list view and configure how the Transport Products appear in the view.

You can use the simple sort, advanced sort and advanced filter functionality to organise your Transport Products as you see fit.

See [Advanced sorting and filtering](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/LIbcI) for more information on how to use the filter and sort functionality.

### Export/Import Transport Products

To update and create Transport Products in bulk you can export and then import them into CartonCloud.

To do so:

- Select the Transport Products you wish to export using the tick-box on the far left.
- Select the three-dot circle in the top right corner.
- Select **Export**.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Jun-01-2026-09-49-21-7937-PM.png?width=1891&height=815&name=image-png-Jun-01-2026-09-49-21-7937-PM.png)

- Edit the excel file and then save the file.

Note, if you are creating a new Transport Product, ensure you keep column A (the id column) empty.

- Select the three-dot circle in the top right corner.
- Select **Import**.
- Select the file to upload.
- Select Import.
- You will then be notified of when the import is complete and be able to view your results.

### Setting up Transport Products with barcodes for the Pack Screen

If you are using the [Pack Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Pack-Screen) you will need to ensure:

- The commonly used packaging (e.g boxes, satchels) is set up as Transport Products.
- A unique barcode is assigned to the Transport Products (add the barcode to the barcode field when creating or updating the Transport Product).

![setting-up-transport-products-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-transport-products-4.png?width=670&height=292&name=setting-up-transport-products-4.png)

When you scan a Transport Product barcode in the Pack Screen, a new Consignment Item is created automatically. The Product Code, Description, and Dimensions are pre-filled, making the packing process faster and more accurate.

### How Transport Product weights interact with the system

When a weight has been entered against a Transport Product, it will interact with Consignment Item weights in the following ways:

- **Pack Screen:**
  - When the Transport Product is selected for an existing Consignment Item, the weight is added to the item's current weight.
  - Scanning a Transport Product barcode automatically creates a new Consignment Item, set to the Transport Product's weight.
- **Consignment Items Screen:**
  - Selecting the Transport Product on theConsignment Items tab of a consignmentwill override and set the Consignment Item's weight to the Transport Product's weight.
- **Sale Order Consignment Creation:**
  - When generating a Consignment from a Sale Order, if the associated Sale Order Product does not have a weight specified, the system will use the Transport Product's weight.

---

<a id="showing-consignment-errors-to-customers"></a>
## Showing Consignment Errors To Customers

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/showing-consignment-errors-to-customers_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Allowing customer access to consignment errors

### Purpose

Consignment Errors are reported by Users of CartonCloud and can be reported from within the Consignments themselves. These Errors range from the Consignment being Undeliverable to having their Cartons/Pallets count changed. Consignment Errors by default are visible only to Admins and Onforwarders. However, if a Customer requests access to the Consignment Errors for whatever reason, Admins can allow access. This access is controlled by an Organisation Setting which means that once turned on, all Customers will have access to the Consignment Errors.

An important note is that when Customers are allowed access to the Consignment Errors, and a Customer views the list of Errors, then the Customer **will only see the Errors that correspond to them**.They will not see errors that belong to other Customers.

### Allowing customer access to consignment errors

To allow Customers access to the Consignment Errors:

1. Click in the "Search For Anything" bar at the top of the screen and type "Organisation Settings" and click the entry that appears. This will bring up the Edit Organisation Settings screen.
2. Navigate to the Features & Options tab.
3. Scroll down the Settings and check the box for the option: Show Consignment Errors Menu to Customers .

While this box is checked all Customers will have access to the Consignment Errors.

---

<a id="submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod"></a>
## Submitting Invoice Photos as Part of a POD

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Submitting an invoice photo
- Accessing an invoice photo

### Purpose

As part of a POD submission through the CartonCloud mobile apps, drivers may want to include an invoice photo. This can be done as an alternative to collecting a signature for consignments where a signature is required to successfully submit the POD, or in addition to a signature to provide additional information.

### Submitting an invoice photo

To submit an Invoice Photo as part of a POD, proceed as normal to the "*Record POD*" view after selecting a consignment from the job list. There you will find the "*Add Invoice Photos*" section and upon tapping any of the "*+*" buttons will be presented with a choice of either taking a photo or choosing an existing photo from your device's photo library.

Once you have either taken a photo or chosen an existing one, confirm your selection by selecting "*Use Photo*".

![submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-0.png?width=670&height=384&name=submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-0.png)

The chosen Invoice Photo will then be visible in the Invoice Photo section.

Should you want to delete the photo again at this stage, simply tap the photo preview and select "*Yes*" when asked if you want to delete this photo.

Proceed as normal with filling out any other required POD data and select "*Save POD*" once completed. The POD (including the Invoice Photo if selected) will then be uploaded to CartonCloud and the consignment marked completed.

![submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-1.png?width=499&height=425&name=submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-1.png)
Invoice Photos allow drivers to record PODs without having to submit a signature, therefore the consignment status will automatically change to completed once a POD including either a signature OR an invoice photo is received (if the consignment requires a signature POD).

### Accessing an invoice photo

Choose the relevant consignment and open its "*View Consignment*" screen. There you will notice several options related to an Invoice Photo POD.

Firstly, the consignment has been marked delivered as an Invoice Photo POD has been received. Secondly, the "*Customer Invoices*" and "*History*" tabs will provide you with more information about the POD and access to the Invoice Photo itself.

![submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-2.png?width=670&height=274&name=submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-2.png)
**Customer Invoices Tab**

Within the Customer Invoices Tab the uploaded Invoice Photo can be easily accessed and modified. Optional actions include downloading the Invoice Photo, or viewing, unassigning, assigning or deleting it.

![submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-3.png?width=670&height=198&name=submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-3.png)
On selecting any of the *Actions*a number of tabs give access to editing and viewing functionalities.

![submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-4.png?width=670&height=207&name=submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-4.png)
![submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-5.png?width=582&height=366&name=submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-5.png)
![submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-6.png?width=670&height=141&name=submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-6.png)
**History Tab**

As for any POD submission, details about an Invoice Photo POD can be accessed via the History tab.
![submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-7.png?width=670&height=85&name=submitting-invoice-photos-as-part-of-a-pod-7.png)

---

### Setting up Transport Products with barcodes for the Pack Screen

If you are using the [Pack Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Pack-Screen) you will need to ensure:

- The commonly used packaging (e.g boxes, satchels) is set up as Transport Products.
- A unique barcode is assigned to the Transport Products (add the barcode to the barcode field when creating or updating the Transport Product).

![transport-products-consignment-items-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/transport-products-consignment-items-6.png?width=670&height=292&name=transport-products-consignment-items-6.png)

When you scan a Transport Product barcode in the Pack Screen, a new Consignment Item is created automatically. The Product Code, Description, and Dimensions are pre-filled, making the packing process faster and more accurate.

### How Transport Product weights interact with the system

When a weight has been entered against a Transport Product, it will interact with Consignment Item weights in the following ways:

- **Pack Screen:**
  - When the Transport Product is selected for an existing Consignment Item, the weight is added to the item's current weight.
  - Scanning a Transport Product barcode automatically creates a new Consignment Item, set to the Transport Product's weight.
- **Consignment Items Screen:**
  - Selecting the Transport Product on theConsignment Items tab of a consignmentwill override and set the Consignment Item's weight to the Transport Product's weight.
- **Sale Order Consignment Creation:**
  - When generating a Consignment from a Sale Order, if the associated Sale Order Product does not have a weight specified, the system will use the Transport Product's weight.

---

### Consignment Items

The Consignment Items are the items on the Consignment. These items are represented by Transport Products, such as a pallet or a carton. From here you can see what items are associated with the Consignment, the quantity and item specifications such as weight and cubic.

Consignment Items can be edited, deleted and added from this view.

To view the history of the Consignment.

<a id="view-service-days"></a>
## View Service Days

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/view-service-days_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- To view service days

### Purpose

Service Days are the days in which you service a particular Delivery Zone.

From this page, it is possible to check the delivery schedule your Transport or Warehousing operation has set up going to a particular Delivery Zone (suburb & postcode) which in turn determines Delivery Run schedules. This is particularly useful for Transport providers who go to rural areas and therefore only service an area on certain days of the week.

Please note that by default delivery schedules will show every day as an active delivery day, so this page is only relevant if your provider has elected to use this feature.

### To view service days

To check the schedule to a specific suburb, search for it in the search bar.

Once found, select it and the service days will appear.

![view-service-days-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-service-days-0.png?width=670&height=429&name=view-service-days-0.png)

In the example provided, the suburb has not been configured, therefore all days are showing as active during workdays.

Active Service days are represented by a tick next to the date.

# Transport Management > Delivery Runs

<a id="change-consignment-delivery-run"></a>
## Change Consignment Delivery Run

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/change-consignment-delivery-run_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to reallocate a consignment
  - Automatically reallocate a consignment
  - Manually reallocate a consignment
  - Reallocating consignments in bulk

### Purpose

To remove a Consignment from one Delivery Run and move it to another.

If you change the Consignment address, you can allow CartonCloud to redetermine the Delivery Run using the new address automatically.

### How to reallocate a consignment

You can reallocate a Consignment to a Delivery Run either automatically or manually.

**Automatically reallocate a Consignment**

CartonCloud can automatically redetermine the Delivery Run of a Consignment when you change the delivery address.

- Navigate to the Consignments page, **Transport**>**Consignments**.
- Select the individual Consignment.
- Select the **Edit** button within the **Details** tab.

![change-consignment-delivery-run-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/change-consignment-delivery-run-0.png?width=670&height=175&name=change-consignment-delivery-run-0.png)

- Change the **Delivery Address.** Upon changing the address, the **Redetermine Delivery** option will appear at the bottom of the screen.
- Select **Yes**.
- Select **Save**.

CartonCloud will automatically redetermine the Delivery Run using the new address. The Driver and Run Sheet will remain unchanged.

**Manually reallocate a Consignment**

You can reallocate a Consignment to a Delivery Run manually, either individually or in bulk.

**Reallocating an individual Consignment**

- Navigate to the Consignments page, **Transport**>**Consignments**.
- Select the individual Consignment.
- Within the **Details** tab, navigate down to the **Allocated to Delivery Run**field.
- Select **Move**.
- Select the **Change Delivery Run**tab.
- Using the **Delivery Run** drop-down menu, select the Delivery Run you wish to add the Consignment to.

![change-consignment-delivery-run-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/change-consignment-delivery-run-1.png?width=670&height=304&name=change-consignment-delivery-run-1.png)

- Select **Move**.

The Driver and Run Sheet will remain unchanged.

### Reallocating Consignments in bulk

- Navigate to the Consignment page, **Transport**>**Consignments**.
- Select the Consignments you wish to move by ticking the select box.
- Select **Move**.

![change-consignment-delivery-run-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/change-consignment-delivery-run-2.png?width=670&height=218&name=change-consignment-delivery-run-2.png)

- Select the **Change Delivery Run** tab.
- Using the **Delivery Run**drop-down menu, select the Delivery Run you wish to add the Consignment to.
- Click **Move**.

![change-consignment-delivery-run-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/change-consignment-delivery-run-3.png?width=670&height=332&name=change-consignment-delivery-run-3.png)

The Driver and Run Sheet will remain unchanged.

---

<a id="delivery-run-details"></a>
## Delivery Run Details

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/delivery-run-details_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to view the Delivery Run
- Delivery Run Details tab
- Delivery Run Consignments tab
- Delivery Run Map tab

### Purpose

Delivery Runs in CartonCloud are the geographical boundaries of the places your operation delivers to. Once you have created your Delivery Runs you can view each Delivery Run, modify the Delivery Run, see what Consignments are assigned to that run and access a map overview of the Delivery Run.

### How to view the Delivery Run

- Navigate to the Delivery Run page, Transport > Delivery Runs .
- Click on the relevant Delivery Run.
- You will be taken to the individual Delivery Run and be able to view and make any changes to the Delivery Run.

![delivery-run-details-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delivery-run-details-0.png?width=670&height=353&name=delivery-run-details-0.png)

### Delivery Run Details tab

![delivery-run-details-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delivery-run-details-1.png?width=670&height=258&name=delivery-run-details-1.png)

From the Details tab you can view:

| **Field** | **Explanation** |
| --- | --- |
| **Basics** |  |
| Name | Name of the delivery |
| Carier | The carrier assigned to the Delivery Run |
| Final Consignment Delivery Status | The final status the Consignment will reach once it is delivered. You can update this status by editing the Delivery Run. |
| Consignment Status when Delivered via App | The status of the Consignment when it has been delivered via the mobile app. This can be updated by editing the Delivery Run. |
| **Specifics** |  |
| Hide on unallocated delivery runs list | If the Delivery Run will be hidden from the unallocated Delivery Runs list. This can be enabled when creating or editing the Delivery Run.  This is useful for runs such as Pickup Runs, which you don't want to see on the "Unallocated Delivery Runs" list, especially if you're automatically allocating the run to a device using: [Automatically allocate Consignments to Drivers from Delivery Runs](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Automatically+allocate+Consignments+to+Drivers+from+Delivery+Runs). |
| Onforwarder | If an onforwarder operates the Delivery Run. This can be set when creating the Delivery Run or by editing the Delivery Run. For additional information about Onforwarder functionality, see [Onforwarder Addresses](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Onforwarder+Addresses). |
| Export Template | The template that is utilised when exporting the Delivery Run |

**Buttons**

| **Button** | **Function** |
| --- | --- |
| Edit | To edit the Delivery Run |
| Manage schedules | To manage the schedule of the Delivery Run. See [Delivery Run Schedules](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Delivery-Run-Schedules) for more information. |
| Link addresses | To set up Address to Delivery Run mapping. |
| Confirm Delivery Run | To confirm the Delivery Run (quantity). |
| Merge Delivery Run | To merge the Delivery Run with another Delivery Run |

### Consignments tab

From the Consignments tab you can view all Consignments on the Delivery Run.

![delivery-run-details-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delivery-run-details-2.png?width=670&height=353&name=delivery-run-details-2.png)

| **Button** | **Action** |
| --- | --- |
| Move | Select a Consignment and select the Move button to move it to a different Delivery Run. |
| Group Consignments | Select more than one Consignment and click Group Consignments to group Consignments together. |
| + Add Consignment | To add Consignments to the Delivery Run. |
| Update Status | By selecting Consignments you can update the status of the Consignments in bulk. |

Note, if there is a lock icon against the Consignment this means there is a required delivery date for that Consignment and the date can not change.

### Map tab

From the Map tab you can see a map view of all Consignments on the Delivery Run.

![delivery-run-details-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delivery-run-details-3.png?width=670&height=293&name=delivery-run-details-3.png)
