<a id="delivery-run-schedules"></a>
## Delivery Run Schedules

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/delivery-run-schedules_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Use cases
- How to create a schedule for a delivery run
- Examples

### Purpose

To select the day and frequency in which a Delivery Run runs each week.

### Use cases

If you have Delivery Runs that:

- Don't run every day
- Runs on specific days
- Has a particular schedule each week which changes week to week

### How to create a schedule for a Delivery Run

- Navigate to the Delivery Runs page, Transport>Delivery Runs.
- Click on the relevant Delivery Run.
- Select the Details tab.
- Click Manage schedules .

![delivery-run-schedules-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delivery-run-schedules-0.png?width=670&height=294&name=delivery-run-schedules-0.png)

- Click +Add .

![delivery-run-schedules-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delivery-run-schedules-1.png?width=670&height=74&name=delivery-run-schedules-1.png)

- Enter a Name
- Use the tick boxes to select the days of the week you wish the Delivery Run to run.
- The start date will be set as the last Sunday of the week.
- Select the interval of weeks you wish the schedule to run. For example, if you enter 1, it will run every week; if you enter 2, it will run every 2nd week.

![delivery-run-schedules-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delivery-run-schedules-2.png?width=670&height=268&name=delivery-run-schedules-2.png)

- Click Add .

Note that if you want to overwrite a Schedule set for a previous period, you will want to delete the old Schedules.

### Examples

If you want to run the Brisbane Run every weekday apart from Thursday.

![delivery-run-schedules-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delivery-run-schedules-2.png?width=670&height=268&name=delivery-run-schedules-2.png)

<a id="delivery-runs"></a>
## Delivery Runs

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/delivery-runs_

### Table of Contents

- What is a delivery run
- Benefits of using delivery runs
- How to create a delivery run
- Delivery runs and automatic consignment allocation

### What is a delivery run

Delivery Runs in CartonCloud are the geographical boundaries of the places your operation delivers to.

On the below map you can see different areas in which a transport company delivers to. Each of these areas will have its own Delivery Run in CartonCloud.

![delivery-runs-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delivery-runs-0.png?width=306&height=569&name=delivery-runs-0.png)

![delivery-runs-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delivery-runs-1.png?width=670&height=255&name=delivery-runs-1.png)

### Benefits of using delivery runs

Delivery Runs break your Consignments into manageable quantities during allocation. In addition, they enable an efficient and automatic allocation process in CartonCloud.

### How to create a delivery run

You can either create Delivery Runs manually or create them in bulk using the Export/Import function.

See [Add a Delivery Run](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/bAeYHw) for more information.

### Delivery Runs and automatic Consignment allocation

CartonCloud can automatically allocate a Consignment to the appropriate Delivery Run depending on its pick up location and delivery location. CartonCloud does this using Transport Lanes. Transport Lanes map the to and from addresses to the corresponding Delivery Run. See [Setting up CartonCloud to automatically allocate Consignments](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-cartoncloud-to-automatically-allocate-consignments) for more information.

![delivery-runs-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delivery-runs-2.png?width=390&height=437&name=delivery-runs-2.png)

---

<a id="delivery-schedules-for-addresses-delivery-zones-delivery-runs"></a>
## Delivery Schedules for Addresses, Delivery Zones, Delivery Runs

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/delivery-schedules-for-addresses-delivery-zones-delivery-runs_

Delivery Schedules affect the automatic 'Delivery Run Date' of Consignments within CartonCloud.

You're probably already using Delivery Schedules within your Delivery Runs as the default Delivery Schedule for a Delivery Run is to operate each day from Monday to Friday.

Delivery Schedules can be applied to three different object types within CartonCloud (**in order of priority**).

1. Addresses
2. Delivery Zones (Suburb / Postcode)
3. Delivery Runs

The order of priority is important.

For instance: If a Consignment is using a particular Address that has a schedule it's schedule will be used over and above that of the Delivery Zone or Delivery Run.

If the Address does not have a schedule, then it'll check for a schedule in the Delivery Zone. If nothing is found, it'll use the Schedule within a Delivery Run.

![delivery-schedules-for-addresses-delivery-zones-delivery-runs-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delivery-schedules-for-addresses-delivery-zones-delivery-runs-0.png?width=309&height=442&name=delivery-schedules-for-addresses-delivery-zones-delivery-runs-0.png)
To add or edit a schedule for an **Address** navigate to the Address you wish to set a schedule for.

![delivery-schedules-for-addresses-delivery-zones-delivery-runs-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delivery-schedules-for-addresses-delivery-zones-delivery-runs-1.png?width=670&height=254&name=delivery-schedules-for-addresses-delivery-zones-delivery-runs-1.png)
For a **Delivery Zone**search for the Delivery Zone you wish to set a schedule for using **Search for anything!**

![delivery-schedules-for-addresses-delivery-zones-delivery-runs-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delivery-schedules-for-addresses-delivery-zones-delivery-runs-2.png?width=670&height=356&name=delivery-schedules-for-addresses-delivery-zones-delivery-runs-2.png)

For a **Delivery Run**search for the Delivery Run you wish to set a schedule for using **Search for anything!**Or navigate to delivery Runs by selecting **Transport** in the main menu, followed by **Delivery Runs** in the drop-down. Then find the desired Delivery Run.

![delivery-schedules-for-addresses-delivery-zones-delivery-runs-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/delivery-schedules-for-addresses-delivery-zones-delivery-runs-3.png?width=563&height=354&name=delivery-schedules-for-addresses-delivery-zones-delivery-runs-3.png)

---

<a id="how-a-consignment-determines-its-delivery-run"></a>
## How a Consignment determines its Delivery Run

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-a-consignment-determines-its-delivery-run_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- 1. Default operation
- 2. Onforwarder address enabled

### Purpose

This document explains how CartonCloud automatically selects a Delivery Run for a specific Consignment.

There are two ways in which the allocation process operates:

1. Default Operation (Onforwarder Addresses Disabled)
2. Onforwarder Addresses Enabled

Once Transport Lanes have been enabled on your CartonCloud account, please refer to the last diagram on this page.

Note the below workflows are impacted by the following settings. Please keep these settings in mind when calculating how the Delivery Run is calculated for a Consignment:

**Customer Settings:**

- Delivery Run Dates
  - Ignore Specified Delivery Run Date (allocate to next Scheduled Run Date always)
  - When a Required Delivery Date is given, snap the delivery to the closest available scheduled date (if unchecked, consignment may get allocated to a date where the run isn't scheduled)

**Organisation Settings:**

- Bulk Allocation Configuration
  - Allocate Run Sheets Defaults
    - Default "Override Cosnignments Delivery Run" checkbox to checked on Bulk allocation and Move Consignments Screens

### 1. Default operation (onforwarder address disabled)

By default, Onforwarder Addresses are disabled so the Allocation process is very straightforward:

![how-a-consignment-determines-its-delivery-run-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-a-consignment-determines-its-delivery-run-0.png?width=334&height=593&name=how-a-consignment-determines-its-delivery-run-0.png)

### 2. Onforwarder Addresses Enabled

*To learn more about what Onforwarder Addresses are, and how to use them, see our page on [Onforwarder Addresses](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/onforwarder-addresses)*

Enabling Onforwarder addresses changes the logic for the Delivery Run allocation whenever Onforwarder addresses are used.

![how-a-consignment-determines-its-delivery-run-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-a-consignment-determines-its-delivery-run-1.png?width=364&height=427&name=how-a-consignment-determines-its-delivery-run-1.png)

**Noteworthy points are:**

1. If an onforwarder address has been specified when creating a consignment (which can only be done through the web interface as imported manifests only contain the delivery address), then the onforwarder address will be used to handle the allocation.
2. When importing a manifest the system will try to automatically insert the onforwarder address if possible by using the A2DR data to perform a Reverse Mapping (a mapping from Delivery Run --> Onforwarder Address)

With Transport Lanes enabled:

![how-a-consignment-determines-its-delivery-run-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-a-consignment-determines-its-delivery-run-2.png?width=468&height=403&name=how-a-consignment-determines-its-delivery-run-2.png)

![how-a-consignment-determines-its-delivery-run-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-a-consignment-determines-its-delivery-run-3.png?width=466&height=450&name=how-a-consignment-determines-its-delivery-run-3.png)

---

<a id="how-delivery-runs-are-determined"></a>
## How Delivery Runs are Determined

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-delivery-runs-are-determined_

This document explains how CartonCloud automatically selects a Delivery Run for a specific Consignment.

There are two ways in which the allocation process operates:

1. Default Operation ( Onforwarder Addresses Disabled)
2. Onforwarder Addresses Enabled

**A2DR**refers to Address to Delivery Run Mapping (A2DR)
**A2A** refers to Delivery Address to Onforwarder Address Mapping (A2A)

1. Default Operation (Onforwarder Addresses Disabled):

By default, Onforwarder Addresses are disabled so the Allocation process is very straightforward:

![how-delivery-runs-are-determined-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-delivery-runs-are-determined-0.png?width=379&height=673&name=how-delivery-runs-are-determined-0.png)

 2. **Onforwarder Addresses Enabled:**

*To learn more about what Onforwarder Addresses are, and how to use them, see our page on [Onforwarder Addresses](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Onforwarder+Addresses)*

Enabling Onforwarder addresses changes the logic for the Delivery Run allocation whenever Onforwarder addresses are used.

Noteworthy points are:

If an onforwarder address has been specified when creating a consignment (which can only be done through the web interface as imported manifests only contain the delivery address), then the onforwarder address will be used to handle the allocation.

When importing a manifest the system will try to automatically insert the onforwarder address if possible by using the A2DR data to perform a Reverse Mapping (a mapping from Delivery Run --> Onforwarder Address)

---

<a id="how-to-add-a-delivery-run"></a>
## How to add a Delivery Run

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-add-a-delivery-run_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Adding a single delivery run
- Export/import delivery runs (create delivery runs in bulk)

### Purpose

When creating Delivery Runs, you can either

create them manually

or

create them in bulk using the Export/Import option

.

### Adding a single Delivery Run

**To add a single Delivery Run:**

- Navigate to the Delivery Runs page, **Transport**>**Delivery Runs**.
- Select **+Add Delivery Run**.

![how-to-add-a-delivery-run-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-add-a-delivery-run-0.png?width=670&height=158&name=how-to-add-a-delivery-run-0.png)

- Using the below field description, fill in each field as required.

![how-to-add-a-delivery-run-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-add-a-delivery-run-1.png?width=604&height=495&name=how-to-add-a-delivery-run-1.png)
**Field Descriptions**

| **Field** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Name | The name given to the Delivery Run |
| Carrier | The Carrier delivering the run (set as your own company unless using multicarriers). |
| Operation Days | The days of the week the run operates on |

**Field Descriptions - Advanced Options**

| Onforwarder | Select whether an onforwarder operates the Delivery Run. For example, if you have a Delivery Run named *TOLL* for all the consignments you give to the freight company Toll for delivery, the run would be an Onforwarder Run. Selecting this option causes two minor differences in Consignments allocated to the run.   Given a Required Delivery Date in the future, CartonCloud will always set the "delivery run date" as soon as possible (rather than trying to allocate to a delivery run date as close to the required date as possible). It is set up this way because generally, with Onforwarders, it's difficult to determine delivery times; hence delivering to the onforwarder as soon as possible is preferred.   The consignment will not be automatically updated to "In Transit" if you have "Enable Auto In Transit" enabled within the organisation settings ([Organisation Settings - Transport](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Organisation+Settings+-+Transport))   For additional information about Onforwarder functionality, see [Onforwarder Addresses](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Onforwarder+Addresses). |
| --- | --- |
| Final Consignment Delivery Status | When a consignment is "completed" within the [Mobile App](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Mobile+App) or from the web interface, the Final Consignment Delivery Status will be used. This is useful for Delivery Runs which are "Pickup from Warehouse", as rather than showing they were "Delivered", they were actually "Collected". |
| Consignment Status when Delivered via App | Suppose an onforwarder operates the Delivery Run, but your drivers must deliver the stock to the Onforwarder. In that case, you may want to modify the "Consignment Status when Delivered via App" to be "With On Forwarder". The "With On Forwarder" status is used to keep track of which deliveries have been given to the Onforwarder but have not yet had a signed POD come back for - once the signed POD is returned, scanned and uploaded to CartonCloud, the job closes and is marked "Delivered". |
| If Onforwarder Address Exists, charge for delivery to the Onforwarders Address (untick if you want to charge to the delivery location always) | This is a very powerful option when working with Onforwarder Addresses. Checking this box enables you to charge only to the Onforwarder rather than the delivery address. For more information on how/when to use this, check out: [Onforwarder Use Cases](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Onforwarder+Use+Cases) |
| Hide on unallocated delivery runs list. | This is useful for runs such as Pickup Runs, which you don't want to see on the "Unallocated Delivery Runs" list, especially if you're automatically allocating the run to a device using: [Automatically allocate Consignments to Drivers from Delivery Runs](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Automatically+allocate+Consignments+to+Drivers+from+Delivery+Runs). |
| Export Format Template | The format of the default run sheet created against the Delivery Run when exported. |

- Select Save.

You will now view the new Delivery Run on the All tab of the Delivery Runs page.

### Export/Import Delivery Runs (create Delivery Runs in bulk)

You will need to create one Delivery Run manually first before following this process, as you will need to export the Delivery Runs first.

- Navigate to the Delivery Runs page, Transport > Delivery Runs .
- Click the Export to CSV button.
- Open the exported file.
- Enter the name of the Delivery Runs you wish to add in the name column and the final status in the final status column.

Ensure you leave the id column blank for the new Delivery Runs you are adding.

![how-to-add-a-delivery-run-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-add-a-delivery-run-3.png?width=419&height=432&name=how-to-add-a-delivery-run-3.png)

- Save the file.
- Navigate back to the Delivery Runs page in CartonCloud.
- Select the Import CSV button.

![how-to-add-a-delivery-run-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-add-a-delivery-run-4.png?width=670&height=159&name=how-to-add-a-delivery-run-4.png)

- Select the file and click Upload File .
- The new Delivery Runs will be created.

If you wish to adjust the advanced options against the Delivery Run, you must do so at the individual Delivery Run level.

---

## How to show the Product Type In Delivery Runs

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-show-the-product-type-in-delivery-runs_

In the Organisation Settings - Transport tab, Click on
**"Show Product Type in Delivery Runs".**

This will show the product types for all the fields displayed on the "
**Delivery Runs**" page.

<a id="linking-delivery-runs-to-role-of-a-driver"></a>
## Linking Delivery Runs to role of a Driver

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/linking-delivery-runs-to-role-of-a-driver_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Use cases
- How to steps

### Purpose

Users with the Driver [Role](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/User-Roles-Explained) can be linked to a specific Delivery Run. By linking a Delivery Run to a Driver, Consignments for the Delivery Run will automatically show on the Driver's app without needing to be allocated. Once the POD is recorded against the Consignment, the Driver will be allocated to the record.
Note, numerous Drivers can be linked to the same Delivery Run.

### Use cases

Use cases for this requirement include:

- Warehouse Pick-Ups
- Repeating Consignments
- Permanent Delivery Runs

### How to steps

- Select Contacts > Users .
- Select the User you wish to edit.
- Select Edit Delivery Runs at the bottom of the page.
- Tick the Delivery Runs you wish to link to the Driver.

![linking-delivery-runs-to-role-of-a-driver-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/linking-delivery-runs-to-role-of-a-driver-0.png?width=670&height=352&name=linking-delivery-runs-to-role-of-a-driver-0.png)

- Scroll down and select Save .

---

<a id="making-delivery-runs-visible-to-customers-and-giving-them-aliases"></a>
## Making Delivery Runs visible to Customers and giving them aliases

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/making-delivery-runs-visible-to-customers-and-giving-them-aliases_

- To adjust the Delivery Runs visible to Customers begin by navigating to a Customer's record by selecting Contacts , then selecting Customers from the drop-down menu.
- On the View Customer page select Edit . Then select the Transport Management tab, followed by the Delivery Runs tab.
- From this page, a complete list of the Delivery Runs within your tenancy is displayed.
- Selecting these Delivery Runs as Visible to Customer will then do exactly that. The Visible Name then also allows you to provide an alias for the Delivery Run which the Customer will see from their view of CartonCloud.
- Ensure to scroll to the bottom of the page select Save after making any changes within this tab.

![making-delivery-runs-visible-to-customers-and-giving-them-aliases-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/making-delivery-runs-visible-to-customers-and-giving-them-aliases-0.png?width=670&height=368&name=making-delivery-runs-visible-to-customers-and-giving-them-aliases-0.png)

---

<a id="merging-or-deleting-delivery-runs"></a>
## Merging or deleting Delivery Runs

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/merging-or-deleting-delivery-runs_

**Be careful, merging Delivery Runs cannot be undone.**

- Delivery Runs cannot be deleted directly as they may be associated with existing data from Consignments and Delivery Zones.
- Instead, to get rid of a Delivery Run you will need to "merge" it into another Delivery Run - This will update all data belonging to the old old Delivery Run and link it to the merged Delivery Run instead.
- To merge a Delivery Run begin by selecting Transport in the main menu, followed by Delivery Runs in the drop-down menu.
- Select the All tab and find the Delivery Run you wish to merge.
- Then go to the Details tab within the Delivery Run and click the Merge Delivery Run button:
- Select the Delivery Run you wish to merge it with (which will continue to exist).
- Finally, click Save and the two Delivery Runs will be merged into the target Delivery Run.

---

<a id="setting-up-delivery-runs"></a>
## Setting up Delivery Runs

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-delivery-runs_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to set up your Delivery Runs

### Purpose

[Delivery Runs](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/nQGYHw) in CartonCloud are the geographical boundaries of the places your operation delivers to. The purpose of Delivery Runs is to break your consignments into manageable quantities during allocation.

Before creating Delivery Runs we recommend generating a comprehensive list of all the runs your Transport Operation services. If you need help with this, please reach out to our experienced Onboarders by submitting a ticket in the [Support Portal](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket).

It is not compulsory to set up the Advanced Options of Delivery Runs when creating them. These are mostly related to using a Delivery Run as a way to allocate consignments to an Onforwarder, which will be covered later in the setup guide.

How to set up your Delivery Runs

When creating Delivery Runs, you can either

create them manually

or

create them in bulk using the Export/Import option

.

Adding a single Delivery Run

**To add a single Delivery Run:**

- Navigate to the Delivery Runs page, Transport > Delivery Runs .
- Select +Add Delivery Run .
- Using the below field description, fill in each field as required.

**Field Descriptions**

| **Field** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Name | The name given to the Delivery Run |
| Carrier | The Carrier delivering the run (set as your own company unless using multicarriers). |
| Operation Days | The days of the week the run operates on |

**Field Descriptions - Advanced Options**

| Onforwarder | Select whether an onforwarder operates the Delivery Run. For example, if you have a Delivery Run named *TOLL* for all the consignments you give to the freight company Toll for delivery, the run would be an Onforwarder Run. Selecting this option causes two minor differences in Consignments allocated to the run.   Given a Required Delivery Date in the future, CartonCloud will always set the "delivery run date" as soon as possible (rather than trying to allocate to a delivery run date as close to the required date as possible). It is set up this way because generally, with Onforwarders, it's difficult to determine delivery times; hence delivering to the onforwarder as soon as possible is preferred.   The consignment will not be automatically updated to "In Transit" if you have "Enable Auto In Transit" enabled within the organisation settings ([Organisation Settings - Transport](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Organisation+Settings+-+Transport))   For additional information about Onforwarder functionality, see [Onforwarder Addresses](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Onforwarder+Addresses). |
| --- | --- |
| Final Consignment Delivery Status | When a consignment is "completed" within the [Mobile App](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Mobile+App) or from the web interface, the Final Consignment Delivery Status will be used. This is useful for Delivery Runs which are "Pickup from Warehouse", as rather than showing they were "Delivered", they were actually "Collected". |
| Consignment Status when Delivered via App | Suppose an onforwarder operates the Delivery Run, but your drivers must deliver the stock to the Onforwarder. In that case, you may want to modify the "Consignment Status when Delivered via App" to be "With On Forwarder". The "With On Forwarder" status is used to keep track of which deliveries have been given to the Onforwarder but have not yet had a signed POD come back for - once the signed POD is returned, scanned and uploaded to CartonCloud, the job closes and is marked "Delivered". |
| If Onforwarder Address Exists, charge for delivery to the Onforwarders Address (untick if you want to charge to the delivery location always) | This is a very powerful option when working with Onforwarder Addresses. Checking this box enables you to charge only to the Onforwarder rather than the delivery address. For more information on how/when to use this, check out: [Onforwarder Use Cases](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Onforwarder+Use+Cases) |
| Hide on unallocated delivery runs list. | This is useful for runs such as Pickup Runs, which you don't want to see on the "Unallocated Delivery Runs" list, especially if you're automatically allocating the run to a device using: [Automatically allocate Consignments to Drivers from Delivery Runs](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Automatically+allocate+Consignments+to+Drivers+from+Delivery+Runs). |
| Export Format Template | The format of the default run sheet created against the Delivery Run when exported. |

- Select **Save.**

You will now view the new Delivery Run on the All tab of the Delivery Runs page

**Export/Import Delivery Runs (create Delivery Runs in bulk)**

To create multiple Delivery Runs at once, we recommend using the Export/Import function.

**You will need to create one Delivery Run manually first before following this process, as you will need to export the Delivery Runs first.**

- Navigate to the Delivery Runs page, Transport > Delivery Runs .
- Click the Export to CSV button.
- Open the exported file.
- Enter the name of the Delivery Runs you wish to add in the name column and the final status in the final status column.

Ensure you leave the id column blank for the new Delivery Runs you are adding.

- Save the file.
- Navigate back to the Delivery Runs page in CartonCloud.
- Select the Import CSV button.
- Select the file and click Upload File .
- The new Delivery Runs will be created.

**If you wish to adjust the advanced options against the Delivery Run, you must do so at the individual Delivery Run level.**

Next Step: [Setting up Transport Zone Sets](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-transport-zone-sets)

## Adding a comment to a Manifest

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/adding-a-comment-to-a-manifest_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits
- How to add a comment to a manifest

### Purpose

To add a comment to a Manifest through the web app for users (excluding customers) to view (on the web app).

### Benefits

- To record important information against the Manifest.
- To communicate key information in relation to the Manifest with other users.

### How to add a comment to a Manifest

- Navigate to the Manifest page, Transport > Manifests.
- Select View against the Manifest you wish to add the comment to.

![adding-a-comment-to-a-manifest-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-a-comment-to-a-manifest-0.png?width=670&height=298&name=adding-a-comment-to-a-manifest-0.png)

- Click Add comment.

![adding-a-comment-to-a-manifest-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-a-comment-to-a-manifest-1.png?width=670&height=304&name=adding-a-comment-to-a-manifest-1.png)

- Click Submit.

<a id="automatically-creating-manifests-assigned-to-a-specific-driver"></a>
## Automatically Creating Manifests Assigned To A Specific Driver

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/automatically-creating-manifests-assigned-to-a-specific-driver_

### Table of Contents

- Requirements
- [Overview](https://help.cartoncloud.com#overview)

### Requirements

This functionality is only available when uploading **Manifests** through a **Parser** that supports this functionality. If the Customer that wants to use this functionality does not a have a Parser that can do it then [Contact CartonCloud](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket) for assistance.

### Overview

When a Customer sends through a Manifest to CartonCloud, the system uses Parsers to convert the file that is sent into a Manifest with Consignments. By default, when a Manifest is parsed by CartonCloud it generates the Manifest and the corresponding Consignments. It does not assign these to a Driver. This step is done manually when allocating Consignments to Drivers. To allow CartonCloud to automatically assign a given Manifest to a Driver when the file is parsed, the file being sent needs to either provide the Driver's Name as part of the overall Manifest information or as a column in the data being sent. As stated above this functionality will not work without a Parser that is capable of handling this functionality.

---

<a id="bulk-export-manifests"></a>
## Bulk Export Manifests

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/bulk-export-manifests_

To access the Bulk Export Manifests page select **Reports** in the main menu, followed by **Bulk Export Manifests** in the drop-down menu.

The Bulk Export Manifests page allows you to export a CSV spreadsheet from CartonCloud containing all data associated with your Manifests which were added over a specified date period.

Each Manifest record will create a new line on the report.

To generate choose the beginning and ending dates for the report to run.

Then, select **Go** and the CSV file will be downloaded.![bulk-export-manifests-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bulk-export-manifests-0.png?width=670&height=507&name=bulk-export-manifests-0.png)

Report Fields

The generated report will contain the following fields for each Manifest line.

- id
- customer_id
- customer
- customer_reference
- pallets
- date_added
- income
- expense
- invoice_id
- status
- start_status
- last_modified
- Chilled Temperature
- Dry Temperature
- Frozen Temperature
