<a id="how-to-split-a-manifest"></a>
## How to split a Manifest

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-split-a-manifest_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Process flow of splitting a manifest
- How to split a manifest

### Purpose

When a Manifest arrives at the warehouse but one or more of the Consignments are still yet to arrive you can split the Manifest.

By splitting the Manifest you are dividing the Manifest into the Consignments that have arrived and the Consignments that are pending arrival.

Benefits of splitting the Manifest when not all Consignment have arrived:

- The data in CartonCloud will accurately reflect what has physically occurred.
- It will increase visibility to all users on what Consignments have and haven't arrived.
- It will be easier to manage the remaining Consignments when they do arrive.

### Process flow of splitting a manifest

![how-to-split-a-manifest-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-split-a-manifest-0.png?width=670&height=270&name=how-to-split-a-manifest-0.png)

### How to split a manifest

You can split a Manifest as it arrives or before it arrives.

**To split a Manifest as it arrives:**

- Navigate to the Manifests page (by typing in Manifests in the Search for anything bar).
- Select View from the Actions column within the relevant Manifest.
- Click the Sort Arrivals button at the bottom of the page.

![how-to-split-a-manifest-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-split-a-manifest-1.png?width=670&height=382&name=how-to-split-a-manifest-1.png)

- Confirm the Consignments that have arrived by clicking the tick box next to the relevant Consignment and then selecting Confirmed .

![how-to-split-a-manifest-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-split-a-manifest-2.png?width=670&height=260&name=how-to-split-a-manifest-2.png)

- Once confirmed, select the Options tab.
- Select Split Non-Confirmed

![how-to-split-a-manifest-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-split-a-manifest-3.png?width=670&height=260&name=how-to-split-a-manifest-3.png)

- Name the Manifest and click Save .

**![how-to-split-a-manifest-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-split-a-manifest-4.png?width=670&height=285&name=how-to-split-a-manifest-4.png)**

**To split a Manifest before it arrives:**

If you receive prior notification that the Manifest will only partially be arriving you can split the Manifest to prepare for what will arrive and what will arrive later.

- Navigate to the Manifests page (by typing in Manifests in the Search for anything bar).
- Select View from the Actions column within the relevant Manifest.
- Click the Split button from the bottom of the page.

![how-to-split-a-manifest-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-split-a-manifest-5.png?width=670&height=312&name=how-to-split-a-manifest-5.png)

- Click the Add New Manifest button at the bottom of the screen.

![how-to-split-a-manifest-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-split-a-manifest-6.png?width=670&height=182&name=how-to-split-a-manifest-6.png)

- Name the second Manifest. In the below example, the Manifest is called '2nd Coastal Coffe Company Pickup' to easily identify the Manifest that will be arriving second.

![how-to-split-a-manifest-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-split-a-manifest-7.png?width=670&height=211&name=how-to-split-a-manifest-7.png)

- Grab and move the relevant Consignment to underneath the new Manifest.
- Select Save.

![how-to-split-a-manifest-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-split-a-manifest-8.png?width=670&height=248&name=how-to-split-a-manifest-8.png)

---

<a id="manifests"></a>
## Manifests

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/manifests_

### Table of Contents

- What is a Manifest
- Manifest usecase examples
  - Example 1 - manifest pickup
  - Example 2 - manifest pickup and deliver
  - Example 3 - manifest is already at the warehouse
- How to create a Manifest
- When the Manifest arrives at the warehouse

### What is a Manifest

A Manifest in CartonCloud is a grouping of Consignments for one customer on a single date that are moving together. This function was originally built for cross-docking with the idea that the Manifest can be used to check off the receipt of Consignments during a pickup.

### Manifest usecase examples

#### **Example 1 - Manifest pickup**

#### In this example, the Customer has sent through a Manifest (via a parser) of all Consignments that need to be collected from their warehouse. Upon receiving the Manifest, CartonCloud automatically creates a Pickup Consignment ([if configured in the Customer Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/creating-automatic-pickup-consignments-for-manifests)). The Manifest Pickup Consignment can then be collected and brought back to the warehouse/depot to be sorted before being dispatched for delivery to the final destination.

![manifests-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/manifests-0.png?width=670&height=217&name=manifests-0.png)

**Example 2 - Manifest pickup and deliver**

In this example, the Customer has sent through a Manifest of all Consignments that need to be collected from their warehouse. The Manifest will be collected and then delivered in one movement.

![manifests-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/manifests-1.png?width=670&height=217&name=manifests-1.png)

#### **Example 3 - Manifest is already at the warehouse**

In this example, the Customer has sent through a Manifest of all Consignments that need to go out for delivery. The Consignments are already at the warehouse and do not need to be collected (for example, they have come from a Sale Order).

It is best to use a Manifest when you have multiple Consignments that will fit onto one truckload. It is less advantageous to use a Manifest when you have several full truckloads of Consignments.

![manifests-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/manifests-2.png?width=670&height=221&name=manifests-2.png)

### How to create a Manifest

There are two ways a Manifest can be created.

**1. Through a Parser file**

- Contact [our Support Team](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket) to set up the Manifest parser.
- Once the Manifest Parser has been added, configure the Parser to the applicable Customer (follow the steps [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/configuring-parsers-for-customers)).
- The Parser can then be imported by the Customer or yourself through the [Parse a File](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/9gGYHw) page.
- The Manifest with all associated Consignments will now be in CartonCloud.

**Downloading the Original Manifest File**

When you import a Manifest via a Parser you have the option to download the Manifest from the View Manifest Page. To do so:

- Navigate to the Manifest page, **Transport**>**Manifests**.
- Select the applicable Manifest.
- Select the **Details** tab.
- Select the blue **Download** button next to the **Download Original Manifest File** heading.

Note, this button will not appear for a Customer user if there is more than one customer associated with the Manifest.

**2. When creating a new Consignment**

Depending on what settings you have configured in your Organisation Settings will determine how you create a Manifest from a new Consignment.

To configure the Manifest settings:

- Navigate to **Organisation Settings** (More > Organisation Settings).
- Select the **Transport** tab.
- Within the **Manifest Settings** box select if you wish to **Add Consignments to Manifests by Default** by selecting **Yes (Default)** or **No**.

![manifests-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/manifests-4.png?width=670&height=410&name=manifests-4.png)

- If you select **Yes**, the **Create New Manifest**will already be selected by default when creating a new Consignment. If you select **No**, the **No Manifest**option will already be selected by default.

**To create a Manifest from a new Consignment (when the setting Add Consignments to Manifests by Default is No):**

- When creating a new Consignment, fill in the applicable information and then select the drop-down arrow next to **Advanced Options**(at the bottom of the screen).

![manifests-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/manifests-5.png?width=557&height=376&name=manifests-5.png)

You can then choose to either

Create a New Manifest

or

Add to Existing Manifest

.

![manifests-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/manifests-6.png?width=670&height=215&name=manifests-6.png)

**To create a Manifest from a new Consignment (when the setting Add Consignments to Manifests by Default is Yes):**

- When creating a new Consignment, fill in the applicable information.
- At the bottom of the screen within the Manifest section, the **Create a New Manifest** option will already be selected by default.
- Type in the **Manifest Reference**.
- Alternatively, you can add the Consignment to one of the Customer's existing recent Manifests by selecting a Manifest from the displayed list under, **Recent Manifests for Customer**.

![manifests-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/manifests-7.png?width=670&height=188&name=manifests-7.png)

### When the Manifest arrives at the warehouse

When a Manifest arrives at your warehouse you will need to manually update the status to **In Warehouse**.

To update the Manifest to **In Warehouse**:

- Navigate to the Manifests page (Transport > Manifests).
- Select the tick box next to the applicable Manifest.
- Select Update to In Warehouse .

![manifests-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/manifests-8.png?width=670&height=157&name=manifests-8.png)

To be able to allocate Consignments that are from a Manifest onto a Delivery Run, the Manifest must be updated to In Warehouse.

Once you have updated the status of the Manifest to In Warehouse you can then sort the Manifest.

To sort the Manifest:

- Select View on the applicable Manifest in the Actions column on the Manifests page.
- Select Sort Arrivals .

- Check the box next to the Consignments you wish to confirm (the ones that have arrived). If not all Consignments arrived at the same time see How to split a Manifest .

- Select Confirmed .

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/8hnv_xee2jA

---

<a id="manifests-customer"></a>
## Manifests (Customer)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/manifests-customer_

### Table of Contents

- What is a Manifest
- How to Finalise a Manifest
- How to make changes after finalising a manifest

### What is a Manifest

A Manifest in CartonCloud is a grouping of Consignments that are moving together on a single date. When adding your Consignments you have the option of adding it to a Manifest. This is useful if you have a number of Consignments moving on the same day. For example, if you require a group of Consignments to be picked up from your warehouse before going out for delivery you would be able to create one Manifest with all of these Consignments on it. Once you have added all of the required Consignments to the Manifest you need to approve or finalise the Manifest. When you finalise the Manifest it will be made available to your 3PL/CartonCloud account owner.

### How to Finalise a Manifest

- Navigate to the Manifests page, Transport > Manifests .

![manifests-customer-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/manifests-customer-0.png?width=670&height=102&name=manifests-customer-0.png)

- To check if you have an Manifests to finalise, click the Draft tab.

![manifests-customer-1-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/manifests-customer-1-1.png?width=670&height=168&name=manifests-customer-1-1.png)

- You will see any Manifests that need to be finalised here.
- Click View against the Manifest.

![manifests-customer-2-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/manifests-customer-2-1.png?width=670&height=139&name=manifests-customer-2-1.png)

- Check all Consignments and Manifest details are correct and click Finalize Manifest .

![manifests-customer-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/manifests-customer-3.png?width=670&height=265&name=manifests-customer-3.png)

### How to make changes after finalizing a manifest

If you need to make changes to the Manifest after finalising it, you will need to contact your CartonCloud account owner/3PL, they will need to make the changes themselves or revert the order to a Draft status so that you can make changes.

---

# Transport Management > Onforwarders

<a id="onforwarder-use-case-1"></a>
## Onforwarder - Use Case 1

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/onforwarder-use-case-1_

### Table of Contents

- Requirements for implementing this use case
- How to steps
  - Step 1
  - Step 2
  - Step 3

### Requirements for implementing this use case

- Your responsibility ends when the consignment is delivered to the onforwarder. You only charge your customer for local delivery.
- You have a large number of consignments which go to a specific onforwarder (completely fills a vehicle, or nearly fills a vehicle).

### How to steps

[**Step 1**:](https://help.cartoncloud.com#step-1) Create a Delivery Run specifically for each Onforwarder (and give it the name of the onforwarder). That way, it's very easy to allocate all of the consignments going to one onforwarder in one go, from one page - and it makes it very clear on your run sheets who is doing each of your onforwarder runs.

[**Step 2**](https://help.cartoncloud.com#step2): Create a 'Reverse Mapping' so the Onforwarders address is automatically loaded into every consignment that is allocated to that Onforwarder Run. This is important because then if you move consignments between runs, they'll automatically have their onforwarder address updated.

[**Step 3**](https://help.cartoncloud.com#step3): (optionally, to provide even more automation) Create a Delivery Address to Onforwarder Address Mapping to automatically map from a particular delivery address to the onforwarder address, and also create a forward mapping on the Onforwarder Address to Delivery Run so it automatically allocates to the correct Delivery Run.

**Step 1: Create a Delivery Run**

- Create a new Delivery Run from: Transport -> Delivery Runs
- Then click Add Delivery Run.
- Give the Delivery Run the same name as your onforwarder, for example: " Max Transport "
- If you have Carrier Options, S elect your Own Company as the Carrier as you won't be paying the onforwarder for the delivery.
- Select which days they operate (which days they'll pick up from you, or you'll deliver to them).
- Open the Advanced Options and from the Onforwarder section, select Yes .
- Set the Final Consignment Delivery Status to Delivered
- Set the Consignment Status When Delivered by App to Delivered
- Lastly, select the Rate Zone you want to charge the customer for delivering to the Onforwarder. Typically this would be a Metro Rate Zone as the Onforwarder is within the city. By doing this, the Rate Zone you select will be used instead of the Rate Zone calculated from the Delivery Address.

![onforwarder-use-case-1-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/onforwarder-use-case-1-0.png?width=670&height=308&name=onforwarder-use-case-1-0.png)
**Step 2: Create a Reverse Mapping for the Delivery Run to the Onforwarders Address**

- Create a new Address to Delivery Run Mapping from:
- More -> Site Map -> Address to Delivery Run Mappings
- Click Add Mapping

![onforwarder-use-case-1-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/onforwarder-use-case-1-1.png?width=485&height=110&name=onforwarder-use-case-1-1.png)

- Then create a Reverse Onforwarder Address Mapping. It's called a 'Reverse Mapping' because by setting the flow direction to point to the left, it causes all consignments allocated to the Max Transport Delivery Run to be given the Onforwarder Address of Max Transport, 1 Carton Way, Carole Park, QLD . (Conversely, a forward mapping would cause any consignment given the onforwarder address of Max Transport to automatically go onto the Max Transport Delivery Run).

![onforwarder-use-case-1-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/onforwarder-use-case-1-2.png?width=527&height=350&name=onforwarder-use-case-1-2.png)

Now, any consignment which is allocated to the **Max Transport** Delivery Run will automatically be given the Onforwarder Address of **Max Transport**, and will also be automatically charged as a Metro delivery.

**Step 3: Delivery Address to Delivery Run Mapping**

This step is optional, however, it's very useful if you're constantly sending stock to the same delivery address via an onforwarder and wish to automate this process.

Mapping the Delivery Address to the Delivery Run, so consignments going to a delivery Address of "**Sydney Packaging & Labels, , Unit 2, 109 Percival Rd, SMITHFIELD, New South Wales, Australia**" will automatically go onto the **Max Transport**Delivery Run, and therefore be given the Onforwarder Address of: **Max Transport, 1 Carton Way, CAROLE PARK, , Queensland, Australia**. (through the Reverse Mapping we created above).

Again, create an Address to Delivery Run Mapping.
This time, however, select:

- Address Type: Delivery
- Flow Direction: -> (so the Delivery Address maps to the Delivery Run) .

![onforwarder-use-case-1-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/onforwarder-use-case-1-3.png?width=573&height=374&name=onforwarder-use-case-1-3.png)
Click **Create** and you're all done! Now, when a consignment is loaded in from the Manifest it'll automatically perform all of those allocations:
![onforwarder-use-case-1-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/onforwarder-use-case-1-4.png?width=555&height=433&name=onforwarder-use-case-1-4.png)

---

<a id="onforwarder-use-case-2"></a>
## Onforwarder - Use Case 2

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/onforwarder-use-case-2_

### Table of Contents

- Requirements for implementing this use case
- How to steps
- Set up for only charging to the Onforwarder address

### Requirements for implementing this use case

- Your responsibility ends when the Consignment is delivered to the Onforwarder and you will charge the customer to the end destination. If you only want to charge to the Onforwarder address, please see here.
- You have a small number of Consignments going to the Onforwarder and wish to allocate the Consignments to regulalr Delivery Runs. You want the Onforwarder address to be inserted automatically and the CartonCloud handle the allocations based on the Onforwarders postcode and suburb.

### How to steps

To set this up in CartonCloud you will need to create a Delivery Address to Onforwarder Address Mapping (A2A):

- More -> Site Map -> Delivery Address to Onforwarder Address Mapping
- Click Add Mapping

![onforwarder-use-case-2-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/onforwarder-use-case-2-0.png?width=670&height=117&name=onforwarder-use-case-2-0.png)

- Simply create a Mapping from the desired Delivery Address, ie: Sydney Packaging & Labels, Unit 2, 109 Percival Rd, SMITHFIELD, New South Wales, Australia to the Onforwarder Address: Max Transport, 1 Carton Way, CAROLE PARK, Queensland, Australia

![onforwarder-use-case-2-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/onforwarder-use-case-2-1.png?width=670&height=262&name=onforwarder-use-case-2-1.png)

- Now, any consignment which is manifested with the Delivery Address of Sydney Packaging & Labels, , Unit 2, 109 Percival Rd, SMITHFIELD, , New South Wales, Australia will be automatically given the Onforwarder Address: Max Transport, 1 Carton Way, CAROLE PARK, Queensland, Australia , however it will remain on your regular WEST Delivery Runs simply based on the Suburb and Postcode of the Onforwarder Address (via Delivery Zones).

![onforwarder-use-case-2-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/onforwarder-use-case-2-2.png?width=580&height=453&name=onforwarder-use-case-2-2.png)

### Set up for only charging to the Onforwarder address

- Navigate to the relevant Delivery Run.
- Select the Details tab and then Edit .
- Open the Advanced Options and untick 'If Onforwarder Address Exists, charge for delivery to the Onforwarders Address (untick if you want to charge to the delivery location always).'
- Click Save.

---

<a id="onforwarder-use-case-3"></a>
## Onforwarder - Use Case 3

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/onforwarder-use-case-3_

### Table of Contents

- Requirements for implementing this use case
- How to steps

Please note that if your CartonCloud account was created after 1 July 2019 the below functionality will not be available. Suppliers are only available for the WMS and are no available for Carriers / Drivers. If you have any questions please use [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/) and lodge a case with our Service Desk.

### Requirements for implementing this use case

- ​​​​​​​Your responsibility ends when the consignment is delivered to the end customer (Delivery Address). This also means you're required to get the POD back from the Onforwarder when they deliver the consignment.
- You pay the onforwarder for their part of the movement and bill the customer for the whole job.

In this use case:

- We'll create a new **Carrier** for the onforwarder, and then create a **Supplier**which is linked to this carrier for billing purposes (knowing what we're supposed to pay the onforwarder, and also preventing being double-billed for Consignments).
- We'll create a **Delivery Run** specifically for the new onforwarder (and give it the name of the onforwarder), linked to the new Carrier. As CartonCloud is based around **Delivery Runs** as a core concept we use Delivery Run Allocation to manage which Carrier handled the consignment.
- We'll then create a '**Reverse Mapping**' so the Onforwarders address is automatically loaded into every consignment that is allocated to that Onforwarder Run. This is important because then if you move consignments between runs, they'll automatically have their onforwarder address updated.(optionally, to provide even more automation) We'll create a **Delivery Address to Delivery Run Mapping** to automatically map from a particular delivery address to the new Delivery Run.

### ​​​​​​​How to steps

**Step 1: Create a Carrier and Supplier**

This step is required so we're able to accurately track onforwarder charges (expenses) associated with each Consignment, and create Bills for those expenses. This is very important to prevent being double-billed by an onforwarder for a particular consignment (notorious in freight, and very costly to your company).

- **Enable CartonCloud's Multi-Carrier support (if not enabled already):** To do this, select **More** in the main menu, followed by **Organisation Settings**then select the **Features & Options**tab**.**
Tick the box labelled **Multi-Carrier Enabled**
- **Create a new Carrier:** To do this, type "Carriers" in**Search for anything!**
Then, click**+Add Carrier**. Give the Carrier the name of your Onforwarder (For Example, **Max** **Transport**).
Tick the box labelled **Onforwarder**

**Create a new Supplier:**

Select **Contacts** in the Main menu, followed by**Suppliers** in the drop-down menu.
Then click **Add Supplier**
Give the Supplier the same name as your Carrier, and select the Warehouses you want to service the Supplier from.

Once created, link the Supplier with the Carrier:

![onforwarder-use-case-3-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/onforwarder-use-case-3-0.png?width=342&height=293&name=onforwarder-use-case-3-0.png)

![onforwarder-use-case-3-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/onforwarder-use-case-3-1.png?width=387&height=296&name=onforwarder-use-case-3-1.png)
**Step 2: Create a Delivery Run**

- Create a new Delivery Run from: Transport -> Delivery Runs
- Then click Add Delivery Run.
- Give the Delivery Run the same name as your on-forwarder: for example, " Max Transport "
- Select your newly created carrier as the Carrier .
- Select which days they operate (which days they'll pickup from you, or you'll deliver to them).
- Open the Advanced Options and from the Onforwarder section, select Inherit from Carrier .
- Set the Final Consignment Delivery Status to Delivered
- Set the Consignment Status When Delivered by App to With On Forwarder - this is important as it will ensure when consignments are signed out as delivered on the App, they'll only update to 'With On Forwarder' (as you're awaiting signed paperwork to be returned by the Onforwarder before updating to Delivered).
- Leave the Rate Zone set to Use default based on Suburb/Postcode

![onforwarder-use-case-3-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/onforwarder-use-case-3-2.png?width=670&height=306&name=onforwarder-use-case-3-2.png)
**Step 3: Create a Reverse Mapping for the Delivery Run to the Onforwarders Address:**

- Create a new Address to Delivery Run Mapping from:
- More -> Site Map -> Address to Delivery Run Mappings

![onforwarder-use-case-3-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/onforwarder-use-case-3-3.png?width=529&height=120&name=onforwarder-use-case-3-3.png)

- Then create a Reverse Onforwarder Address Mapping. It's called a 'Reverse Mapping' because by setting the flow direction to point to the left, it causes all consignments allocated to the Max Transport Delivery Run to be given the Onforwarder Address of Max Transport, 1 Carton Way, Carole Park, QLD . (Conversely, a forward mapping would cause any consignment given the onforwarder address of Max Transport to automatically go onto the Max Transport Delivery Run).

![onforwarder-use-case-3-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/onforwarder-use-case-3-4.png?width=455&height=295&name=onforwarder-use-case-3-4.png)

- Now, any consignment which is allocated to the Max Transport Delivery Run will automatically be given the Onforwarder Address of Max Transport.

**Step 4: (OPTIONAL) Delivery Address to Delivery Run Mapping**

- This step is optional, however, it's very useful if you're constantly sending stock to the same delivery address via an onforwarder and wish to automate this process.
- Mapping the Delivery Address to the Delivery Run, so consignments going to a delivery Address of " Sydney Packaging & Labels, Unit 2, 109 Percival Rd, SMITHFIELD, New South Wales, Australia " will automatically go onto the Max Transport Delivery Run, and therefore be given the Onforwarder Address of Max Transport, 1 Carton Way, CAROLE PARK, Queensland, Australia . (through the Reverse Mapping we created above).
- Again, create an Address to Delivery Run Mapping. This time, however, select:
- Address Type: Delivery (so the Delivery Address maps to the Delivery Run) .

![onforwarder-use-case-3-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/onforwarder-use-case-3-5.png?width=566&height=366&name=onforwarder-use-case-3-5.png)

- Flow Direction: -->
- Click Create and you're done. Now, when a consignment is loaded in from the Manifest it'll automatically perform all of those allocations:

![onforwarder-use-case-3-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/onforwarder-use-case-3-6.png?width=468&height=365&name=onforwarder-use-case-3-6.png)

---

<a id="onforwarders-1"></a>
## Onforwarders

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/onforwarders-1_

### Table of Contents

- What is an Onforwarder
- How does CartonCloud handle Onforwarders
- [Carrier Access and Visibility](https://help.cartoncloud.com#carrier-access-and-visibility)
- Onforwarder Configurations
- Other useful configuration steps for Onforwarders
- Useful Onforwarder Videos

### What is an Onforwarder

An onforwarder is another company that will be handling the delivery on behalf of your company at some point in the Consignment's journey. For example, in areas where there is large distances between places, rather than one transport company covering all the deliveries for their customers, the transport company will use an onforwarder to deliver some of their customers consignments to areas that are not already going to. Using an onforwarder has it's advantages, however, it can also cause complications with multiple addresses and for charging. CartonCloud has specific features and configurations with these factors in mind in order to create a smooth onforwarder process.

### How does CartonCloud handle Onforwarders

- **Onforwarder Addresses:** In CartonCloud, you can make dealing with Onforwarders easier (and even automated) through the use of Onforwarder Addresses. Onforwarder Addresses are used as an intermediate address, between the Pickup Address (or your Warehouse Address), and the Final Delivery Address. See [Onforwarder Addresses](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Onforwarder-Addresses)for more information.
- **Onforwarder allocations and charging via Delivery Run mappings**(see below for more information)

### Carrier Access and Visibility

When a Carrier is set up as an Onforwarder in CartonCloud, the Carrier can only access consignments associated with them across all pages, including Manifests, Delivery Runs, and Run Sheets. The Carrier can also only access drivers that belong to the same Carrier.

⚠️**Before you begin** — the following requirements must be met before configuring an onforwarder:
•    The carrier must have the Onforwarder setting enabled in CartonCloud.

### Onforwarder Configurations

There are a number of ways in which Onforwarders can be configured in your CartonCloud account, through the use of [Delivery Runs](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Delivery-Runs), [Address to Delivery Run Mapping (A2DR)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Address#A2DR-mapping)and [Delivery Address to Onforwarder Address Mapping (A2A)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Address#A2A-mapping) to match your business processes and automate onforwarder allocations.

In order to determine how Onforwarders will be set up in your CartonCloud account you need to know how your Onforwarders operate with regards to billing as this impacts how they should be configured within CartonCloud:

- Scenario A : you don't manage or charge your customer for the work performed by the Onforwarder (the onforwarder already has a relationship with your customer, and charges them directly). Your responsibility ends when you deliver to the Onforwarder and you only charge the customer for local delivery. For this scenario there are two options for managing the Delivery Runs and Allocations and this depends on volume and internal processes:
  - Scenario A:1: You have a large number of Consignments which go to a specific Onforwarder (completely fills a vehicle, or nearly fills a vehicle).
  - Set up guide: See [Onforwarder - Use Case 1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Onforwarder-Use-Case-1) for set up instructions

-
  - Scenario A:2: You have a few Consignments going to the Onforwarder and want to allocate the Consignments to one of your regular Delivery Runs.
  - Set up guide: See [Onforwarder - Use Case 2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Onforwarder-Use-Case-2) for set up instructions
- Scenario B: you manage and charge the customer for all of the work performed, and also pay the onforwarder directly. You're responsible for the Consignment all the way to the final delivery destination and must receive back a signed POD from the onforwarder.
- Set up guide: See [Onforwarder - Use Case 3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Onforwarder-Use-Case-3) for set up instructions

### Other useful configuration steps for Onforwarders

- Using QR codes to automatically attach a POD to a Consignment :  CartonCloud provides a designated email address that can be used to receive signed PODs from onforwarders/carriers, provided the signed documents contain a QR Code overlay. This provides a simple way for onforwarders to send back completed PODs with minimal effort, increasing the chance of you receiving them back quickly. See Using QR codes to automatically attach a POD to a Consignment
- Making Carriers visible to Customers and giving them aliases
- Making Delivery Runs visible to Customers and giving them aliases

### Useful Onforwarder Videos

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/9iyEPWmpTso

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/ZgYtjxXQCco

---

# Transport Management > Run Sheets

<a id="how-to-email-a-runsheet-to-a-driver"></a>
## How to email a Runsheet to a Driver

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-email-a-runsheet-to-a-driver_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits
- Solution 1 - automatic email through the driver set up
- Solution 2 - manually email the runsheet from the drivers page

### Purpose

To email your Runsheets to the allocated Driver either automatically on a daily week-day basis or manually at ad-hoc times.

### Benefits

- Ensures your Drivers have a copy of the correct Run Sheet.
- Reduces admin time of having to download each Run Sheet and then email it to each Driver.
- Eliminates the need to print the Run Sheet.

### ​​​​​​​Solution 1 - Automatic email through the Driver set up

You can set up your Drivers to receive their Run Sheets via email every day at 19:00 AEDT.

The time in which the email is sent each day is not configurable.

Steps to enable the Driver to receive their Run Sheet daily:

- Navigate to the Users page by selecting **Contacts**>**Users.**
- Select the applicable Driver.
- ​​​​​​​Select the Edit button at the bottom of the screen.

![how-to-email-a-runsheet-to-a-driver-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-email-a-runsheet-to-a-driver-0.png?width=626&height=331&name=how-to-email-a-runsheet-to-a-driver-0.png)

- Scroll down to the **Roles** heading and within the **Driver** role section tick**Automatically Email Run Sheets to Driver.**

![how-to-email-a-runsheet-to-a-driver-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-email-a-runsheet-to-a-driver-1.png?width=617&height=326&name=how-to-email-a-runsheet-to-a-driver-1.png)

- The Run Sheet will now be emailed to the email address set up for that Driver every day from Monday through to Friday at 19:00 AEDT.

### ​​​​​​​Solution 2 - Manually email the Runsheet from the Drivers page

- Navigate to the Drivers pages by selecting Contacts>Drivers.
- Select the applicable Driver.
- Select the **Run Sheets** tab.
- Click the **Email Run Sheets to Driver** button at the top of the screen.

![how-to-email-a-runsheet-to-a-driver-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-email-a-runsheet-to-a-driver-2.png?width=670&height=260&name=how-to-email-a-runsheet-to-a-driver-2.png)

- Select the date ranges for the Run Sheets you wish to include and then click the **Send Email** button.

![how-to-email-a-runsheet-to-a-driver-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/how-to-email-a-runsheet-to-a-driver-3.png?width=413&height=242&name=how-to-email-a-runsheet-to-a-driver-3.png)

- The email will then be sent to the email address set up for that Driver.

---

<a id="run-sheet-adhoc-charges"></a>
## Run Sheet Adhoc Charges

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/run-sheet-adhoc-charges_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Loading run sheet adhoc charges
- Where to submit run sheet adhoc charges

### Purpose

Within the CartonCloud mobile apps, drivers can choose to submit Adhoc Charges against Run Sheets, assuming that Adhoc Charges for the Run Sheet have been configured in the web app.

### Loading run sheet adhoc charges

Run Sheet Adhoc Charge details get loaded when the user refreshes the Consignment list. Existing values for Adhoc Charges will not be deleted on refreshing Consignments unless a newer Adhoc Charge value is available in the CartonCloud system. Running timers are never deleted when refreshing from the server.

This makes it possible to preload Adhoc Charges for Run Sheets in the web app that will appear on the driver's mobile app on refreshing Consignments and entering the Adhoc Charge view for a Run Sheet.

For more information on how to Adhoc Charges in the CartonCloud web app, check out these articles: [Adhoc Charge Setup](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Adhoc+Charge+Setup), [View Rate Card](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/View+Rate+Card).

### Where to Submit Run Sheet Adhoc Charges

First step to be able to submit Run Sheet Adhoc Charges is to display Run Sheets in the consignment list.

**For more information on how to split the consignment list by Run Sheets, check out this article: [Consignment Sorting And Filtering - Run Sheet](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Consignment+Sorting+and+Filtering#ConsignmentSortingandFiltering-RunSheet)**

Once the consignment list is separated by Run Sheets, any Run Sheet that has the option of submitting Adhoc Charges against it will display an appropriate Adhoc Charge button on the right-hand side, next to the up/down arrow.

![run-sheet-adhoc-charges-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-adhoc-charges-0.png?width=289&height=595&name=run-sheet-adhoc-charges-0.png)

An Adhoc Charge timer can be kept running while navigating away from a Run Sheet Adhoc Charge View. It will keep running until stopped or until the Run Sheet is no longer visible in the job list.

On selecting the Run Sheet Adhoc Charge button, the Adhoc Charge view will open and present the available Adhoc Charge options.

![run-sheet-adhoc-charges-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-adhoc-charges-1.png?width=276&height=566&name=run-sheet-adhoc-charges-1.png)

---

<a id="run-sheet-filter"></a>
## Run Sheet Filter

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/run-sheet-filter_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Filter access
- Filter options
- Applied filter

### Purpose

When viewing the list of Sale Orders in the CartonCloud mobile app, a Run Sheet filter can be applied, allowing the user to only see the Sale Orders associated with the selected Run Sheet.

### Filter Access

To access the Run Sheet filter, select the filter (funnel) button in the top bar while in the Sale Order list.

![run-sheet-filter-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-filter-0.png?width=237&height=476&name=run-sheet-filter-0.png)

### Filter Options

Once the Run Sheet filter has been activated, a drop down field will be enabled, displaying the filter options currently available (including **Run Sheet**).
![run-sheet-filter-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-filter-1.png?width=424&height=408&name=run-sheet-filter-1.png)
On selecting the **Run Sheet** option, a second drop down field is made available, displaying a list of Run Sheets that the user can filter by. This list is based on all Sale Orders that are currently in **In Progress** or **Awaiting Pick & Pack**status and the Run Sheets that are associated with these Sale Orders.

![run-sheet-filter-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-filter-2.png?width=206&height=414&name=run-sheet-filter-2.png)

### Applied Filter

Once a Run Sheet filter has been applied, a banner will be displayed at the top of the Sale Order list, highlighting the Run Sheet filter that has been applied.

![run-sheet-filter-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-filter-3.png?width=251&height=504&name=run-sheet-filter-3.png)
The applied filter can be cancelled by either tapping the **X** button on the banner, or by once again opening the filter view and either adjusting the filter or switching off the Run Sheet filter altogether.
![run-sheet-filter-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-filter-4.png?width=404&height=386&name=run-sheet-filter-4.png)

---

<a id="run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building"></a>
## Run Sheet Statuses & Pallet Building

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- To enable run sheet statuses
- To use the statuses on the listing table
- To use the statuses in the run sheet details screen

### Purpose

Run Sheet Statuses are useful if you're doing things like building Pallets for your drivers, and need to keep track of the statuses of the Run Building process.

### To enable run sheet statuses

1. To enable the Run Sheet Statuses feature you will need to select **More** in the main menu, followed by **Organisational Settings**in the drop-down menu**.**Within Organisation settings select the **Features and Options** tab.
2. Check the **Show Run Sheet Statuses** checkbox and click **Save**.

### To use the statuses on the listing table

- Navigate to the Run Sheets screen.

![run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-0.png?width=670&height=274&name=run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-0.png)

- You will notice there is a Status column in the table. This status tracks the status of the given run sheet.

![run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-1.png?width=670&height=274&name=run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-1.png)

- At the bottom of the table, you will also notice there is now another button for updating Run Sheet status.

![run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-2.png?width=670&height=111&name=run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-2.png)

- To update the status make a selection using the checkboxes and then click the Update Run Sheet Status button and select which status you would like to update the Run Sheet to.

![run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-3.png?width=670&height=122&name=run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-3.png)

- The page will reload and once done you will see that the Status for the select row or rows has been updated to your selection.

![run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-4.png?width=670&height=82&name=run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-4.png)

### To use the statuses in the Run Sheet details screen

- View a Run Sheet. You will notice that in the Details tab there is now a new section on the right side.

![run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-5.png?width=670&height=238&name=run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-5.png)

- This is the status for this Run Sheet. It can be updated by clicking on the Update Run Sheet Status button and choosing a status just like on the listing table. When choosing a status a prompt will appear new the top of the browser asking for confirmation of the status update.

![run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-6.png?width=670&height=243&name=run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-6.png)

**Pallet Building**
 ![run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-7.png?width=670&height=154&name=run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-7.png)

- Once a Run Sheet is in Ready to Build or Building Statuses, you can then enter the Run Building Screen. This is used by staff who build pallets for loading into the trucks. The screen allows them to ensure that each consignment on the Run Sheet is loaded correctly.
- Within the Run Sheet Building Screen your warehouse staff can specify which consignments have been loaded onto which pallet. Begin by pressing the "Confirm" button beside the jobs, then down the bottom select the Pallet that they're being loaded onto. This will then allocate the Consignments to those pallets. Once they've been allocated a 2nd pallet will be created which may be used for additional consignments.

![run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-8.png?width=670&height=204&name=run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-8.png)

![run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-9.png?width=670&height=266&name=run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-9.png)

- With pallets created, you can now filter into each Pallet to see what is on it. Right now we're looking at Unallocated Consignments (those not allocated to a Pallet)

![run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-10](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-10.png?width=670&height=375&name=run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-10.png)

- Clicking on a particular pallet will show what is on that pallet. To unallocate a consignment from a Pallet simply press the Confirm Checkbox again to "Unallocate" it. It will then disappear from the screen as it is taken off the pallet.

![run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-11](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-11.png?width=670&height=285&name=run-sheet-statuses-pallet-building-11.png)

- Once you've finished building pallets, click Complete Building , the status will then update to "Built".

---

<a id="run-sheets"></a>
## Run Sheets

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/run-sheets_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Creating run sheets
  - Creating run sheets whilst allocating consignments (from the consignments page)
  - Creating Run Sheets from the Run Sheets page
- Creating run sheets from the run sheets page
- Downloading the run sheet
- Run sheet list configuration
- Run Sheet List Sorting
- Sorting consignments within a run sheet (in map view)

### Purpose

Run Sheets are utilised to allocate consignments to a driver. The Run Sheet contains all of the consignments going with a single driver for that day. For example, deliveries for a single day on the [Delivery Run](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Delivery+Runs) "Gold Coast" might be split up across multiple Run Sheets (East, North, West), as each Run sheet is allocated to a different driver.

For more information on allocating consignments to drivers see the [Allocating Consignments to Drivers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Allocating+Consignments+to+Drivers)section of the setup guide.

To customise the Run Sheet for either an individual Customer or all your Customers please see [Document Templates](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Document-Templates?r=53&ui-knowledge-components-aura-actions.KnowledgeArticleVersionCreateDraftFromOnlineAction.createDraftFromOnlineArticle=1)[https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/LAiYHw](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/LAiYHw) and [Document Template Placeholders.](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Document-Template-Placeholders?r=53&ui-knowledge-components-aura-actions.KnowledgeArticleVersionCreateDraftFromOnlineAction.createDraftFromOnlineArticle=1)

Creating Run Sheets

There are multiple ways in which Run Sheets can be created. The method you utilise will depend on how you allocate consignments within CartonCloud.

You can create Run Sheets from within the Run Sheets or Consignments page. It is recommended that you create your Run Sheets within the consignments page whilst allocating your Consignments, this is the most logical and time-efficient method. If you have a large number of Consignments and/or Delivery Runs you may wish to use the [Bulk Allocation](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Bulk+Allocation) function.

If you would prefer to have the Run Sheet created before you start allocating consignments, then you can do this from within the Run Sheets page.

#### **Creating Run Sheets whilst allocating consignments (from the consignments page)**

- Once on the consignments page, select the consignments you wish to allocate (do so by selecting the tick box next to the relevant consignment).
- Select **Move** from the top bar.
- You will now have two options. You can either assign the consignment to an existing Run Sheet or create a new one.

![run-sheets-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheets-0.png?width=670&height=269&name=run-sheets-0.png)

- The date that you have selected will dictate what existing Run Sheets you have to choose from.
- If you wish to create a new Run Sheet, fill the applicable fields in the 'Create New Runsheet' window.
- If you would like to allocate the consignment to an existing Run Sheet, click the title of the existing Run Sheet in the 'Existing Run Sheets' window.
- Select **Save** in the pop-out window.

#### **Creating Run Sheets from the Run Sheets page**

- Once on the Run Sheets page, select Add in the top left corner.

![run-sheets-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheets-1.png?width=670&height=107&name=run-sheets-1.png)

Fill in the following fields:

| **Field** | **Example** | **Info** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Delivery Run | East | This field is optional and if provided all consignments allocated to the Run Sheet will have their Delivery Run overwritten with this value. This is useful when working with [Onforwarder Addresses](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Onforwarder-Addresses?r=53&ui-knowledge-components-aura-actions.KnowledgeArticleVersionCreateDraftFromOnlineAction.createDraftFromOnlineArticle=1) |
| Carrier | Your Tenancy Name | Allows you to assign which carrier will complete the Run Sheets. For your own drivers, the carrier would be your own tenancy name. |
| Name | East - AM Run | A name given to the run, normally to describe what it is for. |
| Date | 2017-02-5 | The date the run is taking place. |
| Driver | Douglas Adams | The name of the driver performing the run. |
| Vehicle | XYZ123 | This field is optional and if utilised will assign a vehicle to the run. It can only be selected if Vehicles - [Setting up Vehicles in CartonCloud](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Setting-up-Vehicles-in-CartonCloud?r=53&ui-knowledge-components-aura-actions.KnowledgeArticleVersionCreateDraftFromOnlineAction.createDraftFromOnlineArticle=1). |
| ID | 10201 | This field is automatically assigned and is an incrementing ID for the Run Sheet. **Does not require user input.** |

### Downloading the Run Sheet

CartonCloud allows you to have your Runsheets automatically emailed to your Drivers, saving you time and reducing errors. For information on how to email Runsheets to your Drivers see - [How to email a Runsheet to a Driver](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/How-to-email-a-Runsheet-to-a-Driver?r=53&ui-knowledge-components-aura-actions.KnowledgeArticleVersionCreateDraftFromOnlineAction.createDraftFromOnlineArticle=1)

**To download the Run Sheet:**

**From the Run Sheets page:**

- Navigate to the Run Sheets page, Transport > Run Sheets .
- Use the select column to tick the relevant Run Sheets.

![run-sheets-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheets-2.png?width=670&height=165&name=run-sheets-2.png)

- Click Export .
- Select a download option from the Export drop-down menu.

![run-sheets-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheets-3.png?width=670&height=220&name=run-sheets-3.png)

**From the View Run Sheet page:**

- Navigate to the Run Sheets page, Transport > Run Sheets .
- Within the Details tab and Export field, select Export Run Sheet .

### Run Sheets List Configuration

The Run Sheets List view can be configured and customised by adding and removing columns as required. This is useful if you wish to view completed and incomplete Run Sheets in the same view.

The data column options include the different consignment item variables (e.g pallets, cubic (m3), quantity, etc.). For each variable, you can select the total, the number of completed (delivered), and/or the number of incompleted (not delivered) of that certain variable.

The data columns you select will apply to the Filter, All, and Ready to Build tabs within the Run Sheets list view.

**To configure the Run Sheets list;**

- Select the configuration cog icon in the top right corner.

![run-sheets-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheets-4.png?width=670&height=107&name=run-sheets-4.png)

- A pop-out window will appear. From here you will be able to choose the data columns to be visible on the Run Sheets List view.
- To add a data column, click the tick box next to the relevant data.

![run-sheets-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheets-5.png?width=381&height=220&name=run-sheets-5.png)

- To remove the data column, un-select the tick box.
- To view completed and non-completed Run Sheets, select the 'Complete' data column. You can also include the '#Incomplete Consignments' and '#Complete Consignments' data columns to track the number of consignments that have been delivered and the number left to be delivered.
- Select Save at the bottom of the window once all relevant data columns have been selected.

### Run Sheet List Sorting

From the Run Sheet List view you can sort standard columns on the page. This allows you to view the Run Sheets in an order that is applicable for you. The columns you can sort by include - ID, Name, Delivery Run, Driver and Vehicle.

![run-sheets-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheets-6.png?width=670&height=89&name=run-sheets-6.png)

### Sorting Consignments within a Run Sheet (in map view)

Within the Run Sheets page, you have the ability to re-order consignments on a Run Sheet through the map view.

To view a Run Sheet and re-order consignments through the map view;

- Select the Run Sheet you wish to view by ticking the tick box in the 'Select' column.
- Select **Sort Run Sheets** from the top bar above the column headings.

![run-sheets-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/run-sheets-7.png?width=670&height=144&name=run-sheets-7.png)

- You will then be directed to the map view where you will see all consignments (for that Run Sheet) locations on a map.

- To re-order the consignments on the Run Sheet, click the consignment name until a red box appears around it. Grab and hold the consignment and drag to re-order.

- Select **Save Consignment Order**at the bottom of the screen.

### View Run Sheet page

For information on how to use the View Run Sheet page click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Run-Sheets) .

---

### Table of Contents

### Details

The details tab gives an overview of the Run Sheet. From here you can edit the Run Sheet, update Consignment statuses, download documents, delete the Run Sheet and more.
![view-run-sheets-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-run-sheets-0.png?width=670&height=280&name=view-run-sheets-0.png)

### Other functions

| **Function** | **Description** |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Edit | To edit the Run Sheet. |  |
| Update Consignment Status | Select the status you want to update the Consignment to from the drop-down arrow. This will update the status of all Consignments on the Run Sheet. If you wish to only update a selection of Consignments, use the Consignments & Statistics tab. |  |
| Download | **Consignment Invoices:**download the Consignment Invoices for all Consignments on the Run Sheet.  **Connotes (where invoices don't exist)**: to download the connotes associated with the Consignments that do not have invoices for. **Consignment Invoices and Connotes (where invoices don't exist)**: to download the Consignment invoices and connotes (for the consignments that do not have invoices associated with them) for all Consignments on the Run Sheet. | **Consignment Invoices:**download the Consignment Invoices for all Consignments on the Run Sheet.  **Connotes (where invoices don't exist)**: to download the connotes associated with the Consignments that do not have invoices for. **Consignment Invoices and Connotes (where invoices don't exist)**: to download the Consignment invoices and connotes (for the consignments that do not have invoices associated with them) for all Consignments on the Run Sheet. |
| **Consignment Invoices:**download the Consignment Invoices for all Consignments on the Run Sheet.  **Connotes (where invoices don't exist)**: to download the connotes associated with the Consignments that do not have invoices for. **Consignment Invoices and Connotes (where invoices don't exist)**: to download the Consignment invoices and connotes (for the consignments that do not have invoices associated with them) for all Consignments on the Run Sheet. |  |  |
| More | **Recalculate Consignment Charges:** will recalculate charges for all Consignments on the Run Sheet.  **Reset Consignment Ordering**: will reset the Consignment order to the default order which is based on their addresses.  **Run Sequence Setup:**to set up the sequence of the Run Sheet. |  |
| Delete | To delete the Run Sheet. |  |

### Charges

If there is an invoicing customer assigned to the Run Sheet, charges can be assigned to the Run Sheet.

#### **To assign an invoicing customer to the Run Sheet:**

- Navigate to the Charges tab on the Run Sheet.
- Click edit .

![view-run-sheets-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-run-sheets-1.png?width=670&height=130&name=view-run-sheets-1.png)

- Select a customer from the Customer (for invoicing only) drop-down menu.

![view-run-sheets-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-run-sheets-2.png?width=670&height=96&name=view-run-sheets-2.png)

- Scroll down and select Save .
- Upon navigating back to the Charges tab on the Run Sheet you will now be able to add Income and Adhoc Charges to the Run Sheet.

![view-run-sheets-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-run-sheets-3.png?width=670&height=311&name=view-run-sheets-3.png)

### Consignments & Statistics

From this tab, you can see all Consignments on the Run Sheet, add Consignments, remove Consignments and update their status.

**![view-run-sheets-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-run-sheets-4.png?width=670&height=305&name=view-run-sheets-4.png)**

**To add a Consignment:**

- Select the green **+Add** button under the Consignments heading.

![view-run-sheets-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-run-sheets-5.png?width=670&height=284&name=view-run-sheets-5.png)

- Use the check box to select what Consignments you would like to add to the Run Sheet.

- Click **Add Selected Consignments**.

**To move a Consignment:**

- Use the check box to select the Consignment you wish to move.
- Select **Move**.

![view-run-sheets-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-run-sheets-6.png?width=670&height=307&name=view-run-sheets-6.png)

- Create a new Run Sheet or select an existing Run Sheet in the far right panel.

![view-run-sheets-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-run-sheets-6.png?width=670&height=307&name=view-run-sheets-6.png)

- Scroll down and select Save .

**To group Consignments:**

- Select the Consignments you wish to group using the checkboxes.
- Select the blue **Group Consignments**button.
 ![view-run-sheets-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-run-sheets-7.png?width=670&height=341&name=view-run-sheets-7.png)

**To remove Consignments:**

- Select the Consignments you wish to remove from the Run Sheet using the checkboxes.
- Select the yellow **Remove** button.

![view-run-sheets-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-run-sheets-8.png?width=670&height=307&name=view-run-sheets-8.png)

**To download the Connote:**

- Select the Consignments you wish to download the Connote for using the checkboxes.
- Select the green **Connote** button.
 ![view-run-sheets-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-run-sheets-9.png?width=670&height=307&name=view-run-sheets-9.png)

**To update the status of the Consignment:**

- Select the Consignments you wish to update the status of using the checkboxes.
- Select**Update Status** and select the status you wish to update the Consignment to.

![view-run-sheets-10](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/view-run-sheets-10.png?width=670&height=307&name=view-run-sheets-10.png)

### Map

From the Map view, you can change the order of the Run Sheet and see all Consignments on the Run Sheet in a map view.

**To rearrange the order of the Run Sheet:**

- Drag and drop the deliveries in the right-hand pane. As you adjust the order the pin numbers against each delivery will change.
- Click **Save Consignment Order** to save the new order.
- Click on the pins to see the Consignment details.
