# Transport Management > Transport Lanes

<a id="setting-up-transport-lanes"></a>
## Setting up Transport Lanes

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-transport-lanes_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Prerequisites
- Steps to create a Transport Lane
- Using the Transport Lanes page
- Example Delivery Run Mappings

### Purpose

Please note that if your CartonCloud account was created prior to 1 July 2019 the below functionality may not be available at this stage. If you would like to discuss migrating to the newer version of the CartonCloud TMS, please use [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com) and lodge a case with our Service Desk.

To create your [Transport Lane](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/transport-lanes)follow the below steps and ensure you have met the specified prerequisites.

### Prerequisites

- [Create a Transport Zone Set](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-transport-zone-sets)
- [Set up your Delivery Runs](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-add-a-delivery-run)
- Ensure there is no other Delivery Run Mappings that will force the Transport Lane mapping to be overridden. See [When Delivery Run Mapping is overridden](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+Transport+Lanes#SettingupTransportLanes-delivery) for more information.

### Steps to create a Transport Lane​​​​​​​

**1. Add a new Transport Lane**

- Select **Add Transport Lane** from the top left corner.
- A new screen will appear (as seen below). From here, you will be able to set up your Transport Lane.

![setting-up-transport-lanes-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-transport-lanes-0.png?width=670&height=335&name=setting-up-transport-lanes-0.png)

**2. Set up your Transport Lane**

To set up your Transport Lane follow the below steps:

- Fill in the below fields:
  - Name - we suggest using a descriptive name, for example, Sydney South to Sydney North.
  - Effective Date - to use this lane immediately, use today's date.
  - Expiry Date.
- Select the **From** and **To** zone that you wish to map to a Delivery Run.
- If you wish to have multiple zone combinations mapped to a single Delivery Run select the plus icon next to your first zone combination. There is no limit to the number of zone combinations you can associate with a Delivery Run.

**3. Map the Transport Lane to a Delivery Run**

Once the **F****rom** and **To** zones have been selected you then need to map the Transport Lane to a Delivery Run using the Delivery Run Mapping tool.

With this tool, you will be able to specify different conditions to determine which consignments will be allocated to which Delivery Runs. It is important to configure the correct conditions as when a consignment is created and it matches the conditions you have specified, CartonCloud will assign it to that mapped Delivery Run.

To map a Transport Lane to a Delivery Run follow the below steps:

- The first Delivery Run Mapping will be set to the default condition of 'Always'. This is the simplest form of mapping and means that the consignment matching the specified zones will always be assigned to the mapped Delivery Run.

![setting-up-transport-lanes-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-transport-lanes-1.png?width=670&height=294&name=setting-up-transport-lanes-1.png)

- To change the condition variable and create more specific Delivery Run Mappings select the blue plus icon in the middle of the window.
- Select a condition variable from the drop-down menu. Choose the one that is most appropriate for the condition you are creating.
- Select the logical operator that should be applied. For example, equal to or greater than. The type of logical operators you have to choose from will depend on what condition variable you selected in the previous field.
- Next, select the second condition variable to complete the condition equation.
- Then, select the Delivery Run that you wish to apply to the condition. When a consignment meets this condition CartonCloud will allocate it to this Delivery Run.

**![setting-up-transport-lanes-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-transport-lanes-2.png?width=670&height=262&name=setting-up-transport-lanes-2.png)
Multiple conditions within the one Delivery Run Mapping**

You can have multiple conditions within the one Delivery Run mapping.

To add an additional condition:

- Select the plus icon next to the current condition.
- You will be prompted to select either **And**or **Or.**
  - **And** will inform CartonCloud that both conditions must be met before a consignment is allocated to the specified Delivery Run.
  - **Or** will tell CartonCloud that either condition can be met for the consignment to be assigned to the specified Delivery Run.

**Multiple Delivery Run Mappings within a single Transport Lane**

You can have multiple Delivery Run Mappings within the one Transport Lane.

To add an additional Delivery Run Mapping:

- Select **Add Delivery Run**at the bottom of the screen.

CartonCloud will attempt to match each Delivery Run Mapping by starting from the top of the page, then proceeding to the bottom.

Once a matching condition is found, the Consignment will be assigned to that Delivery Run and no further mappings below that condition will be checked.

![setting-up-transport-lanes-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-transport-lanes-3.png?width=670&height=330&name=setting-up-transport-lanes-3.png)

To order the Delivery Run Mappings, simply grab the four-dot square icon in the Delivery Run Mapping window you wish to move and slide it into the desired order.

![setting-up-transport-lanes-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-transport-lanes-4.png?width=670&height=328&name=setting-up-transport-lanes-4.png)
It is important that your last Delivery Run Mapping (below all other Delivery Run Mappings) on your Transport Lane has the configuration of 'Always'. This Delivery Run Mapping will act as a fall-back if a consignment does not meet the previous Delivery Run Mapping requirements. Without this fall-back, consignments can be left without a Delivery Run allocation as they do not meet any of the defined requirements.

### ​
​​​​​Using the Transport Lanes Page

To navigate to the Transport Lanes page, type 'Transport Lanes' into the [Search for anything](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/GoCLAQ) bar at the top of the CaronCloud application.

The below screen will appear. From here, you can add new Transport Lanes and sort and filter existing lanes.

For information on how to use the advanced sort and filter functions please read the [Advanced sorting and filtering](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/LIbcI) article.

![setting-up-transport-lanes-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-transport-lanes-5.png?width=670&height=327&name=setting-up-transport-lanes-5.png)

### Example Delivery Run Mappings

#### **Example 1 - Consignment Type**

![setting-up-transport-lanes-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-transport-lanes-6.png?width=670&height=227&name=setting-up-transport-lanes-6.png)

In this Delivery Run Mapping, if a consignment is of the type 'Return' and traveling from the GC Hinterland then it will automatically be allocated to the 'Returns' Delivery Run.

If this requirement is not met then any other consignment traveling from the GC Hinterland will be assigned to the 'Hinterland Daily' Delivery Run.

**Example 2 - Weight Based**

![setting-up-transport-lanes-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-transport-lanes-7.png?width=670&height=168&name=setting-up-transport-lanes-7.png)

In this Delivery Run mapping, if a consignment is traveling within the GC Metro area, and the consignment weight is 1kg or less, then the consignment will be allocated to the 'CBD Motorbike' Delivery Run.

For all other consignments traveling within the GC Metro area that are not less than 1kg in weight, they will be assigned to the 'GC Metro' Delivery Run.

**Example 3 - Service Type**

![setting-up-transport-lanes-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-transport-lanes-8.png?width=670&height=229&name=setting-up-transport-lanes-8.png)

In this Delivery Run Mapping, if a consignment is traveling from Brisbane Metro to the Northern Gold Coast, and has a service type of 'Express', then it will be allocated to the 'North Coast Priority' Delivery Run.

For all other service types, the consignment will be allocated to the 'North Coast Daily' Delivery Run.

**Example 4 - Pallet quantity**

![setting-up-transport-lanes-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-transport-lanes-9.png?width=670&height=284&name=setting-up-transport-lanes-9.png)

In this Delivery Run Mapping, if a consignment is traveling from Brisbane Metro to the Northern Gold Coast, and it contains more than 14 pallets, then it will be allocated to the 'Direct Semitrailer' Delivery Run.

For all other pallet quantities (14 or less), the consignment will be allocated to the 'North Coast Daily' Delivery Run.

The below video explains what a Transport Lane is and provides examples of the different ways in which you can configure your Transport Lanes.

**When Delivery Run Mapping is overridden**

Before CartonCloud utilises the Delivery Run mapping logic defined in the Transport Lane it will check that there are no other Delivery Run mapping configurations defined elsewhere in CartonCloud that should take precedence over the Transport Lane. The below diagram highlights the other ways in which a consignment can be mapped to a Delivery Run and the order in which CartonCloud prioritises them. As you can see, Transport Lanes will only be used once all other mapping configurations have been checked.

For more details on how CartonCloud prioritises information when assigning a consignment to a Delivery Run please see the article: [How a Consignment determines its Delivery Run](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-a-consignment-determines-its-delivery-run)

![setting-up-transport-lanes-10](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-transport-lanes-10.png?width=365&height=387&name=setting-up-transport-lanes-10.png)

**Duplicate Transport Lanes**

The system will not allow duplicate Transport Lanes containing the same From zone and To zone combinations to be active at the same time.

While it is possible to create two Transport Lanes containing a delivery run Mapping from 'Brisbane' to 'Gold Coast', only one of those transport lanes can be made active at a time.

---

<a id="transport-lanes"></a>
## Transport Lanes

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/transport-lanes_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Application of a transport lane
- How CartonCloud automatically assigns the consignments to a delivery run
- ABC transport consignment example

### Purpose

Please note that if your CartonCloud account was created prior to 1 July 2019 the below functionality may not be available at this stage. If you would like to discuss migrating to the newer version of the CartonCloud TMS, please  use [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com) and lodge a case with our Service Desk.

Transport Lanes contain the logic and rules that dictate what Delivery Run a consignment is assigned to. Defining this logic in the Transport Lane enables CartonCloud to automatically assign consignments to the appropriate Delivery Run. The logic is defined using both your  [Transport Zone Set](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/wILcI) (the defined geographical zones your operation delivers to) and your  [Delivery Runs](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Delivery+Runs) (how you operationally group your consignments for allocating activities to drivers and vehicles).

### Application of a transport lane

To understand the application of Transport Lanes we will use an example delivery consignment for ABC Transport travelling from Burleigh Heads to Paradise Point. ABC Transport has created a Transport Lane that specifies that any delivery consignment moving from the GC Metro zone must be assigned to the 'Metro Daily' Delivery Run.

Using the logic defined in the Transport Lane, CartonCloud will match the consignments to and from zone to the corresponding Delivery Run.

### How CartonCloud automatically assigns the Consignments to a Delivery Run

### ![transport-lanes-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/transport-lanes-0.png?width=369&height=419&name=transport-lanes-0.png)
ABC Transport Consignment Example  ![transport-lanes-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/transport-lanes-1.png?width=670&height=508&name=transport-lanes-1.png)

To set up your Transport Lanes, please see [Setting up Transport Lanes](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-transport-lanes)

---

# Transport Management > Zone Sets

<a id="assigning-location-entries-to-zones-transport-zone-set"></a>
## Assigning Location Entries to zones - Transport/Income Zone Set

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/assigning-location-entries-to-zones-transport-zone-set_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Example
- How To Steps
- Filtering and sorting zones

### Purpose

Please note that if your CartonCloud account was created prior to 1 July 2019 the below functionality may not be available at this stage. If you would like to discuss migrating to the newer version of the CartonCloud TMS, please use [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket) and lodge a case with our Service Desk.

Once all zones and location entries have been created you can then begin to associate location entries with their appropriate zone. By associating location entries with zones, you are defining in CartonCloud which postcodes/suburbs fall within each of the geographic zones your operations services for either income or allocation purposes.

Please note, location entries should be associated with the most specific child zone they belong to.

Before assigning locations to zones, it is important to first understand how to use the filter and sort functionality. This functionality simplifies the assign locations to zones process. Please read [filtering and sorting zones](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/advanced-sorting-and-filtering) in this article before beginning to assign locations to zones.

### Example

For the ABC Transport example using the Transport Lane Zone Sets, **Burleigh Heads**would be associated with the **GC Metro** zone and **Paradise Point**would be assigned to the **GC North** zone.

### ![assigning-location-entries-to-zones-transport-zone-set-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/assigning-location-entries-to-zones-transport-zone-set-0.png?width=670&height=503&name=assigning-location-entries-to-zones-transport-zone-set-0.png)

### How To Steps

**1.  Assign a location to a zone**

To assign a location to a zone you can either (a) assign a single entry, (b) assign multiple entries in bulk, or(c) assign multiple entries to multiple zones through the export/import function.

**(a) Assigning a single entry**

- To assign a single entry, select the checkbox next to the entry so it is ticked.
- Select Assign 1 Entry to a Zone.

![assigning-location-entries-to-zones-transport-zone-set-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/assigning-location-entries-to-zones-transport-zone-set-1.png?width=670&height=185&name=assigning-location-entries-to-zones-transport-zone-set-1.png)

- A new window will appear, from here select the zone from the dropdown menu that you wish to assign the location to.
- Click, Assign.

**(b) Assigning multiple entries in bulk**

When you need to assign a large number of entries to a zone it is best to do so in bulk. Before completing the below steps, please read the [advanced sorting and filtering article](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/advanced-sorting-and-filtering)(you need to use the filter function to complete the below steps).

To assign multiple entries in bulk;

- Apply filters to your location entries so that only the location that you wish to assign appears.
- Click the checkbox to the left of State to select all entries.
- This will select all location entry records on the current page. To select all entries within the filter parameters, select the text which appears as displayed on the next step.
- To assign all entries that you have selected to a zone, select Assign x Entries to a Zone

**c) Assigning multiple entries to multiple zones in bulk**

If you wish to assign a large number of entries to multiple zones it is best to do so through the export/import function.

To assign location entries through the export/import function:

- To export location entries, select the 3 vertical dot icon in the top right corner of the location entries window, then Export xlsx.
- The red bell at the top right of the page will then notify you when the export file is ready.
- Select the bell icon then Download here.
- Open the file in Excel or your chosen spreadsheet editing software.
- To assign location entries to zones simply fill in the zone column for the applicable location entries (ensure you are using a zone that has already been created in CartonCloud otherwise, the reimport will fail).
- When updating location entries do not change the id column.
- Once the file is saved and ready to be imported, select the 3 vertical dot icon, then Import and select the file.
- You will be notified once it is complete through the red bell at the top right of the page.
- Review the import results to check if all location entries were assigned successfully, or review any errors that may have occurred.

### Filtering and sorting zones

Within the location entry window, you have the ability to use the advanced sort and filter function. For information on how to utilise these functions, please find the [advanced sorting and filtering article](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/LIbcI).

Deleting a location entry

To delete a single Location Entry *(you can also follow these steps if you need to delete more than one)*:

- Select the Location Entry you would like to delete by clicking the tick box on the left-hand side.
- Select Delete 1 Entry .

To delete multiple Location Entries at once:

- Select the filter icon in the top right corner.
- Filter for the locations that you wish to delete (refer to the above filter instructions for more details).
- Select the tick box on the top line.
- Select Delete 5 Entries .

Next Step - [Setting up Transport Lanes](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/transport-lanes)

---

<a id="associating-the-rate-card-with-the-appropriate-income-zone-set"></a>
## Associating the Rate Card with the appropriate Income Zone Set

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/associating-the-rate-card-with-the-appropriate-income-zone-set_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to associate the Rate Card with the Income Zone Set
- How to change the Income Zone Set associated with the Rate Card

### Purpose

Please note that if your CartonCloud account was created prior to 1 July 2019 the below functionality may not be available at this stage. If you would like to discuss migrating to the newer version of the CartonCloud TMS, please use [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com) and lodge a case with our Service Desk.

Once the Income Zone Set has been created, you will then need to associate it with the applicable [Rate Card](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/rate-cards-overview). By associating the Zone Set with a Rate Card, CartonCloud will know what rates to apply when automatically calculating consignment charges.

You will not be able to create Transport Rates until you have associated the Rate Card with the appropriate Income Zone Set.

Note, once you have associated a Zone Set with a Rate Card you can not change the Zone Set unless there are no Transport Rates associated with the Rate Card. See How to change the Zone Set associated with the Rate Card for more information.

### How to associate the Rate Card with the Income Zone Set

- Within the Rate Card page (use the 'Search for anything' bar at the top of the application to navigate to the Rate Card page), select the Rate Card you would like to associate an Income Zone Set to.
- Click the Transport Rates tab within the Rate Card.
- You will then be prompted to select the appropriate Income Zone Set from the drop-down menu.
- Click Save.

![associating-the-rate-card-with-the-appropriate-income-zone-set-0-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/associating-the-rate-card-with-the-appropriate-income-zone-set-0-1.png?width=670&height=299&name=associating-the-rate-card-with-the-appropriate-income-zone-set-0-1.png)

You can use different Income Zone Sets for each Rate Card, meaning you can use different Income Zone Sets for different customers. You can also use the same Income Zone Set for each Rate Card.

### How to change the Income Zone Set associated with the Rate Card

To change the Zone Set associated with the Rate Card there must be no Transport Rates associated with the Rate Card.

**To change the Zone Set associated with the Rate Card:**

- Navigate to the Rate Card you wish to change the Zone Set for.
- Select the Transport Rates tab.
- If there are Transport Rates associated with the Rate Card :
  - The Zone Set bar will be blocked out and you will not be able to edit it.

![associating-the-rate-card-with-the-appropriate-income-zone-set-1-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/associating-the-rate-card-with-the-appropriate-income-zone-set-1-1.png?width=670&height=176&name=associating-the-rate-card-with-the-appropriate-income-zone-set-1-1.png)

- To be able to edit the Zone Set bar, all Transport Rates associated with that Rate Card will need to be deleted.
- To delete the Transport Rates, select the heading tick box in the left corner.

![associating-the-rate-card-with-the-appropriate-income-zone-set-2-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/associating-the-rate-card-with-the-appropriate-income-zone-set-2-1.png?width=670&height=176&name=associating-the-rate-card-with-the-appropriate-income-zone-set-2-1.png)

-
  - Select Delete Entries .
  - You will now be able to edit the Zone Set bar and select the relevant Zone Set from the drop-down menu.
- If there are no Transport Rates associated with the Rate Card:
  - The Zone Set will not be blocked and you will be able to select the relevant Zone Set from the drop-down menu.

![associating-the-rate-card-with-the-appropriate-income-zone-set-3-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/associating-the-rate-card-with-the-appropriate-income-zone-set-3-1.png?width=670&height=176&name=associating-the-rate-card-with-the-appropriate-income-zone-set-3-1.png)

- Select the relevant Zone Set from the drop-down menu and select Save .

![associating-the-rate-card-with-the-appropriate-income-zone-set-4-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/associating-the-rate-card-with-the-appropriate-income-zone-set-4-1.png?width=670&height=176&name=associating-the-rate-card-with-the-appropriate-income-zone-set-4-1.png)

  Next Step: [Setting up Transport Rates](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/creating-transport-rates)

---

<a id="creating-a-transport-zone-set-and-zones"></a>
## Creating a Transport/Income Zone Set and zones

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/creating-a-transport-zone-set-and-zones_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to create a Zone Set

### Purpose

How to create a Zone Set and applicable Zones within the Zone Set.

### How to create a Zone Set

**1. Create a Zone Set**

- Navigate to the Zone Sets page by typing in Zone Sets into the Search for anything bar.
- Once on the Zone Sets page, Select **+Add Zone Set** in the top left corner.
- You will then need to fill in the Name and Type fields, as seen in the below example.

![creating-a-transport-zone-set-and-zones-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-transport-zone-set-and-zones-0.png?width=367&height=269&name=creating-a-transport-zone-set-and-zones-0.png)

- If you are going to be using the Zone Set immediately, select the toggle (in the top right corner) to make it active.
- If you are creating a Zone Set Cascade, see the [Zone Set Cascade](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Creating+a+Transport+Zone+Set+and+zones#CreatingaTransportZoneSetandzones-cascades) section of this article. Otherwise, leave this option blank.

Once you have created your Zone Set you will be directed to the Zone Set configuration page. You will see the Zone Hierarchy panel on the left-hand side (image below), this is where you will create your zones and define the hierarchy of those zones.

The purpose of defining a zone hierarchy is that it informs CartonCloud which zones are contained within each other. For example, in the image below a zone has been created for the Gold Coast area. Within this parent zone, five child zones have been created to define the areas within the Gold Coast.

**Zone Hierarchy Panel**![creating-a-transport-zone-set-and-zones-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-transport-zone-set-and-zones-1.png?width=312&height=351&name=creating-a-transport-zone-set-and-zones-1.png)

| **Button** | **Function** |
| --- | --- |
| Three dot icon | Show or hide Inactive zones - this is useful if you have a lot of inactive zones and only wish to see the active ones.    Import and export zones - if you have a large number of zones to create, it is best to do so in bulk using the export/import function. See [Creating zones in bulk - using the export/import function](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Creating+a+Transport+Zone+Set+and+zones#CreatingaTransportZoneSetandzones-export).    To select, expand or collapse all zones in one action. |
| Search Zones | Search bar to find the zone you are looking for. |
| + Add Zone | To add a new zone. |
| Blue plus icon | To add a child zone to the select zone. |
| Red square icon | To deactivate a zone when they are no longer in use. You can not delete a zone entirely (as it may be associated with historical data), therefore, you must deactivate the zone if you no longer wish to use it. |
| Green edit icon | To edit the zone. From here you can reactivate/deactivate a zone and change the zone name. |

**2. Add Zones**

To add a new zone, you can either (a) add a single zone or (b) create zones in bulk using the export/import function.

**(a) Adding a single-zone**

- Use the Zone Hierarchy panel and click **+ Add Zones.**
- The Zone Hierarchy panel allows you to define a zone hierarchy with parent zones and child zones. Child zones are contained within a parent zone.
- Name the zone and if it falls within the geographic boundaries of another zone, for example, Gold Coast, set that zone as its parent.

![creating-a-transport-zone-set-and-zones-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-transport-zone-set-and-zones-2.png?width=347&height=269&name=creating-a-transport-zone-set-and-zones-2.png)

Once you have created all relevant zones your Zone Hierarchy should resemble something similar to the Zone Set Hierarchy below:

![creating-a-transport-zone-set-and-zones-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-a-transport-zone-set-and-zones-3.png?width=425&height=383&name=creating-a-transport-zone-set-and-zones-3.png)
**(b) Creating zones in bulk - using the export/import function**

If you have numerous zones to create, you can save time by creating the zones in bulk by using the export/import function. This function enables you to export zones to an XLS sheet, add new zones within the sheet, then import them back into CartonCloud.

Follow the below steps to add new zones through the export/import function:

- Select the 3 vertical dot icon in the top right of the Zone Hierarchy panel and select **Export xlsx.**
- The red bell at the top right of the page will notify you when the export file is ready.
- Select the bell icon then **Download here.**
- Open the file in Excel or your chosen spreadsheet editing software.
- To add new zones fill in the name, parent (if you have an applicable parent zone to associate it with), and status column (type in either active or inactive).
- Do not change the id column when updating or creating new zones.
- Children zones cannot be associated with a parent zone that has not already been created in CartonCloud. Therefore, ensure you have created the applicable parent zone within CartonCloud before exporting.
- Once the file is saved and ready to be imported, select the 3 vertical dot icon, then **Import**and select the file.
- You will be notified of completion through the red bell at the top right of the page.
- Review the import results to check if all zones were created/updated successfully, or review any errors that may have occurred.

**Zone Set Cascades**

Cascading Zone sets allow you to chain multiple Zone Sets together so that if a consignment fails to find a Zone on the first Zone Set, it will then check the Cascade Zone Set.

This functionality is currently only possible with Income Zone sets (as you can only have a single Transport Zone Set).

Next Step -[Creating Location Entries](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set)

---

<a id="creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set"></a>
## Creating Location Entries - Transport/Income Zone Set

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to steps

### Purpose

Please note that if your CartonCloud account was created prior to 1 July 2019 the below functionality may not be available at this stage. If you would like to discuss migrating to the newer version of the CartonCloud TMS, please use [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com) and lodge a case with our Service Desk,

Once you have added your zones to the Zone Set, you will then need to create location entries.

A location entry is a suburb and postcode combination that will be used to find a match against addresses on consignments. These location entries will then be associated with the relevant zone.

### How to steps

**1. Select the location entry type**

Once you have created your zones in the Zone Hierarchy panel you will then need to use the window to the right of the panel to create your location entries. As you do not have any location entries yet, the window will appear as below.

![creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set-0.png?width=670&height=328&name=creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set-0.png)

- Select, **Add the first one to get started.**
- You will have three types of location entries to choose from. Select the location entry type you would like to start using (use the below table to help you select the most suitable location entry type).

| **Location Entry Type** | **Definition** |
| --- | --- |
| Australian Locations | Used to associate Australian locations with a Zone. These entries must contain a postcode of 4 digits in length. |
| Addresses to Zones | Used to associate a specific address with a Zone. This is useful if you wish to create a Transport Rate (using the Income Zone) and/or Transport Lane (using the Transport Zone) related to that particular address. |
| Global Locations | Used to associate suburbs/postcodes outside of Australia with a Zone. Global location entries can contain postcodes of any length.  Global Location entries can include just the Country and do not require a state, city, suburb or postocde. This allows you to add a country as a location without having to manually add each individual state/province. ![creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set-1.png?width=670&height=345&name=creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set-1.png) |

- You can have multiple location entry types for the one Zone Set. Each additional location entry type will appear as a tab at the top of the window.

**2. Add a new location entry**

Upon selecting the location entry type a new tab will appear with the location entry type as the header.

To add a new location entry, you can either **(a) add a single entry** or **(b) create multiple entries with the export/import function.**

When creating your location entries you have the option to associate a zone to the entry. If you already know what zones will be associated with the location entries it is recommended you associate the zones in this step. If not, you can complete this in the next step - Assigning location entries to a zone.

**(a) Add a single entry**

- Select + Add Entry.

![creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set-2.png?width=670&height=147&name=creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set-2.png)

Complete the required fields, as seen in the below example, and select save.

![creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set-3.png?width=433&height=275&name=creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set-3.png)

**(b) Add multiple entries with the export/import function**

When adding a large number of location entries it is suggested you use the export/import function. This is especially useful when you already have the location entries you use stored in a spreadsheet format.

If you do not have your locations saved in a spreadsheet format you can use the below **Australian Locations** file. This file contains all postcodes and suburbs in Australia. When using this file be sure to remove the locations that are not applicable to your operation before importing them into CartonCloud.

[Australian Postcodes file](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hubfs/Knowledge%20Base%20Files/18500%20postcodes%20on%20Zoneset%20template%2030-09-2025.xlsx)

- **If you already have location entries in CartonCloud and need to edit/add more location entries follow the below export/import process:**
  - To export location entries, select the 3 vertical dot icon, then **Export xlsx.**
  - The red bell at the top right of the page will then notify you when the export file is ready.
  - Select the bell icon then **Download here.**
  - Open the file in Excel or your chosen spreadsheet editing software.
  - To add new location entries, add the state, postcode, suburb, and zone (if you wish to associate the zone in this step)
  - When updating or creating new location entries do not change the id column.
  - Once the file is saved and ready to be imported, select the 3 vertical dot icon, then **Import**and select the file.
  - You will be notified once it is complete through the red bell at the top right of the page.
  - Review the import results to check if all location entries were created/updated successfully, or review any errors that may have occurred.

- **If you have no location entries and wish to add entries through the import function:**
- To import location entries, select the 3 vertical dot icon, then Import.
- If using the Australian Locations template (ensure you have deleted the irrelevant entries) then select this file, if using your own file make sure the excel file matches the below heading format and keep the id column blank.

![creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set-4.png?width=412&height=50&name=creating-location-entries-transport-zone-set-4.png)

- You will be notified once it is complete through the red bell at the top right of the page. Please note, if the import is large there may be a slight delay in the import success notification showing in the bell notification.

- Review the import results to check if all location entries were created/updated successfully, or review any errors that may have occurred.

If you have not yet associated the location entries to a zone, please follow the next step -[Assigning Location Entries to zones](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/i4bcI)

If you are using location entries in New Zealand please ensure you have all fields filled in for your location entry including state, postcode and suburb. When CartonCloud is looking for the correct location entry to match to the address on the Consignment, it will use the below list to find the best match. For example if the location entry has a postcode , state and suburb that match to the address it will select that location entry over one that has a city postcode and suburb match.

New Zealand location matches in order of best match:

- city + postcode + state + suburb
- postcode + state + suburb
- city + state + suburb
- city + suburb
- city + postcode
- suburb + postcode

---

## Exporting / Importing Location Entries

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/exporting_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to export / import location entries

### Purpose

The export / import function allows you to create location entries in bulk or make changes to existing entries.

### How to export / import location entries

If you already have location entries in CartonCloud and need to edit/add more location entries follow the below export/import process:

-
  - To export location entries, select the 3 vertical dot icon, then **Export xlsx.**
  - The red bell at the top right of the page will then notify you when the export file is ready.
  - Select the bell icon then **Download here.**
  - Open the file in Excel or your chosen spreadsheet editing software.
  - To add new location entries, add the state, postcode, suburb, and zone (if you wish to associate the zone in this step)
  - When updating or creating new location entries do not change the id column.
  - Once the file is saved and ready to be imported, select the 3 vertical dot icon, then **Import**and select the file.
  - You will be notified once it is complete through the red bell at the top right of the page.
  - Review the import results to check if all location entries were created/updated successfully, or review any errors that may have occurred.

If you have no location entries and wish to add entries through the import function:

-
  - To import location entries, select the 3 vertical dot icon, then Import.
  - If using the Australian Locations template (ensure you have deleted the irrelevant entries) then select this file, if using your own file make sure the excel file matches the below heading format and keep the id column blank.

![exporting-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/exporting-0.png?width=626&height=76&name=exporting-0.png)

-
  - You will be notified once it is complete through the red bell at the top right of the page. Please note, if the import is large there may be a slight delay in the import success notification showing in the bell notification.
  - Review the import results to check if all location entries were created/updated successfully, or review any errors that may have occurred.

<a id="setting-up-income-zone-sets"></a>
## Setting up Income Zone Sets

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-income-zone-sets_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to steps

### Purpose

Please note that if your CartonCloud account was created prior to 1 July 2019 the below functionality may not be available at this stage. If you would like to discuss migrating to the newer version of the CartonCloud TMS, please use [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com) and lodge a case with our Service Desk.

[Income Zone Sets](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Zone+Sets) contain the zones your operation uses for charging. These zones will be used when creating your [Transport Rates](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Rate+Card+-+Transport+Rates) to allow CartonCloud to automatically calculate your consignment charges. If the geographic regions you use for charging vary, see [Using multiple Income Zone Sets](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Zone+Sets).

### How to steps

To set up your Income Zone Sets, complete each of the below steps.

1. Create your Zone Set and zones - create your Zone Set and the applicable zones within each Zone Set.
2. Create location entries - add or import the suburb and postcode combinations for the locations you want to include in each zone.
3. Assign location entries to zones - associate location entries with the applicable zones.

The below video helps to explain what Zone Sets are and how to set them up within your CartonCloud account.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/LYZHi9BuqOk

First Step: [Create your Zone Set and zones](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Creating+an+Income+Zone+Set+and+zones)

---

<a id="setting-up-transport-zone-sets"></a>
## Setting up Transport Zone Sets

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-transport-zone-sets_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Creating Transport Zone Sets
- Checking Transport Zones on a Consignment

### Purpose

Please note that if your CartonCloud account was created prior to 1 July 2019 the below functionality may not be available at this stage. If you would like to discuss migrating to the newer version of the CartonCloud TMS, please please use [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com) and lodge a case with our Service Desk.

[Transport Zone Sets](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/get-started-with-transport-zone-sets) are the zones your operation uses for allocating consignments. These zones will work in conjunction with [Delivery Runs](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/delivery-runs) and [Transport Lanes](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/transport-lanes) to enable CartonCloud to automatically assign consignments to the appropriate Delivery Run. Only one Transport Zone Set can be created.

### Creating Transport Zone Sets

To create your Transport Zone Set follow the below steps:

1. [Create your Zone Set and zones](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Creating-a-Transport-Zone-Set-and-zones) - create your Zone Set and the applicable zones within each Zone Set
2. [Create location entries](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Assigning-Location-Entries-to-zones-Transport-Zone-Set) - add or import the suburb and postcode combinations for the locations you service
3. [Assign location entries to zones](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Assigning-Location-Entries-to-zones-Transport-Zone-Set)- associate location entries with the applicable zones

The below video helps to explain what Zone Sets are and how to set them up within your CartonCloud account.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/LYZHi9BuqOk

### Checking Transport Zones on a Consignment

Once you have set up your Transport Zones you can check which Transport Zones are applied to a Consignment from within the Consignment itself.

- Navigate to the relevant Consignment, Transport > Consignment and select the relevant Consignment.
- Scroll down to Specifics.

**![setting-up-transport-zone-sets-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-transport-zone-sets-0.png?width=670&height=332&name=setting-up-transport-zone-sets-0.png)**

- Scroll down to Transport Zones to see which Transport Zones have been applied to the Consignment.

![setting-up-transport-zone-sets-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/setting-up-transport-zone-sets-1.png?width=670&height=307&name=setting-up-transport-zone-sets-1.png)

<a id="zone-set-matching-criteria"></a>
## Zone Set Matching Criteria

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/zone-set-matching-criteria_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Zone Set Matching Criteria

### Purpose

[Zone Sets](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Zone-Sets) are the defined geographical areas your operation uses for allocating deliveries and determining delivery rates. Zone Sets provide the framework and logic for CartonCloud to automatically assign consignments to Delivery Runs and calculate consignment charges. For Zone Sets to work, [Delivery Runs](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Delivery-Runs), [Transport Lanes](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Transport-Lanes), and [Transport Rates](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Creating-Transport-Rates) must be set up correctly for each to work together to provide this core functionality. In addition, for the Consignment to find a matching Zone Set there is a certain criteria utilised to find the best matching zone for that consignment. This zone will then determine the allocation and rating of the consignment.

### Zone Set Matching Criteria

For a consignment to find a matching zone the below criteria is utilised. Depending on the location of the address on the consignment will determine what criteria is utilised. For example, if the address is an address in Australia the consignment must have a suburb, postcode and state to find a matching zone. However, on the other hand, if the address is in a country other than Australia and New Zealand the address only needs at a minimum suburb or postcode to find a matching zone.

CartonCloud will work down the criteria list until it finds a match, it will look for a full match and then work down the criteria list if none found. Therefore, to ensure the consignments are matched to the correct zones it is recommended the full address is provided.

**Australia**

- suburb + postcode + state

**Global Locations**

- city + postcode + state + suburb
- postcode + state + suburb
- city + state + suburb
- city + postcode + suburb
- city + postcode
- suburb + postcode
- suburb
- postcode
- country

**Global Locations (New Zealand)**

- city + postcode + state + suburb
- postcode + state + suburb
- city + state + suburb
- city + postcode + suburb
- city + suburb
- city + postcode
- suburb + postcode

---

<a id="zone-sets"></a>
## Zone Sets

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/zone-sets_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Zone set types
- Application of zone sets
- Using multiple income zone sets
- Creating your transport zone set and income zone sets

### Purpose

Please note that if your CartonCloud account was created prior to 1 July 2019 the below functionality may not be available at this stage. If you would like to discuss migrating to the newer version of the CartonCloud TMS, please use [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket) and lodge a case with the Service Desk.

Zone Sets are the defined geographical areas your operation uses for allocating deliveries and determining delivery rates. Zone Sets provide the framework and logic for CartonCloud to automatically assign consignments to Delivery Runs and calculate consignment charges. For Zone Sets to work, [Delivery Runs](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/delivery-runs), [Transport Lanes](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/transport-lanes), and [Transport Rates](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Rate+Card+-+Transport+Rates) must also be created as the different logic for each work together to provide this core functionality.

To move straight to setting up your Zone Sets, see [Creating your Transport Zone Set and Income Zone Sets](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Zone+Sets#ZoneSets-creating).

### Zone set types

**Income Zone Sets:**Income Zone Sets contain the zones your operation uses for charging. These zones will be used when creating your Transport Rates to allow CartonCloud to automatically calculate your consignment charges. If the geographic regions you use for charging vary, see [Using multiple Income Zone Sets](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Zone+Sets#ZoneSets-multiple).

**Transport Zone Sets:**Transport Zone Sets are the zones your operation uses for allocating consignments. These zones will work in conjunction with Delivery Runs and Transport Lanes to enable CartonCloud to automatically assign consignments to the appropriate Delivery Run. Only one Transport Zone Set can be created.

Each Zone Set is made up of multiple zones and each individual zone is made of single or multiple suburbs and postcodes. When creating zones, you can associate as many or as few suburbs and postcodes with the one zone. This means you can create a zone for a state, city, an area within a city, or even a specific suburb.

### Application of zone sets

To understand the application of Zone Sets we will use a hypothetical transport company, ABC Transport, that operates in the Gold Coast area.

The below map shows how ABC Transport has divided the Gold Coast into different zones for both its delivery allocation (Transport Zone Set) and rate calculation (Income Zone Set).

![Zone Set_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Zone%20Set_1.jpeg?width=670&height=483&name=Zone%20Set_1.jpeg)
If ABC Transport has a consignment moving from **Burleigh Heads** to **Paradise Point**, CartonCloud will find the Income and Transport Zone associated with the suburbs Burleigh Heads and Paradise Point.

CartonCloud will then use the Income Zone pairing to find the associated Transport Rates and likewise use the Transport Zone pairing to find the matching Delivery Run.

**Consignment 1:**

- From address: CartonCloud, 5/27 Dover Drive, Burleigh Heads 4220
- To address: FoodWorks Paradise Point, Shop 1/3 Grice Avenue, Paradise Point 4216
- Income Zones: Area 2 → Area 1
- Transport Zones: GC Metro → GC North
- Delivery Run: Metro Daily

![Zone Set_2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Zone%20Set_2.jpeg?width=670&height=488&name=Zone%20Set_2.jpeg)

### Using multiple income zone sets

ABC Transport has two Income Zone Sets, a Standard Income Zone Set and a Radius Income Zone Set. This allows ABC Transport to use different geographic definitions for calculating consignment charges for different customers.

For example, ABC Transport has two consignments for two different customers (Customer A and B) both moving from the same address in Robina to the same address in Helensvale. Customer A's Rate Card is associated with the Standard Income Zone Set and Customer B's Rate Card is associated with the Radius Income Zone Set (which is based on the distance from their depot).

Customer A's consignment will be traveling from Area 2 to Area 1 whereas Customer B's consignment will be traveling from Zone 1 to Zone 3. Even though both consignments have the same to and from address, the rates can be configured differently in accordance with the different Income Zone Sets.

![Zone Set_3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Zone%20Set_3.jpeg?width=670&height=510&name=Zone%20Set_3.jpeg)

### Creating your Transport Zone Set and Income Zone Sets

Transport Zone Sets and Income Zone Sets are separate and unrelated, meaning the geographical zones you define for one type of Zone Set can also be used for the other. This also means there is no particular order that you need to create the two different Zone Sets in.

To set up Transport Zone Sets please see - [Setting up CartonCloud to automatically allocate consignments](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-cartoncloud-to-automatically-allocate-consignments)

To set up Income Zone Sets please see - [Setting up CartonCloud to automatically rate consignments](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-cartoncloud-to-automatically-rate-consignments)

---
